tataH kimityata Aha- tattveti ||
na kevalaM jalpavitaNDayoreva nigrahasthAnasadbhAvaH kintu vAde.api | nigR^ihyate.aneneti nigraho nigrahasthAnaM syAdeva | ayaM tu visheShaH | na jalpavitaNDayoriva samastam.h | api tu yAvattattvanirNayavirodhi tAvadeva | siddhaprashnAdikaM cha tattvanirNayavirodhItyuktam.h, tatkuto vAde na nigrahasthAnamiti | yo hi yadarthaM pravartate sa tadviruddhamAcharankathaM nAparAdhI syAditi hishabdArthaH | nigrahanimittaniShkarShArthaM vailomyamiti bhAvapratyayaH |

nadIpUradarshanenottaradeshe vR^iShyayanumAnaM, pratyagrasharAvachakrabhramadarshanena kulAlAsattyanumAnaM chAshaN^kaya kenachiduktaM nottaradesho.atra pakShaH kinnAma nadI | taddhamareNaiva pUreNa, taddharmasya vR^iShyimaduttaradeshasambandhasya sAdhyatvam.h | evaM sharAvachakradharmAbhyAM pratyagratvabhramAbhyAM taddharmasyaiva kulAlAsatteranumAnamiti | ata idamudAharaNAntaramuditam.h | nahi ta(theho)treveha rohiNyAH kR^ittikAyA vA dvau dharmau sampAdayituM shakyau |
nanvihApi kAlaM pakShIkR^itya prayoktavyam.h | vimataH kAlo rohiNyudayAsattimAnkR^ittikodayavatkAlatvAdatItakAlavaditi | (maivam.h) evaM sati deshaM kAlaM vA.a.adAya sAmAnAdhikaraNyasya sarvatra sattvAdvayadhikaraNAsiddha eva na syAditi vyarthaM tatparisaN^khayAnam.h | evamaprayoge vyadhikaraNatvaM sAvakAshamiti chenna | tathA satyasiddheruktidoShatvAbhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | nachoktidoShatvamapi | vyadhikaraNatayokterapi sAdhyasiddhayaN^gatvAnubhavAt.h | evameva hi laukikAnAmuktayaH | parIkShakA api hi "tatprAmANyamapAtaprAmANyAt.h' ityAdi prayujyate | tadidamuktam.h iti vyadhikaraNatayA ukte.apyetadvAkyaM, sAdhanaM sAdhyasidhyaN^gaM no kiM bhavatyeveti |
kiJNcha kAlAdikamAdAya prayogavipariNAmaH kArya ityatra (kiM) naiyAyikAdisamayo niyAmakaH, kiMvA(tra)pramANamasti | AdyaM dUShayati- na hIti ||
atra upapatti(siddhe.arthe) sAdhye.arthe | Aj~naiva samayamAtram.h | tathA sati sarvaM vAN^mAtreNaivopadeShyavyam.h | na punaH kvApi pramANaM vAchyam.h | viparItAj~nayA satpratipakShatA cha syAditi hi shabdArthaH | Aj~nA khalu pramANAtparaviShaye dharmAdau bhavati | sA chAvagatAptabhAvAnAm.h | nApi dvitIyaH | tadanupalambhAt.h | 
syAdetat.h | vyAptistAvadanumAnAN^gam.h | sambandhavisheShashcha vyAptiH | nacha vyAshrayayoH sambandho yujyate | ato vyAshrayatvasya doShatvAtsambha(tavi)te viShaye vipariNAma iti | maivam.h | avinAbhAvamAtrasya vyAptitvAt.h | avinAbhAvashcha kvachidekAshrayatAmantarbhAvya bhavati | yathA kR^itakatvasyAnityatvena | ata evAnyagatena tena nAnyatrAnityatAsiddhiH | kvachidvibhinnAshrayayoreva | yathA dhUmasyAgninA | dhUmAgnI khalu na samavAyavR^ittyA samAnAshrayau | nApi saMyogavR^ittyA | UrdhvAdhodeshasaMyogitvAt.h | (dhUmasyAdhodeshasaMyogasya siddhatvAt.h) | tathA.apyekaparvatasaMyogitA dvayorastIti chenna | tathA satyagnyarthino niyamena pradeshavisheShe pravR^ittyanupapatteH | dhUma eva dhUmatvena mUle.agnimAnsAdhyata iti chet.h | kimeShA laukikI pratItiH | Ahosvitsamayasiddhaye vipariNAmaH kriyate | na prathamaH | laukikA hyUrdhvadeshaM dhUmavantamavalokyAdhodeshaM 
vahnimantamavagachChanti | na dvitIyaH | nirmUlatvAt.h | api cha dehAdInAM tAvatpareNa kShaNikatA svIkriya(.a.asthIya)te | tatra patanakamarNA gurutvAnumAnaM durghaTaM syAt.h | nahi tayoH kAlataH sAmAnAdhikaraNyam.h | kAryakAraNabhAvAt.h | nApi deshataH | vibhinnadravyAshrayatvAt.h | ataH kasyachidvibhinnAshrayeNaivAvinAbhAvaH|
nanu vyadhikaraNasya pakShadharmatA nAstIti chenmA bhUt.h | tanniyamasya nirnibandhanatvAt.h | tathA sati sAdhya(sya)niyatadeshatA kathaM siddhayediti chedvayAptisvabhAvAditi brUmaH | yathA hi | yatkR^itakaM tadanityamiti sAmAnAdhikaraNyamantarbhAvya vyApteH kR^itakatvaM svAshraya evAnityatvaM gamayati | tathA kR^ittikodayo vyadhikaraNayaiva rohiNyudayAsattyA vyApta iti tau tathaiva gamayati | yathA cha sAmAnAdhikaraNye.apyasti pradeshAdiniyamastathA vaiyadhikaraNye.apIti ko doShaH | tasmAdyatredaM tatredamitivadyadedaM tadedamitivat.h yadevaM tadevamitivachcha yadIdaM tarhIdamiti vyAptisambhavAt.h | vyAptyanurodhenaiva hetusiddherAvashyakatayA pakShadharmatAnAvashyakatvAdyuktaM vyadhikaraNasyApi hetutvamiti |
tathA sAdhyavisheShaNasyAprasiddhAvapi | tathAhi | sAdhyavisheShaNashaprasiddheH kuto dUShaNatvAt.h | kiM vishvaM sadasadvilakShaNaM bAdhyatvAdityAderapi prAmANyaprasaN^gAt.h | uta sAdhyavisheShaNAprasiddhau tatsandehAnupapattau pakShatvAnupapatterhetoH pakShadharmatvAnupapattiprasakteH | athavA sAdhyavisheShaNAprasiddhau tena sAdhanasya vyAptipratItyanupapattiprasaN^gAt.h | yadvA pratij~nAvAkyasyApratItapadArthakatvenAbodhakatvApatteH | AdyaM dUShayati- anyaditi ||
sanna bhavatItyukte.asattvamuktaM bhavet.h (syAtsa)sattvapratikSheparUpatvAdasattvasya | punarasanna bhavatItyukte svavachanavyAhatiH | evamasanna bhavatItyuktyA dvau naJNau prakR^itamarthaM sAtishayaM gamayata iti sattvaM labhyate | punaH sanna bhavatItyukte svavyAhatireva | tadevaM vishvaM sadasatoH sakAshAdanyat.h sadasachcha na bhavatItyeShA pratij~nA svavyAhatereva amA(.apramA) sAdhanAN^gaM na bhavati | natu visheShaNasya sadasadvailakShaNyalakShaNasyAprasiddhatvena | kutaH | svavyAhatirhi me mAtA vandhyetyAdau dUShaNatvena sampratipannA | svavachanasvanyAyasvakriyAsvasiddhAntapramANAntarApratihatAyA evokteH sAdhanadUShaNAN^gatvAt.h | nahi svaviShavimUrChitA bhujaN^gI paraM dashati | nacha doShAntarAsaN^kIrNaM sAdhyavisheShaNAsiddherudAharaNaM pashyAmo yena doShatvaM pratImaH | kasyachidasAdhAraNadharmeNa shashaviShANAdimattvasAdhanamapi pramANaM kinna syAditi chenna | tatrApi dR^ishyAnupalambhabAdhasya vidyamAnatvAt.h | atIndriyasaMsagarsAdhane na ko.api doSha iti chenna | IshvarAdisaMsargeNa siddhasAdhanatvAt.h | evamanyatrApi sampratipannAprAmANye doShAntaramanveShaNIyam.h | tadidamuktaM chashabdena | ata eva vyAhaterityupalakShaNam.h | 
dvitIyaM parAchaShye- asiddheti ||
sAdhyAprasiddhayA yatra pakShadharmatvAsiddhiruchyate(hetau) tatra vyAptyAdItarAN^gasAkalyamasti na vA | na chettata evAnumAnaM duShyaM kiM sAdhyavisheShaNAprasiddhayA | yadi vyAptyAdikaM vidyate tadA.asiddhasAdhane ko doShaH | na ko.api | ayamabhisandhiH | hetorhi pakShadharmatvAsiddhistadA syAt.h | yadi dharmI vA hetostaddharmatvaM vA na syAt.h | sandehAbhAvena pakShadharmatvAsiddhistadA syAt.h | yadi dharmI vA hetostaddharmatvaM vA na syAt.h | sandehAbhAvena pakShatvAnupapattyA pakShadharma(tva)tAbhAve tu svArthAnumAnavisheShavilopaH syAt.h | yadA hi yo dhUmavAnasAvagnimAniti gR^ihItavyAptiko girishekhare dhUmaM pashyanvyAptiM smarati | tadotpadyata evAsyAnumitiH | nacha tasyAgnisandeho.asti | yadA chAptavachanAdvinishchitaparvatAgnisambandhaH parvataM pratyAsIdandhUmamavalokayati | tadA.api tasya vinA sandehenAgnyanumitirbhavatyeva | nahi sAmagrI buddhimatI | yena yanmayA kartavyaM tadanyena kR^itamiti paryAlochyodAsIta | nApi Chinne ChidAyA iva parichChinne parichChedAntarotpAdo.ayuktaH(vaktuM na shakyaH) | nApi parArthAnumAne sandehaniyamaH | viparyastasyApi prativAditvopapatteH | ata eva siddhasAdhako.asaN^gata eva nAshrayAsiddha ityuktam.h | 
kiJNcha viditatattvo.api yadA paraparIkShArthaM (dyarthe) tatra pramANaM pR^ichChati | tadA prayuktamanumAnamamAnaM syAt.h | sandehAbhAvAt.h | tasmAtsandigdhasAdhyaH pakSha ityAdyAH prAchAM vAchaH sambhAvanAbhiprAyAH | paramArthatastvanumitiviShaya eva pakShaH | ataH sandehAbhAve pakShatvAnupapattyabhAvAnnAprasiddhasAdhane pakShadharmatvAsiddhirUpo doSha iti |
tR^itIyaM nirAkaroti- vyAptishcheti ||
tatra jIvAchCharIrajAtaM sAtmakaM prANAdimattvAt.h, bhUritarebhyo bhidyate gandhavattvAt.h, IshvaraH sarvaj~naH savarkartR^itvAdityAdau kevalavyatirekiNi sAdhanasamUhe | taiH aprasiddhairapi sAtmakatvAdibhiH sAdhyaiH | vyAptishchAsti | na kevalaM pakShadharmatA | vyatirekeNa sAdhyAbhAvasya sAdhanAbhAvavyAptatvena liN^genAvagamyate cha sA | 
idamuktaM bhavati | sAdhyavisheShaNAprasiddhayA vyAptipratItyabhAvaM prasajjayato vyAptyabhAvaH | tathAhi | kevalavyatirekyanumAnaM pramANaM 
na vA | neti pakShe vakShyAmaH | Adye tasya vyAptisadbhAvo vyAptyavagama(shchAvashyamaN^gI)shchAN^gIkAryaH | anyathA.anumAnatvavyAghAtAt.h | nacha kevalavyatirekiNi sAdhyaM prasiddham.h | pakShe prasiddhau siddhasAdhanatvAt.h | anyatra prasiddhau kevalavyatirekiNi sAdhyaM prasiddham.h | pakShe prasiddhau siddhasAdhanatvAt.h | anyatra prasiddhau kevalavyatirekiNi sAdhyaM prasiddham.h | pakShe prasiddhau siddhasAdhanatvAt.h | anyatra prasiddhau tatra hetorvR^ittau kevalavyatirekitvAnupapatteH | avR^ittAvasAdhAraNyaprasaN^gAt.h | ataH (pra)shithilamUlaH prasaN^gaH vyatirekiNaH kva vyAptiH kena chAvagamyata iti chet.h | pakSha eva vyatirekeNAvagamyata iti brUmaH | pakShAdipravibhAgAtprAgavagatA tatraiva vipratipattyopadarshayitumashakyA vyatirekeNopapAdyata iti | tairiti bahuvachanenAtiprasiddhatAM prasaN^gavyAptibhaN^gasya sUchayati |
na kevalaM kevalavyatirekisAdhanasya sAdhyena vyAptirvyatirekeNa tadavagamashchAsmAbhirevAN^gIkriyate | kintvaprasiddhavisheShaNatvadUShaNatvavAdibhirapi kaishchidityAha- taishcheti || avagamyate abhyupagamyate | yathA.a.ahuH | yadi sAdhyenAsya kvachidapyanvayo nAsti tadA viruddha evAyamityAshaN^kaya nopeyatvamanvayasya vyAsedhAmo.api tUpA(yami)yatvamityAdi | tathA, yathA cha vyatirekabalAdanvayasiddhistathA vaisheShikairapyupapAdanIyam.h | anyathA sAdhyasAdhanayoravyAptau vyatirekiNo gamakatvabhaN^gAdityAdi | tathA chAprasiddhavisheShaNasyApi kevalavyatirekiNo vyAptyupapAdanamaprasiddhavisheShaNatve vyAptyapratItiprasaJNjanaM cha kathaM na vyAhatamiti bhAvaH | 
yaduktaM kevalavyatirekiNo vyAptyavagamAtparairabhyupagamAchcha nAprasiddhavisheShaNatve.api vyAptyavagamAtparairabhyupagamAchcha nAprasiddhavisheShaNatve.api vyAptyanavagatiriti | tadayuktam.h | yataH kevalavyatirekiNyanyaiva gatiH | ye hi sampratipannapramANabhAvAH kevalavyatirekiNasteShu sAmAnyato.anvayavyAptirevAbhidhAtavyA | tathA hi | prANAdimattvena jIvachCharIrasya sAtmakatve sAdhye yadyatkAryavattattatkAraNavadyathA.ahaN^kuravatI bhUmirbIjagarbheti | (ya)tathA gandhavattvena bhuvo.anyabhedasAdhane yadyadasAdhAraNadharmavattattato bhidyate yathA abAdIti | evamIshvarasya sarvakartR^itvena sArvaj~nasAdhane yo yasya kartA sa tasya kAraNaM prayojanaM cha jAnAti | yathA kulAla iti | evaM shabdaH pR^ithivyAdyaShyadravyAtiriktadravyAshritaH pR^ithivyAdivR^ittau bAdhakopapannatve sati guNatvAdityAdau yo yad.hvR^ittau bAdhakopapannatve sati guNaH sa tato.anyadravyavR^ittiryathA gandha ityAdirUpeNa sAmAnyato vyAptirabhidhAtavyA | 
yadvA sAmAnyato visheShaNaprasiddhiM vidhAya kevalavyatirekI prayoktavyaH | yathA j~nAnatAratamyaM kvachidvishrAntaM tAratamyatvAdityanena sAmAnyataH sArvaj~nasiddhau tasyeshvarasambandhaH kevalavyatirekiNA sAdhyate | tathechChAdayaH kvachidAshritA guNatvAdrUpavat.h | yashchechChAdInAmAshrayaH sa evAtmeti sAmAnyenAtmasiddhau tatsambandho jIvachCharIrasya kevalavyatirekiNA sAdhyate | evamanyatrApi yathAsambhavamUhyam.h |
kvachitpakShaikadesha eva visheShaNaprasiddhimAshritya kevalavyatirekI pravartate | yathA pR^ithivI itarebhyo bhidyate pR^ithivItvAnna yadevaM na tadevaM yathA jalAdItyatra ghaTAdAveva visheShaNaprasiddhernAprasiddhavisheShaNatA | nachaivaM sapakShasambhavena kevalavyatirekitvabhaN^gaH | ghaTAdeH pakShaikadeshatvAt.h | nachAMshe siddhasAdhanatA | ekaikatra prasiddhAvapyAparamANaroH A cha bhUgolakAdasiddheriti | 
abhAvo vA kevalavyatirekiNA sAdhyaH | bhAve hi pratipAdye vyatirekavyAptau tadabhAvasya pratiyogipratItisApekShatayA visheShaNaprasiddhayapekShA | abhAve tu sAdhye nAyaM doShaH | abhAvAbhAvasya bhAvatvena pratiyoginirapekShatvAt.h | evamanye.apyuktivisheShaprakArA draShyavyAH | JOSHI-13 
teShvanyatamasyApyabhAve.aprasiddhavisheShaNatA dUShaNameva | ato na kevalavyatirekiprAmANyamavalambyAprasiddhavisheShaNatAdUShaNatvaM nirasanIyamityata Aha- aprasiddhasyeti ||
sAdhyasyeti karmaNi ShaShThI liN^gasyeti kartari | ayamiti buddhisthaparAmarshaH | bhavedetadyadyayaM kevalavyatirekiNyuktivisheShaH kArya ityatra niyAmakaM syAt.h | na chaitadasti | tathAhi | kimanenoktivisheSheNa kevalavyatirekisAdhyamanvayitAM nIyata uta neti vaktavyam.h | nAdyaH | ukterarthatathAtvaparivartakatvAsambhavAt.h | nahi sahasreNApyuktInAM naro vAnarIkartuM shakyate | shakyatve vA kevalavyatirekiprAmANyaM tyaktaM syAt.h | dvitIyasyedamuktam.h | yadA liN^gasyAprasiddhasya sAdhyasya sAdhakatvamiShyate | yadyuktivisheShaNApi liN^gaM kevalavyatirekisAdhyasAdhakameva nAnvayitAmApadyata itIShyata iti yAvat.h | tadA.ayamuktau visheShaH kena mAnena kartavyatayA j~nAyate na kenApi | ato.aprasiddhavisheShaNa eva kevalavyatirekI sAdhakashcheti nAprasiddhavisheShaNatvasya doShatvamiti |
astyevoktivisheShasya kartavyatAyAM niyAmakam.h | tathAhi | yadyapyuktivisheSho na vyatirekiNamanvayinaM karoti | tathA.api liN^gasya sAdhyena vyAptistAvadashyambhAvinI | nacha sA kevalavyatirekiNi sAkShAduparshayituM shakyA | anvayagrahaNasthalasya vipratipattyA pratiruddhatvAt.h | ataH sAdhyavyatirekasya sAdhanavyatirekeNa vipakShe vyAptiM pradarshyopapAdanIyA | 
yadi vA vyatirekavyAptireva sAdhyasiddheraN^gam.h | tathA.api tad.hgraho.avashyambhAvI | vyatirekashcha pratiyogipratItyadhInapratItika eva | pratiyoginau cha liN^gasAdhyadharmau | tatra liN^gaM pakShe pratItameva | sAdhyadharmashcha na pakShe pratIto nApyanyatra | tatkathaM vyatirekayorapi vyAptigarR^ihyatAm.h | etaistUktivisheShaiH kathaJNchitpratiyoginaH sAdhyadharmasya buddhisthatAyAM sukaro vyAptigrahaH syAt.h | 
pratij~nAvAkyaM chaivamaviditapadArthakaM na prasajyata ityata Aha- sAdhanamiti ||
paramANukArakatAM kAryANAmabhyupagachChatA vaisheShikAdinA paramANusadbhAvaH sAdhyate | tathA pradhAnopAdAnatAM vadatA sAN^khayena pradhAnasadbhAvaH | evamanyadapi samavAyAdikaM tadaN^gIkAribhiH samarthyate | tatra pR^ichChAmaH | yaH paramANvAdikamabhyupaiti taM prati tatsadbhAvaH sAdhyate, uta na santi paramANava iti tadabhAvamabhyupagachChantaM prati | nAdyaH | siddhasya sAdhanAyogAt.h | dvitIye tvabuddhayArUDhasya paramANvAdeH sAdhanAya kathaM vAdinaH prayatnaH kathaM cha tadabhAvaM paro manyeta | pratiyogino.aviditatvAt.h | 
atha manyase kaNAdAdyupadeshena, sAmAnyato dR^iShyasvArthAnumAnena vA svayamavagataM paramANvAdikaM vAdinA shakyata eva sAdhayitum.h | vAdivAkyena cha pratiyoginaH paramANvAderavagame tadabhAvA(numa)bhimatiH prativAdino yuktaiva | nahi pramANenaiva pratiyogI j~nAtavya iti niyamo.asti shashaviShANAdyabhAvapratItyAnupapattiprasaN^gAditi |
yadyevamatyantAprasiddhasyApi paramANvAderanubhavamArgamanatikramya sAdhanamiShyate | tadaitadvayatirekisAdhyasAdhanamapyanubhavAnusAreNaiva kuto nAN^gIkAryam.h | tathAhi | pratyakSheNopadeshena vA.asAdhAra(Nadha)Nau dharmAvekatropalabdhavatastato.anyatra savartrApi tadabhAvopalambhasambhave vyatirekavyAptigrahastAvadvAdinaH sukara eva | prativAdino.api vAdivAkyAvagatapratiyoginastadabhAvAvagamasambhavAt.h | vyatirekavyAptigrahaH sambhavatyeva | tathAcha prAguktarItyA.anvayasamarthanena aprasiddhasAdhyasAdhane sambhavati kimetAbhiH kliShyakalpanAbhiH | evaMcha na pratij~nAvAkyasyAviditapadArthakatvaprasaN^gaH | vAdinA tadarthasya vyutpAditatvA(dyatvA)diti |
upasaMharati- yatreti ||
viShaye kevalavyatirekiNi | evaM sAmAnyAnva(vamanva)yAbhidhAnAdinA sAdhanaM kAryamiti niyAmakaM (mAnaM vA) nAsti | vyAptipratItyAderanyathAsiddhatvAt.h | R^ijunA.anubhavAnusAriNA mArgeNa siddhayato.arthasya vakreNAnAnubhAvikena sAdhanAyogAt.h | viparyaye tathA sAdhanAkaraNe, atiprasaN^gashcha nAsti | svavyAhatyAdinaivAparasyAbhAsatvAt.h | atra kliShyakalpanayaiva sAdhyasAdhanaM kAryamityatiduShyaM vAkyamiti | anena vishiShyavyatirekamAshritya yA mahA.avidyAdivakrarItiH sA.apyapAstA veditavyA | 
bhavedetadyadi kevalavyatirekyanumAnaM bhavet.h | nachaivam.h | pakShadharmatvaM sapakShe sattvaM vipakShAdvayAvR^ittirabAdhitaviShayatvamasatpratipakShatvaM cheti paJNcharUpopapannaM khalvanumAnaM bhavati | nacha kevalavyatirekiNastadasti | sapakShAbhAvena sapakShe sattvAbhAvAt.h | nachaivaM kevalAnvayino.api vipakShAbhAvena vipakShAdvayAvR^itterabhAvAdananumAnatvaprasaN^ga iti vAchyam.h | anvayavyatirekavata evAnumAnatvenAniShyAbhAvAditi | 
dvitIyamAshaN^kayAha- parisheSha iti ||
prasaktapratiShedhe parishiShyamANe buddhiH parisheShaH | dvayoH parasparApekShayotpattirj~naptirvA mithaHsiddhiH | bahUnAM chakravaditaretarApekShayotpattyAdikaM chakrakam.h | svApekShaM svotpattyAdi svAshrayaH | AdipadenAnavasthA | sA chAnavasthitAsiddhotpAdakAdiparamparApekShA | asiddhasAdhakatvena hetunA | paJNchAvayavatAM paJNcharUpopapannatAm.h | aN^gIkAryAH anumAnatvena samastairvAdibhiH | na khalu ko.api vAdI parisheShAdInanAdR^itya parIkShAyAM pravR^itto.asti | 
etaduktaM bhavati | parisheShAdIni tAvadanumAnAni, vyApyaj~nAnAdvayApakaj~nAnamiti tallakShaNAkrAntatvAt.h | pramANaprapaJNcharuchibhirapyanumAnAdbahirbhAvena tatprAmANyasyAnabhyupagatatvAchcha | tAni chAsiddhasyaiva sAdhyasya sAdhakAni | shabdasya hi pR^ithivyAdyaShyasaMsarge pratiShiddhe parisheShAttadatiriktadravyAshritatvaM siddhayati | nacha prAgAkAshasiddheH pR^ithivyAdyatiriktaM dravyaM siddham.h | yena tadAshritatva kvachitprasiddhaM syAt.h | yat.h yasya kAryaM pramitaM pareNAN^gIkR^itaM vA tasya tatkAryatAmaN^gIkurvANaM prati mithaHsiddhiruchyate | nacha sA kvachitprasiddhA | dvayorapi parasparApekShayA pUrvabhAvitvaM (se tve) seti pakShe.api tathA | etena 
chakrakaM vyAkhyAtam.h | asyaiva ghaTasyaitatkAryatvamyupa(mupa)gachChantaM prati svAshrayatvamabhidhIyate | (tachcha) svasyaiva svApekShayA pUrvabhAvitvaM pashchAdbhAvitvaM chAprasiddhameva | asiddhasyaiva kAraNatAM bruvANaM pratyanavasthochyate | nacha kvachitkArye.anavasthitAsiddhakAraNaparamparA siddhA | sAmAnyataH prasiddhistu kevalavyatirekiNyapi samAnA | asiddhasAdhakatvena chaiShAM paJNcharUpopapannatA nAsti | tathA chAnumAnAnAmapyeShAM paJNcharUpopapannatvAbhAvAt.h | vyatireki nAnumAnaM paJNcharU(popannatA)patAvaidhuryAdityanaikAntikamiti |
dUShaNAntaramAha- tanniyama iti ||
anumAne paJNcharUpopapannatAniyamasya nirnibandhanatvAdatAdR^ishasyApyanumAnatve bAdhakAbhAvAchchAprayojako.ayaM hetvAbhAsaH | nanvepAM rUpANAM vyAptipakShadharmataupAyikatvAdasiddhayAdihetvAbhAsapaJNchaka(sya)vyudAsArthatvAchcha kathaM nirnibandhana(tva)tA | kathaM cha vipakShe bAdhakAbhAvaH | uktaprayojanAsiddhereva bAdhakatvAt.h | sapakShe sattvaM vinA.apyanumAnatve bhUrnityA gandhavattvAdityAderasAdhAraNasyApyanumAnatvaM syAditi chenna | sapakShasadbhAvAsadbhAvAbhyAM bhedasiddheriti |
evamAshrayAsiddhayAderadUShaNatvamupapAdya yaduktaM "parihare.api siddhatvaM dUShaNam.h' iti tadayuktam.h | vAde nigrahasthAnAbhAvasyoktatvAdityAshaN^kAM pariharati- siddheti ||

tatra kechidAchakShate | dvividhaM vyAptyabhAvAdikam.h | vAdiprativAdinoranyataramatenobhayamatena cheti | anye tu manyante | anyatarAvyAptyAdikaM nAma nAstyeva | vastuvikalpAsambhavAditi | tatra kintattvamityAkAN^kShAyAmAha- vyabhichAra iti ||
atra vyabhichAra ityavyAptimAtropalakShaNam.h | na kevalamubhayapakShe kintu vAdiprativAdinorekasya pakShe.api vyabhichAro hetvasiddhishcha hetordUShaNameva | yadyapi vastuto.anyataravyabhichArAdikaM na sambhavati tathA.api prAgvastutattvAvadhAraNAdAbhimAnikaM sambhavatyeva | tathAcha hetusAmarthyasandehe.apyahetutvamAvashyakameva | vyAptyAdinimittayA nishchitasyaiva hetutvAditi | tadanyasyetyanena dR^iShyAntasyApi sAdhyAdimattvenAsiddhirdUShaNamiti sUchitam.h |

yadvA dR^iShyAntasya sAdhyasAdhanavaikalyamapi vyabhichArAsivadubhayAnyatararItyA dvividhaM pratipattavya na punarekavidhameva | abhimAnato dvaividhyasyApi sambhavAdityAha- sAdhyeti || ekapakShe.api dUShaNamityanuvartate |

tatra prashnadoSheShvaprayojanatA yadyapyu(ttaro)ttaraprashneShvavadhArayitumashakyA | tathA.api prathamaprashne sambhAvitA dUShaNatvenodbhAvayituM shakyata eva | nahi kathopakrame pradhAnaprameyaprashnamapahAyaivaMvidhaH prashnaH sambhavatIti | anenaiva nyAyenAsaN^gatirapi sarvathA saN^gatyanupalambha evodbhAvyeti draShyavyam.h | 
nanvevaM sati ShaDeva nigrahasthAnAnIti bhajyeta | svavyAhatyasaN^gatyorvirodhAsaN^gatyantarbhAve.api siddhArthatAvaiphalyayoratiriktatvAdityata Aha- siddheti ||
dUShaNAntarbhAvakathanaprasaN^gena prAguktapramANatritvaniyamasiddhaye paraiH pR^ithak.hpramANatvenAN^gIkR^itAnAmarthApattyAdInAmuktAntarbhAvamAha- arthApattIti ||

etenaitadapi nirastam.h | yadAhuH | anumAnatvapakShe kiM bahirbhAve jIvanamAtraM liN^gamuta gR^ihAbhAvamAtram.h athavA vishiShyam.h | na prathamadvitIyau | vyabhichArAt.h | na tR^itIyaH | viruddhayorvisheShaNavisheShyabhAvAnupapatteH | avirodhapratIteshcha bahirbhAvakalpanottarakAlInatvenetaretarAshrayApatteriti | jIvanagrahAbhAvayorvirodhasya abhAvAt.h | bhAve vA.arthApatterapyanupapatteH | ato.avinAbhAvabalenArthapratItihetutvAdarthApattiranumAnameva |

gavaya ityatideshavAkyAnubhUtamarthaM pratyakShe(Na) gavaye pratyabhij~nAnam.h gavayapadaM smaran.h gavayapadasya gavaye saN^gatimavagachChati | tadidaM sAdharmyopamAnam.h | vaidharmyopamAnaM tu gavAdivad.hdvishapho na bhavatyashva iti vAkyArthapratyabhij~nAnAdashve.ashvapadasaN^gatigrahaNam.h | dharmamAtropamAnamapi dIrghagrIvatvAdidharmavAnpashuruShyra iti vAkyArthapratyabhij~nAnAduShyrapadavyutpattiriti manyante | tatra yadyapi saMj~nAsaMj~nisambandhapratipattiH prAggavayAdidarshanAdatideshavAkyena prayogAdinA liN^gena vA bhavituM nArhati | sambandhino.anavagame sambandhasyAvagantumashakyatvAt.h | tathA.api gavayAdidarshanottarakAlaM sAdharmyAdinA liN^genaiva bhaviShyati | etasyAM dashAyAmatideshavAkyaM vyAptigrAhakatvenopayujyate | yathA hi pR^ithivItvAbhisambandhAtpR^ithivIti vyavahartavyeti shrutavataH pR^ithivItvAbhisambandhaM kvachiddravye pashyato.anumAnenaiva saMj~nAsaMj~nisambandhapratipattirabhyupagatA | tathA prakR^ite.apIti kathamidaM pR^ithak.h pramANaM syAditi |

chastvarthaH | sukhAderAntarasya sAkShivedyasyAbhAvastu niyamena sAkShipratyakSheNaiva grAhya ityarthaH | yadvA.abhAva iti pramANamevochyate | tasya sukhAderiti paramparayA sambandhaH | niyamena pratyakShAntargata iti sambandhaH | anena bAhyAnAM pratyakShayogyAnAM ghaTAdInAmabhAvaH pratyakShAnumAnavedya ityuktam.h | tadayuktam.h | ekasyaiva j~nAnasya svatantrakAraNadvayajanyatvAnupapatteH | parasparaviruddhaparokShAparokShatvalakShaNAkAradvayaprApteshchetyata uktam.h- kvachiditi ||
tathA.apyanupapattireva, pratyakShagrAhye.athare.anumAnAnavakAshAdityata Aha- anyatreti || sukhAderanyatra ghaTAdau pratiyogini sati, yo.abhAvo.abhAvapramANaM khaDiti prApnoti, tatpratyakSham.h | yattu vilambena jAyate tadanumAnamiti | etaduktaM bhavati | ghaTAdyabhAvagrAhakaM yogyAnupalabdhirUpaM pramANaM pR^ithageveti mImAMsakAH | anupalabdhiliN^gakamanumAnameve taditi saugatAH | tadubhayamapyanupapannam.h | pratiyogismaraNavataH purovartini bhUtale ghaTAdyabhAvasya pratyakSheNaiva(chAva)gamyamAnatvAt.h | indriyAnvayavyatirekAnuvidhAyino.abhAvapratyayasyApratyakShaphalatvAnupapatteH | aparokShakAratvasyAnubhavasiddhatvAt.h | bAdhakAbhAvAchchAnyatropakShayakalpanAnupapatteH | anyathA rUpAdij~nAne.api pramANAntarakalpanAprasaN^gAt.h | liN^gadarshanavyAptismaraNAdivilambena vinA khaDiti jAyamAnasyAnumAnaphalatvAnupapatteH | liN^gasya j~nAtasyaiva karaNatvAdanupalabdherapyabhAvatvenAnupalabdhyantarApekShAyAmanavasthAprasaN^gAchcha | 
nanu cha prAtashchatvarAdau pratiyogismaraNAbhAvena gajAdyabhAvaMmananubhUya deshAntaraM gato gajasmR^itimAnprAtashchatvare gajo nAsIditi pratipadyate | na tatra pratyakShasyAvakAsha ityanupalabdhilakShaNaM pR^ithak.h pramANaM tatrAN^gIkAryamiti | maivam.h | tatrAbhAvasyApratyakShatve.apyanupalabdhiliN^gakAnumAnavedyatA.abhyupagamAt.h | anupalabdheshcha smaraNAbhAvaliN^gAnumeyatvAt.h | ata eva tatra kShaNaM dhyAtvA nAsIchchatvare gaja iti pratipadyate | smaraNAbhAvo.apyanupalabdhyantarAnumeya ityanavasthetyapi nAsti | sAkShigrAhyANAM buddhisukhAdInAmavabhAvasya niyamena sAkShi(pratyakSha)vedyatvAditi |
tathA.apyupakramopasaMhArAvabhyAsApUvartAphalArthavAdAH pramANAni santIti kathaM tattritvaniyama ityata Aha- prArambhAdyAshcheti ||
yuktayaH anumAnAni | kuta ityata Aha- Agameti ||
yato.akhilAH prArambhAdyA niyatavyAptayo, yo yatra prArabhyate sa tatra pratipAdya ityAdirUpAM vyAptimapekShamANA evAgamArthAvasityarthA bhavantyato yuktaya evetyarthaH | etenAgamAntarbhAvo.api nirastaH | upakramAdyA AgamaviShayA eva na chArthApattyupamAbhAvA iti yogavibhAgaH | 
vAkyAdInAmapi pramANAnamanumAnAntarbhAvamAha- vAkyamiti ||
yato vAkyAdayo.api tathAvidhA vyAptimapekShyaivAgamArthAvasityarthAstatastathAvidhA yuktaya evetyarthaH | upakramAdInAmuttarottaraM prAbalyaM vAkyAdInAM tu pUrvapUrvamiti j~nApanAya yogavibhAgaH  
yadyupakramAdayo vAkyAdayashchAnumAne.antarbhavanti tarhi katham.h "upakramopasaMhArAvabhyAso.apUrvatA phalam.h | arthavAdopapattI cha liN^gaM tAtparyanirNaye' ityupakramAdInAmanumAnAparaparyA(yAyA upa)yopapatteH pR^ithaktvenoktiH ta| tathA "shrutirliN^gaM samAkhyA cha vAkyaM prakaraNaM tathA' iti vAkyAdInAM liN^gAdityata Aha- kurupANDavavaditi ||
yathA pANDavAnAM kuru(visheSha)tve.api sAmAnyavisheShApekShayA "santAnabIjaM kurupANDavAnAm.h' ityAdau kurubhyaH pR^ithagvachanaM tathA teShAmupakramAdInAM vAkyAdInAM chAnumAnatve.apyupapatterliN^gAchcha pR^ithagvachanaM yuktamityarthaH | 
nanu tathA.api shAkunalipyakSharacheShyAsambavaitihyaparisheShAH pR^ithak.h pramANAni santIti chet.h(na) | shAkunalipyakSharacheShyAnAmantarbhAvasya na vilakShaNAdhikaraNe sUchitatvAt.h | sambhavaitihyayoranumAnAgamAntarbhAvasya sarvavAdisampratipannatvAt.h | parisheShasya cha "parisheSho mithaH siddhiH' ityanenaivAnumAnatvasya sthitatvAt.h | 
nanu tathA.api jainAstarkaM pR^ithak.h pramANamAhuH | satyam.h | mithassisiddhirItyAdinA so.apyanumAnAntargata iti sUchitameva | 
atrAha tarkaH pramANameva na bhavati | kuto.anumAnam.h | tathAhi | aniShyaprasaJNjanaM tarkaH | aniShyaM cha dvividhaM (dhA) prAmANikaparityAgo.aprAmANikasvIkArashcheti | sa paJNchavidhaH | AtmAshrayAnyonyAshrayachakrakAnavasthApramANabAdhitArthaprasaN^gabhedAt.h | tatra prasaN^go nAma vyApyAN^gIkAre.aniShyavyApakaprasaJNjanam.h | 
so.ayaM tarkaH pramANAnAmanugrAhakaH | anugrahashcha pramANaviShayasambhAvanAdirUpaH | tathAhi | bhUtale ghaTaH kinna syAditi viparItashaN^kayA kuNThitashaktikaM pratyakShaM na tAvadghaTAbhAvaM nishninuyAdyAvadyadyatra ghaTo.abhaviShyattadA bhUtalamivAdrakShyata tattulyadarshanasAmagrIkatvAditi tarkeNa viparItashaN^kA nApanIyate | tarko hi durjana iva parAbhilaShitaM vi(vyava)chChidya ghaTAbhAvaM sambhAvayati | athedAnIM pratyakShaM sujana iva svaprameyaM nishchinoti | 
evaM kvachidvayabhichArashaN^kayopAdhishaN^kayA vA dhUmavAnapi parvato.agnimAnmA bhUditi pakShe vipakShashaN^kayA.anumAne kuNThite yadi niragnikaH syAtparvatastadA nirdhUmo.api syAdityAdirUpastarkaH pravartate | sa hyupAdhikoTau tadAyattavyabhichArakoTau vA.aniShyamupajanayanviparItechChAM vichChinatti | tatashcha nishchitAvinAbhAvamanumAnaM niShkammapevAgnimattvaM nishchAyayati | 
tathA svargakAmo yajetetyatra liN^gA pratIyamAnAyA bhAvanAyA bhAvyapekShAyAM, kiM bhAvyo dhAtvartho bhavatu, bhavatu vA svarga, iti sandehe samAnapadopAttatvAddhAtvartha eva bhAvya iti shaN^kayA kuNThitashaktiH shabdo joShamevAste | yadi dhAtvartho bhAvyaH syAttadA vidheriShyAbhyupAyatvaM shAstrasya cha tadbodhakatvaM tatpraNetushchAptatvaM prekShAvatAM pravR^ittishchetyetatsavarM na syAditi tarkeNApanItAyAM shaN^kAyAM shabdaH svargameva bhAvyatayA.avadhArayati | 
evaM nAnAvidhastarkasAdhyo.anugrahaH svayameva boddhavyaH | 
so.ayaM pramArUpaM vA pramANaM syAlliN^gadasharnavadapramArUpaM vendriyAdivat.h | na tAvadanyaH | ta(rka)syAhAyarrUpatvAt.h | na tatkaraNamapi pad.hANam.h | pramAphalatvAbhAvAt.h | na dvitIyaH | AropitaviShayatvAt.h | viparyayaprAmANyopagatau tu tenAsya niyAmakaH sambandho nAsti | asambaddhasya gamakatve chAtiprasaN^gaH | anumAnatve chAsyApAdakaM liN^gamApAdyaM sAdhyamiti vaktavyam.h | nacha tadyuktam.h | ApAdakasyAhAryatvenAnyatarAsiddhatvAt.h | ApAdyasya chAniShyatvena bAdhitatvAt.h | na hyasiddhaM liN^gaM bhavati | nApi bAdhitaM sAdhyam.h | sati chAshraye.anumAnaM bhavati | na(hi)cha bhUtale ghaTo.asti yaH sAdhyasAdhanayorAshrayaH syAt.h | vyadhikaraNatA chApAdyApAdakayorbahulamupalabhyate | ApAdyasya sAdhyatve.apasiddhAntashcha syAt.h | dhUmasadbhAvasya svayamabhyupagantavyatvAt.h | tasmAdviparyayaparatantratvAdapramANameva pramANAnAmanugrAhakastarka iti kuto.asyAnumAne.antarbhAva ityata Aha- svanyAyairiti ||
nyAyashabdena dhamirliN^gavyAptidR^iShyAntA uchyante | na kevalaM parasya kintu svasyApi ye siddhA nyAyAste svanyAyAH | sAdhanamiti dUShaNasyApyupalakShaNam.h | parasyaiva siddhA nyAyAH paranyAyAH svasyaiva siddhA nyAyAH svanyAyAH | chashabdena sAdhanaM cha prativAdinaH prati | 
etaduktaM bhavati | dvividhaM hi kAryaM kathakasya, svapakShasAdhanaM parapakShadUShaNaM cheti | tatra sAdhanaM svaparasammataireva nyAyaiH kAryaM nAnyataramAtrasiddhaiH | yathA parvato.agnimAndhUmavattvAdyo yo dhUmavAnasAvagnimAnyathA mahAnasa iti | kvachitpunaH sAdhanaM svamAtrasiddhaireva nyAyaiH kriyate | tatra cha pareNAnyatarAsiddhayAdAvudAhR^ite taM prati tatsAdhanaM kriyate | yathA shabdo.anityaH kAryatvAt.h | kAryashchAsAvavyaJNjakaprayatnAnantaropalabdherityAdi | sarvathA sAdhanamubhayasiddhanyAyasAdhyam.h | dUShaNaM tu dvividham.h | idamitthaM na bhavatIti vA.aniShyopadarshanena vA | tatrAdyamubhayasiddhanyAyaireva kAryam.h | yathA shabdo na dravyaM shrotragrAhyatvAtsAmAnyavaditi | kvachitpunaH svamAtrasiddhairnyAyaiH sAdhanamiva dUShaNamapi kR^itvA paraM prati tatsAdhanaM kriyate | yathA tatraiva prayoge kAlenAnaikAntyaudbhAvane tasyAtIndriyatvasAdhanamityAdi | sarvathA.a.adyaM dUShaNamubhayasiddhanyAyasampAdyameva | dvitIyaM tu parasiddhaireva nyAyaiH kAryam.h | yathA yadi parvato niragnikastadA nirdhUmaH syAditi | atra hyApAdakasya parasiddhatvameva bhAvyaM na 
svasiddhatvam.h | tadatiriktAN^gAnAM tu svasiddhaH satI asatI vA na vivakShitA parasiddhirevopayujyate | tadeva cha tarka iti vyavahriyate | tena tatrAshrayAsiddhayanyatarAsiddhI bhUShaNe eva na dUShaNe | 
vyadhikaraNatvaM tu na kvApi dUShaNamityuktam.h | shakyasampAdanaM cha tarke.api sAmAnAdhikaraNatvam.h | avashyaM chaitadevam.h | anyathA kevalAnvayidharmasya kevalavyatirekiNyabhAvAt.h tasyAnanumAnatvApatteH | sAmAnyalakShaNasadbhAvAt.h, visheShalakShaNAbhAve.api na doSha iti chetsamaM prakR^ite.api | vyAptyapekShayA gamakatvasya tarke.api vidyamAnatvAt.h | vidyamAna evAshraye vidyamAnasyaivetyapi sAmAnyalakShaNe niveshyata iti chet.h | tarhi vipakShAbhAvo vA sapa(kShe sa)pakShasadbhAvo.api vA niveshyatAm.h | prayojanAbhAvAnneti chenna | prakR^ite.api samatvAt.h | tarkanirAsaH prayojanamiti chettatrApi kevalavyatikinirAsaH prayojanaM bhaviShyati | nirnibandhano.asAviti chet.h  samaM prakR^ite.api | sAdhane.apyasiddhasyAnumAnatvaM syAditi chettarhi vipakShavataH sapakShe.asato.api kevalAnvayitvaM syAt.h | tadvisheShalakShaNa eva nikShepyamiti chetsamAnamatrApi | ata eva svanyAyaiH sAdhanamityAdinA vyavasthA darshiteti | JOSHI-14 
AbhUdAshrayAsiddhayanyatarAsiddhayoratra dUShaNatvam.h | tathA.api bAdhApasiddhAntasadbhAvAnna tarkasyAnumAnatvamiti chet.h na | tayorapyasiddhivatsAdhanadUShaNavisheShayoreva dUShaNatvena prasaN^gAnumAne tadabhAvAditi pUrvavatparihAraH siddha eva | tathA.api, sAdhane.apyavAntarabhedakalpanayA tarhi bAdhAderadUShaNatvaM kalpyatAmityatiprasaN^ganirAsAya parihArAntaramAha- prasaN^geti ||

paroktasyArthAntaraM parikalpya tasyArthAntarasyottaramityarthaH |

tadA ChalavAkye.api tathA shakyamiti | evaM tarhi parasiddhenaiva nyAyena parashChalajAtyorduShyiM bodhanIyaH | tataH paraM tu na shaN^kayata eva | vyAghAtAvadhitvAdAshaN^kAyA ityuktaM bhavati | tathAcha paranyAyastAvadasAdhuH | tena bodhyamAnA duShyirAbhAsabhUtaiveti ChalAdervAstavamaduShyatvaM syAt.h | na syAt.h | na hyatra paranyAyaH pramANatvenopanyasyate kintvasAdhurayaM tvadIyo nyAyo yataH svAtmAnamapi vyAhantItyabhiprAya iti chettulyametatprakR^ite.api | na hyatrApi niragnikatvaM pramANatayopanyasyate.api tu asAdhurayaM tvadIyo niragnikatvAN^gIkAro yataH pramANaviruddhaM nirdhUmatvamapyaN^gIkArayatItyabhiprAyaiti | jAtyAdau svaviru(ddhatApa)ddhApattistarke tu pramANaviruddhApattiriti vailakShaNyamAtram.h | asti cha svaviruddhApattirantatastarke.api | yathoktam.h | "vyAghAtAvadhirAshaN^kA tarkaH shaN^kAvadhirmataH' iti | tadevaM tarkasya dUShaNAnumAne.antarbhAvAdyuktamuktamiti |

syAdetat.h | brahmaNaH pratiyogitvAbhAve.anuyogitvaM syAt.h | tathAcha svapnasya tato vailakShaNyaM na syAt.h | tadabhAve cha sAlakShaNyApattyA brahmasvapnayormithyAtvAdi prasajyetetyuktamayuktam.h | sadharmake hi vastunyekasya dharmasyAbhAvena tadviruddhasya dharmasya bhAvo bhAvena chAbhAvo(nyasya bhAvo) vaktuM shakyate | yathA parimANavattvAddravyasya mahattvAbhAve.aNutvasya aNutvabhAve vA mahattvAbhAvasyApAdanam.h | yathA (vA) vakturmandavachanAbhAve tIvravachanam.h | tadbhAve vA tadabhAvaH shakyApAdanaH | brahma tu sakaladharmavikalamiti kathaM tatrApAdanaM pratiyogitvAderivAyogitvAderapyabhAvAt.h | nahi parimANarahite guNAdau vaktR^itvashUnye kAShThe choktaprasaN^gAvakAsho.asti | tathA svapane.api noktaprasaN^gAvakAshaH | svayamasatyasya vailakShaNyavadavailakShaNyasyApyabhAvAt.h | nahi bhrAntasarpavisarpaNAdayaH satyA bhaveyurityAshaN^kaya brahmaNo nirdharmakatvaM dUShayati | yadItyAdinA Ishatajj~nAnetyataH prAktanena prakaraNena |

na khalvanumAnavichArAparaparyAyAyAH jij~nAsAyA vastusvarUpamAtraj~nAnaM prayojanam.h | tasya prAgeva siddhatvAt.h | asiddhau vA(chA).a.ashrayAsiddhasyAnumAnasyAnutthAnAt.h | kinnAmedamiti svarUpAnuvAdenetthamiti vyApakadharmavishiShyadharmij~nAnam.h | dhUmAnumAnAdau tathA darshanAt.h | tathA cha kathaM nirdharmakasya jij~nAsyateti | etena svapne.api prasaN^gAnavakAsho(.api) nirastaH | tathA sati mAyAmAtramityanumAnAsambhavAt.h | AropitAbhyAM vyApyavyApakAbhyAM tatsambhavaM iti chenna | svarUpAsiddhibAdhaprasaN^gAditi |
yadyapi na brahmaniShThena kenachiddharmeNa tatra dharmAntaraM vidhitsitaM tathA.api kasyachiddharmasya nivR^ittyA dharmAntarasya bhrAntiprasaktasyAnyatra sato nivR^ittirj~nApyate | yathoktam.h | siddhaM tu nivartakatvAditi | evaJNcha nirdharmakasya kathaM jij~nAsyatA.anupapattirityata Aha- itthambhAvo hIti ||
asya brahmaNaH pratiyogitA virodhitA | prapaJNchadharmavyAvR^ittimatteti yAvat.h | na khalu nirAdhArayA kasyachiddharmasya nivR^ittyA nirAdhAraiva dhamarAntaravyAvR^ittiranumAtuM shakyA | evaMvidhAnumAnapravR^itteralaukikatvAt.h | ato brahmaniShThayaiva brahmaniShTheti vAchyam.h | yadi chAsya dharmo na syAnna tarhi vyAvR^ittimattA.api syAditi | itthamiti j~nAnaM jij~nAsAphalaM chedbrahmaNItthambhAva eva svIkAryaH syAt.h | tat.h kiM dharmeNeti mandAshaN^kAnirAsAya "itthambhAvo hi dhamaro.asya' ityanuvAdena parihAro.abhihitaH | yadvA.astu vyAvR^ittimattA brahmaNaH kiM dharmeNetyata idamuktam.h | na vidhirUpa eva dharmaH kinnAmetthambhAvamAtraM prakR^itamiti | tadanena brahma na nirdharmakaM jij~nAsyatvAtparvatavadityanumAnaM (cha) sUchitaM bhavati |

prabhuNA.apIti sambandhaH | "adR^ishyatvAdiguNako dharmokteH' ityAdineti sheShaH | yadvA na vidhirUpa eva dharmaH kinnAmetthambhAvamAtramityata prayogamanena pramANayati | atrachApishabdo na bhinnakramaH | guNashabdashcha dhamarvachano na pAribhAShikavachanaH | adR^ishyatvAdInAM tadabhAvAt.h | 
nanvasmAbhirbhAvarUpA eva dharmA brahmaNo nAN^gIkriyante.abhAvAtmakAstu svIkriyanta eva | ato na sUtravirodha ityata Aha- yadIti ||
tAdR^ishA abhAvAtmakAH | yatA.adR^ishyatvAdyAH pramANAvagatAstathA sarvaj~natvAdayo bhAvarUpA api yaH sarvaj~na ityAdishrutisiddhA iti te.apyaN^gIkAryAH | atha tadaN^gIkAre neha nAnA.astItyAdishrutivirodha ityuchyate so.adR^ishyatvAdyaN^gIkAre.api samAnaH | ato.ardhachara(jara)tIyasyAprAmANikatvAtsarvaj~natvAdayo.api svIkAryAH | adR^ishyatvAdayo.api vA tyAjyA iti |

te sarvaj~natvAdayo.anyApekShA iti yadi nAN^gIkriyante tarhi te.adR^ishyatvAdayo.api na dR^ishyamadR^ishyamityevamanyApekShAssyuriti nAN^gIkAryA eva | tathA cha sUtravirodhastadavastha eva | viShayatayA.anyApekShatvaM pratiyogitayA.anyApekShatvamiti (tu) vaiShamyamAtram.h | syuShya iti suShAmAdiShu draShyavyam.h |

nanUtpattau sArvaj~nAdeH sarvAsApekShatAbhAve.api j~naptau sA.astyeva | vidita eva sarvasminsArvaj~nAdi vij~nAyate nAvidita iti | evaM tarhi sattA.api mA bhUdutpattau parApekShA | j~naptau tu bhavatyevetyAha- desheti ||
deshakAlAnapekShA deshakAlapratItyanapekShA | deshakAlapratItyapekShaiva dR^ishyata ityanvayo.api draShyavyaH | yadi kashchidvaiyAtyAtkvachiddeshakAlapratItyanapekShA.api sattA dR^ishyata iti brUyAttadA vyAghAtaH syAt.h | deshakAlavyatirekeNa (kvachitsattAsha) kiMshabdArthAnirvachanAt.h | sattApratItAvavarjanIyatayA deshakAlau dR^ishyete na tu tadapekSheti chenna | abhUdbhavati bhaviShyatItyAdipratItimavadhUya sattAyA apratibhAsAt.h | niyatavishiShyapratItike.a(tadana)napekShAyAM na kutrApyapekShA syAt.h | tadidamuktam.h- kvApIti ||

tat.h tarhi tanmithyAtvamiti vA | satyameva tvayA.aN^gIkR^itamiti | nacha tadupapadyate(dyujyate) | sarvo.api hi vedo.apauruSheyaH svataHpramA(NaM cha)NabhUtashcha | tatra chaikasya bhAgasyAprAmANye parasyApi tatsyAt.h tasya prAmANye.asyApi kathaM tanna syAt.h | tAtparyaliN^gabhAvAbhAvAbhyAM vyavastheti chAsaN^gatam.h | tathAtve hyasya bhAgasyAnyatra tAtparyaM vAchyaM syAt.h | nacha niShedhAyAnuvAda ityupapAditam.h | ahiMsAdishyenAdividhivadvidvadavidvadviShayatayA vyavasthA.astviti chenna | vaiShamyAt.h | dhanatvasya chAnabhidhAnAt.h | athaikyaM pratipAdayituM buddhishuddhaye sArvaj~nAdyavidyAmAnamapi pratipAdyate | sarvatra prasR^itA hi buddhiH saguNe brahmaNi dattapadA krameNaikye pravishatIti chenna | pratikUlatvAt.h | sArvaj~nAdipratipAdanena hi bhedavAsanaiva dR^iDhanirUDhA syAdityeShA dik.h |

evaM tarhyaikyavAkyaprAmANyamapi tathAvidhameva (mantavyam.h) | tadabAdhyatve.apyadvaitahAnisAmAnyenoktalakShaNamokShAsiddheH | nahi vAkyaM vA tatprAmANyaM vA tadartho bhedAbhAvo vA brahmeti | pratyakShaprAmANyasyAbAdhyatve bahuprapaJNchApattiH | AgamaprAmANyAbAdhyatAyAM tu naivamiti chenna | asya visheShasya vyarthatvAdityAshayavAnAha- neti ||

svatastvadharmasya prAmANyaM dharmi, adhikaraNatayA vivakShitamiti saptamyupapattiH | yadyAgamaprAmANyasya svatastvamuchyate tadA pratyakShaprAmANyamapi svata eveti brUmaH | samyaN^.hmithyAj~nAnasAdhAraNakAraNamAtrajanyatvaM vA samyaN^.hmithyAj~nAnasAdhAraNaj~nApakamAtraj~neyatvaM vA prAmANyasya svatastvam.h | tadAgamajanyaj~nAnavatpratyakShajanyasyApyavishiShyameva | tathA chAgamaprAmANyasya svatastvamaN^gIkurvato yatA tadviShayasatyatA sammatA tathA svataHpramANapratyakShaviShayavishvasattA(tyatA).api kathaM na te sammateti |
syAdetat.h | pratyakShAgamayoH svataHprAmANye.apyasti visheShaH | yatpratyakShaM tAtkAlikameva j~nAnasya prAmANyaM janayati 
vAkyantvAtyantikam.h | tathA j~nAnagrAhakaH sAkShI pratyakShaj~nAnasya tAtkAlikameva prAmANyaM gR^ihNAti vAkyajanyaj~nAnasya tvAtyantikamiti | maivam.h | asyAM vyavasthAyAM niyAmakAbhAvasyoktatvAt.h | doShAntaraM chAha- prAmANyasya cheti ||
amAnaM bAdhitamAnatvaM (naM) chetpratyakSham.h | tAtkAlikashabdena hIdAnImasti kAlAntare tu bAdhya(tva)miti parasyAbhimatam.h | tatra yadi cha pratyakShaM kAlAntare.api bAdhitaprAmANyaM syAttarhIdAnIM tasya mAnatA.astIti kutaH syAt.h | kAlatrayasattAniShedharUpatvAdbAdhasya yadi cha pratyakShaprAmANyamidAnIM satsyAtkathaM kAlAntare.api tarhi bAdhyeteti vyAhatameva tAtkAlikatvavachanam.h | apramANameva bhavatu tarhi pratyakShamiti chet.h | satyam.h | bhavati bhavato.ayaM manorathaH | tatsiddhirevedAnImapi ka(po)phoNiguDAyate | 
advitIyabrahmAvasthAnalakShaNaM mokShamabhyupetya pratyakShaprAmANyAbAdhyatAvadAgamaprAmANyAbAdhyatAyAmapi taddhAniH samAnetyuktam.h | idAnIntu sa evAnupapanna ityAshayavAnpR^ichChati- mithyAtvamAnamiti || 
vishvamithyAtvapratipAdakamAnamAgamo.anumAnaM vA mokShe.api mAnamiti mokShasamaye.apyabAdhitasvarUpaprAmANyamityarthaH | neti bAdhitasvarUpaprAmANyamityarthaH | kiMshabdaH pUrveNa pareNa cha sambaddhayate | yadvA kAkvaiva mAnamityayaM prashno j~nAtavyaH | iti pR^iShyasyottaraM, bhaNyatAm.h | Adye doShamAha- mAnatva iti ||
abAdhitasvarUpaprAmANyapakShe tenaiva sad.hdvitIyatvAdadvaitahAniH syAdityuktalakShaNo mokSho na siddhayet.h | dvitIye dUShaNamAha- amAnatve.apIti ||
amokShatA vivakShitAvasthAyA iti sheShaH | vishvamithyAtvamAnasya tatprAmANyasya cha bAdhyatvapakShe.api mokSho na siddhayati | kathamityata Aha- vishvasyeti ||
vishvamithyAtvamAnaM yadA na mA bAdhitasvarUpaprAmANyaM syAttadA vishvasya punarApattiH syAt.h | nAstitvapramANabAdhasyAstitvAvyabhichArAt.h | vishvasadbhAve cha kathamuktalakShaNo mokShaH syAditi | Adau tAvatpratyakSheNa vishvaM prAptam.h | tadAgamAdinA.a.apAtato.apanIyam.h | AgamAdeshcha bAdhe punastadApatitamiti pratItyapekShayA punaHshabdaH | vishvaM tadbAdhakaM chobhayamapi bAdhitamiti chenna | uttaratra dUShaNAt.h |
kiJNcha muktiH satI vA.asatI vA | pakShadvaye.api noktalakShaNA muktiH siddhayati | kathamiti | AdyaM pratyAha- asti chediti ||
AtmasvarUpameva muktiH | yathoktam.h | "AtmaivAj~nAnahAniH' iti | "avidyAstamayo mokShaH' iti cha | tatkathaM dvaitApattirityato muktyavasthetyuktam.h | avasthaivaiShA.a.atmano na tvAtmaiva | tathAtve hi prAgeva siddhatvAt.h prayatnavaiyarthyam.h | na chAtmA j~nAnasya sAdhyo.anAditvAt.h | avidyAdhvaMsavishiShyo na prAk.hsiddho j~nAnasAdhyashcheti chettatkiM sa eva muktiH | addheti chet.h | tarhi vishiShyasya sattvAbhAvena satI muktirityayuktaM syAt.h | kiJNcha muktirnAma dharmaH | sa kathamAtmaiva syAditi | 
dvitIyaM parAchaShye- ato.anyashcheti ||
sattvapakShAtpakShAntare | yadi muktirasatI syAttadA.a.atmano.amuktatvaM syAt.h | viShANAsattve shasho hyaviShANI dR^iShyaH | tathAcha kuta uktalakShaNatvam.h | atha matam.h | na muktiH satI nApyasatI kintvanirvachanIyeti | tadA.apyamuktataiva(dapyayuktameva) | saMsAre.apyanirvachanIyenaiva hi dvitIyena sad.hdvitIyatvam.h | taduttaramapi tachchetsyAtkathamamuktatvaM na bhavet.h | etena paJNchamaprakAratA.api nirastA | anirvachanIyatA.aparihArAt.h | nahi chaturthaprakAratAvasthitiranirvachanIyatvam.h | tathA sati nirvachanIyatApatteH | anirvachanIyAvidyAnivR^ittiH kathamanirvachanIyA syAditi chet.h | ghaTapradhvaMso yathA tatheti jAnIthAH | tadetatsaN^grahAyAto.anyathetyuktam.h | anyathA.asatI chedityavakShyat.h | 
evameva mukteradvitIyabrahmAvasthAnarUpatAnirAsAya kAle.api vikalpya doSho.abhidhAtavya ityAha- tathA kAla iti ||
nanu cha mokShadashAyAM kAlo.asti na veti vikalpya "asti ched.hdvaitApattiH' iti dUShaNaM chAstu | "ato.anyathA.amuktatvam.h' iti kathamatidesha ityata Aha- kAlAdhInA hIti ||
kAlAdhInA niyamena kAlAdhikaraNA | yadvastu tatkAlasambandhyeveti vyApteriti hi shabdArthaH |

kintato yadyevamadhikaraNena kAlena vyAptA muktirityata Aha- kAleti ||

chaitanyasya sato bandhAbhAvalakShaNe mokShe.asati devadattavanmuktAbhimatasyApi saMsAritvaM bhavet.h | bandha(sya)mithyAtvAtsaMsAro muktishcha na sta eveti chennAnaN^gIkR^itatvamevAniShyatvaM kintvaprAmANikatvAdikam.h | nacha bandhamithyAtvaM prAmANikamityuktaM prAk.h | tadevamAgamAditaH pratyakShasya daurbalyaM nirAkurvatA tanmiSheNa prAbalyaM cha vyutpAditam.h | sAkShipratyakShasyAgamAdiprAmANyagrAhakatvenopajIvyatAyAstaditarasya sAkShinishchitapramANa(prAmANya)tAyAshcha sUchitatvAt.h | tatastadviruddhasyAgamAderevAprAmANyaM yuktamiti | 
na kevalamupajIvyatvAdiguNenAnyataH prabalaM pratyakSham.h | kintu svabhAvato.apItyAshayavAnAha- kva cheti ||
pratyakShataH prAptamiti sAkShAtkArasiddham.h | anumAnAgamashabdau liN^gavachanavachanau | prAmANyanirNayasyedAnIM kriyamANatvAt.h | dR^iShyamiti sheShaH | yadi hi pratyakShaprAptaM kvachidanumAnAgamAbhyAM bAdhitamupalabdhavantaH tadA pratImo.anumAditaH pratyakShasya daurbalyam.h | nacha tathA | Ishvare doShagrAhipratyakShamAgamAdibAdhitaM dR^iShyamiti chet.h | satyam.h | tatrAgamAderupajIvyatayA bAdhakatvamiti vakShyAmaH | "prAbalyamAgamasyaiva jAtyA teShu triShu smR^itam.h' ityasya vaidikArtaviShayatvAdatra cha pR^ithivyAdiprapaJNchasya prastutatvAnna virodhaH | 
dR^iShyaM cha dahanashaityAnumAnasya, mama karNe pravishya gajo garjatItyAdivAkyasya cha pratyakShabAdhitatvAt.h | tatrApi pratyakShamupajIvyatvAdbAdhakaM natu svabhAveneti chet.h | na | dharmivyApakavyApyavyAptigrAhakatvAbhAvAddahanauShNyAdigrAhiNaH pratyakShasya | anauShNyamuShNatA.abhAvaH | sa cha pratiyogij~nAnAdhInaj~nAnaH pratiyogibhUtaM chauShNyaM tejasyeva pratyakSheNa pratyetavyamiti tasyopajIvyatvamiti chenna | uktottaratvAt.h | anuShNatAsAdhane hIdamupapA(ditam.h)danam.h | kenachiddhetunA shaityasAdhane tvasyAnavakAshaH | yadA cha samastasyApi tejaso.anauShNyaM sAdhyate tadA bhavatvidaM vyutpAdanam.h | agnimAtrapakShIkAre tu nedamupayujyate | saurAdau tejasyuShNatAM sparshanenopalabhya chakShuShopalabdhe.agnAvanauShNyasAdhanasya tu svabhAvaprabalenaiva pratyakSheNa bAdha ityeShA dik.h | 
dehasyAtmatvaM pratyakShaprAptamapi deho nAtmA bhUtatvAtkAryatvAdghaTavadityAdyanumAnena "taM svAchCharIrAtpravR^ihet.h' ityAgamena cha bAdhitaM dR^iShyam.h | anyathA bAdhakAntarAbhAvAddehAtmatvasya vAstavatApAtAt.h | tatkathametadityata Aha- dehAtmatvamiti ||
dehAtmatvaM pratyakShataH prAptamanumAnAgamabAdhitaM dR^iShyamiti yadi brUyAttadA tanneti brUma ityarthaH | na taditi pUrveNottareNa cha sambaddhayate | kuto netyata Aha- na taditi ||
dehAtmatvaM pratyakShaprAptameva na bhavati | ataH pratyakShaprAptasyAnumAnAdinA bAdha ityatra nedamudAharaNam.h | ayamabhisandhiH | nAstyeva dehAtmatvapratItiH | yA.anumAnAdinA bAdhyate | yeShAM chAsti nAstikAdInAM teShAmapi nendriyajA | kintvanumAnAgamAbhAsajanyaiveti | mA bhUtpaNDitarUpANAM dehAtmatvapratItiH | pAmArANAM tvastyeva | saivAsmAkamudAharaNaM bhaviShyatItyataH kvachidityuktam.h | 
tadupapAdayati- mameti ||
sarvasyApi jantormama deha ityeva hi pramA pratItirna tu kasyApi deho.ahamiti | yadvA yasmAtsarveShAM mama deha ityeva pramA samyak.hpratItiH sa(rva)dAnuvartate tasmAddeho.ahamiti pratItirnAvakAshamAsAdayatIti | dehAtmatvapratItyabhAve.api dehadharmANAM kArShNyAdInAmAtmaniShThatvapratItistAvadastyeva kR^iShNo.ahamityAdivyavahArasandarshanAt.h | sA cha liN^gAdyanapekShaiva jAyamAnA pratyakShajanyaiva bAdhyate chAnumAnAdineti saivodAharaNaM bhaviShyatItyata Aha- upachArashcheti ||
kR^iShNo.ahamiti cha pratItirnAstItyanuvartate | kathaM tarhi vyavahAraH | kR^iShNo.ahamiti vyavahArastUpachAra eveti yojanA | asya yo vyavahArabalena tathAvidhAM pratItimapyanuminoti | tasyAnaikAntikatvaM syAdityAshayavAnuktArthe dR^iShyAntamAha- kardameti ||

yadi vastra ivAtmani dehopAdhikR^itaM kArShNyamastIti tatpratItiH sambhAvyate tadA pratyakShapratItasyAnumAnAdinA bAdha ityatra nedamudAharaNamiti sheShaH | kathamityata Aha- svata iti ||
atra dR^iShyAnte dArShyAntike chaikadeshotkIrtanenAnyadapyupalakShyate | tathA chAyamarthaH | vastre khalu kArShNyaM kardamopAdhikR^itaM (aupAdhikaM) pratIyamAnamevaM pratyetavyam.h | svatiH shuklamevedaM vastraM na kR^iShNam.h | kArShNyantUpAdhikR^itamiti | tathA.atrApi svato nIrUpa evAham.h | kArShNyaM tu na mama svabhAvataH | kintu dehopAdhikR^itamiti pratIyata ityaN^gIkartavyam.h | tathAchAsyAH pratIteryathArthatvAnnAnumAnAdinA(to) bAdha iti |

jAtA eva na tu vyApArAntaraM kR^itavantaH | bhujyata iti bhogaH sukham.h | Adipadena duHkham.h | siMhavyAghrAdIni bhayakAraNAni, mAtrAdInyabhayakAraNAni, stanapAnAdIni sukhakAraNAni, shaN^.hkvAdinA nayanAntaHkaNDUyanAdIni duHkhakAraNAnIti vijAnate | ata eva siMhAdidhvanimAtreNa palAyante, mAtrAdIni chopasarpanti, stanapAnAdyarthaM pravartante, varjayanti shaN^kukaNDUyanAdIni | tadvij~nAnaM bhayAdikAraNametaditi vij~nAnam.h | pUrvadehAsmaraNe tadvij~nAnaM(kR^ito) kathaM na bhavedityata Aha- anvayeti ||
Adipadena dR^iShyAntadharmiNorgrahaNam.h | yadvA.a.adigrahaNenopadesho gR^ihyate | anvayavyatirekAdervismR^itAviti sambandhaH | na kevalametAvat.h | kintu tathA chAyamityanusandhanasya cha vismR^itau satyAM vij~nAnaM tatkathaM bhavediti sambandhaH | 
etaduktaM bhavati | asti tAvanmR^igAdInAM stanapAnAdau pravR^ittiH shaN^kukaNDUyanAdito nivR^ittishcha | tato.anumIyate vidyete tatra teShAM rAgadveShAviti | rAgadveShayoreva pravR^ittikAraNatvenAsmadAdau nirNItatvAt.h | rAgadveShAbhyAM cheShyAniShyasAdhanatvaj~nAnam.h | tasyaiva rAgAdikAraNatayA nishchitatvAt.h | nacha tajj~nAnaM pratyakShasAdhyam.h | kAryakAraNabhAvasyAtIndriyatvAt.h | kintvanumAnopadeshasAdhyameva | nacha mR^igAdInAmupadeshaH sambhavati | anadhikArAt.h | tasmAtprAgbhavIyopadesha iti vAchyam.h | nachAsmR^ito.asau tatkAraNamiti tatsmR^itisadbhAvo.aN^gIkAryaH | yadvA.anumAnam.h | nacha tat.h, yadyatstanapAnaM tadiShyasAdhanaM, 
yadiShyasAdhanaM na bhavati tatstanapAnaM na bhavati, yathA.amukam.h, stanapAnaM chedamityanvayAdismaraNena vinA bhavati | nachAnanubhUte smR^itirutpadyate | nachAsmiJNjanmanyanvayAdyanubhavo.asti | jAtamAtrANAmudAhR^itatvAt.h | ato janmAntarAnubhUtAnvayAdismaraNameShyavyam.h | 
prAgbhavIyasyopadeshasyAnvayAdeshcha smaraNe pUvardehasmaraNamapyaN^gIkartavyam.h | samAnayogakShematvAt.h | nacheddehAntarasmaraNaM mR^igAdInAM tadA tadavishiShyAnvayayAdismaraNamapi na syAt.h | tadabhAve chAnumAnAdyabhAveneShyAniShyakAraNatAj~nAnaM notpadyeta | tadanutpAde cha rAgAdyanutpAdAtpravR^ittyAdyanutpa(dyata)dyate | kAraNAbhAve kAryAbhAvasya sulabhatvAt.h | adR^iShyavashAtpravR^ittyAdIti chenna | dR^iShyAtikramadoShAt.h | 
etAvAMstvadR^iShyasyopayogo yaJNjanmAntarAnubhUtaM sarvamasmarannetAvatsmarati | yAdR^ichChikaM pravR^ittyAdi bhavatviti chenna | anantAnAM tadanupapatteH | ata eva mR^igA ityAdibahuvachanam.h | astu jAtisvabhAvo.ayam.h | na | bhinnajAtIyAnAmapyupalambhAt.h | ata eva mR^igA gAva ityAdyuktam.h | dR^iShyAtikramadoShashchAparihAryaH |

tathA.api kiM prakR^ita ityata Aha- yadeti ||
yadaivametaddehavartino mama na kevalamayameva dehaH kintu tatprAganyo.apyabhUditi dehAntarasmaraNaM pramitam.h(NamApatitam.h) | tadaitaddehena svasyaikyA(dhya)vasAyaH kutaH syAt.h | kintvanekamaNiShvanusyUtaM sUtramivAnekadehAnusyUtamAtmAnaM pashyataH svasya tato.atyantabhedAvasitireva yuktA | tathAcha kArShNyAdInAmasaMsargaj~nAnamapi susthameve | pareNa dehAdyAropanibandhanatvAbhyupagamAttadAropasya | ahaMpratyayastu nAropa iti prAgevoktam.h | ato mama deha iti pratyayo nAnyathayitavyaH kR^iShNo.ahamityAdishchopachAro.aN^gIkaraNIya iti |

etena parakIyaM bAdhakathanaM nirastam.h | vyaktistirodhAnaM cha na j~nAyata ityato.adhikaraNadvayArthamupasaMharati- sR^iShTvaiveti ||

|| OM sa eva cha karmAnusmR^itishabdavidhibhyaH OM || kechidevaM vyAchakShate | suShuptau brahmasampanno ya eva jIvaShaH (kiM) sa evottiShThatyutAnyo.apIti saMshaye mahAjalanidhau kShiptasyodabindoriva brahmaNaikIbhUtasyoddharaNAsambhavAdaniyama iti prApte samAdhIyate | sa evottiShThati, yaH suptaH | kutaH | karmasheShasamApanAtpratyabhij~nAnAchChabdebhyo vidhibhyashcha | suptasya muktatvApattyA vidhyanupapatteriti | tadetadapavyAkhyAnamiti sUchanAyAdhikaraNatAtpayarmAha- nAnya iti ||
svapnAdInAM parameshvarakR^itatve.abhihite kiM deshakAlAntare.anyo.api kartA.astyuteshvara eveti saMshaye laukikeshvarANAM deshakAlavyavasthayaishvaryadarshanAdayamapi tathAvidha iti prApte | sa eveshvaro.asya svapnAdeH kartA natu deshakAlAntare.anyaH kashchanetyeSha evArtho.atra pratipAdyata iti | nahi yaH suptaH sa evottiShThatyanyo veti kasyachitsaMshayo.asti | nacha suptasya brahmaNaikyaM pramANadR^iShyamiShyaM vA parasyeti yatkiJNchidetat.h | lAghavArthaM kramollaN^ghanena vyAkhyAnamiti bo(ddhavya)dhyam.h | sUtrakR^itA cha svapnAdivanna mohaH svatantrAvastheti j~nApanAya vyavadhAnaM kR^itamiti |

|| atha sthAna(to.apya)bhedAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM na sthAnato.api parasyobhayaliN^gaM sarvatra hi OM || kechididamitthaM vyAchakShate | dvirUpaM brahma shrUyate sarvakarmA sarvakAma ityAdau savisheShamasthUlamanaNvityAdau nirvisheSham.h | tatra kimubhayarUpaM brahma pratipattavyamutAnyatararUpam.h | yadA.apyanyatararUpaM tadA(.api) kiM savisheShamuta nirvisheShamiti saMshaye dvividhashrutyanurodhAdubhayarUpameva brahmeti prApte idamuchyate | na tAvatsvata eva parasya brahmaNa ubhayarUpatvaM sambhavati virodhAt.h | astu tarhi sthAnataH pR^ithivyAdyupAdhiyogAt.h | maivam.h | na hyupAdhiranyadanyathAkaroti kintvavidyopasthApitAH pR^ithivyAdyupAdhayo bhramamupajanayanti | atashchAnyataraparigrahe.api nirastasamastavisheShameva brahma pratipattavyam.h | sarvatrAshabdamasparshamityAdivAkyeShu tathAbhUtameva hi brahmopadishyate | na bhedAditi chenna pratyekamatadvachanAt.h | na nirvisheShameva brahma | chatuShpAdbrahma ShoDashakalaM brahmetyAdau bhedenopadeshAditi chenna | yashchAyamasyAM pR^ithivyAmityAdinA pratyupAdhi bhedAbhAvavachanAt.h | api chaivameke | neha nAnA.asti kiJNchanetyAdau bhedadarshananindApUrvakamabhedameke shAkhinaH samAmanantIti |
tadidaM vyAkhyAnaM samyagvyAkhyAnenaivApahastitaM bhaviShyati kiM punaH prayatnenetyAshayavAnvyAkhyAnamevArabhate |

atra sthAnashabdastadbhedasyopalakShaNa ityuktaM bhavati | saptamyarthe tasiH | AdyAdibhya upasaN^khayAnAt.h |

OM na bhedAditi chenna pratyekamatadvachanAt.h OM || uktamarthamAkShipya samAdhAtuM sUtraM na bhedAditi | nirbhedaM sarvatra sarvadoShadUraM sakalaguNaparipUrNaM brahmeti nopapadyate | "kAryakAraNabaddhau tau' ityAdishrutipurANAdivAkyairbhinnatvadoShitvAlpaguNatvAderbhedashabdopalakShitasyoktatvAdityAkShepArthaH | neti parihArAMshaM vyAchaShye- tadviruddhaM tviti ||
yattu vAkyaM tasyoktArthasya viruddhaM pratIyate tattatra uktaviruddhe kvachidarthe mAnaM naiva bhavetkintvanya eva tasyArthaH pratipattavyaH | kuta ityataH pratyekamatadvachanAdityuktam.h | tadanupapannamivAbhAti | sarvatra hItyuktasya pratipakShachodanAyAM punastanmAtropanyAsasya vyarthatvAt.h | atastAtparyamAha- mahAtAtparyeti ||
sakalasmR^itItihAsapurANAnAM parameshvarasyAsheShadoShadUratve samastaguNaparipUrNatve cha yanmahAtAtparyaM tadvirodhena tat.h vAkyaM atra bhagavato doShitvAdau kathaM mAnaM bhavet.h | tushabdo mahAvAkyatvAvAntaravAkyatvalakShaNavisheShArthaH | dR^iShyaM hi nirNItamahAvAkyArthaviruddhasya tadavAntaravAkyasya tatrAprAmANyam.h | yathA svargaprayojanAgnihotraparamahAvAkyArthaviruddhasya yadyamuShminlloke.asti vA na vetyAdestadavAntaravAkyam.h | tadatharpratipattihetutvAt.h | 
syAdetat.h | yadi parameshvarasya sakalaguNaparipUrNatve nirastasamastadoShatve cha vedAdInAM mahAtAtparyamityarthaH pramANavAnsyAt.h | tadeva tu na pashyAma ityata Aha- duHkheti ||

tat.h duHkhApyayAdirUpaM kaivalyam.h | IshAnAt.h viShNoreva bhavennAnyasmAt.h | sa hi tasyeShye nAnyaH | astu tarhi sa eva viShayaH kiM guNapUrNatvAdinetyata uktaM prasannAdeva nAnyathA na j~nAtamAtrAditi |

viShNoH prasannatA cha tadIyaguNotkarShaj~nAnAdeva kevalaM nirdoShatAparij~nAnAchcha bhavati | hishabdaH pramANaprasiddhiM dyotayati | tachcha vakShyate | kevalashabdo.avadAraNArthaH | nAnyena kenachidityetatpratirUpeNAlpaguNatvAdij~nAnena karmAdinA vA netyarthaH | tathAcha mokShAdiprayojanena shAstreNa tatsAdhanabhUtaM bhagavadguNotkarShanirdoShatAj~nAnameva jIvAnAmutpAdanIyamityataH sakalaguNaparipUrNe nirastasamastadoShe nArAyaNa evAsheShashAstrasya mahAtAtparyamityavasIyate |

|| OM ata eva chopamA sUryakAdivat.h OM || iha parameshvare jIvasyAtyantikabhaktisiddhaye bhedAbhedamataM nirAkriyate | tathAhi | jIvabrahmaNorbhedastAvatsiddhAntinA.aN^gIkriyata eva | abhedastvanumAnataH siddhaH | jIvo brahmAbhinnashchetanatvAdbrahmavataH, brahmAMshatvAt.h | yo yadaMshaH sa tadabhinno yatheshvarAMshA matsyAdistadabhinna iti | ato bhinnAbhinnA brahmaNA jIva ityevaM prApte prativihitaM sUtrakR^itA sUryakAdivaditi sUtrakhaNDena | tadetad.hdR^iShyAntavachanamAtraM na kasyachidarthasya sAdhakaM bAdhakaM vetyataH pUvarpakShaniShedhapUrvakaM pratij~nAhetU darshayati- nacheti ||
chittvAdityaMshatvasyApyupalakShaNam.h | abhinnatvaM brahmaNeti sheShaH | Ishavat.h brahmavadIshvarAvatAravachcha | Apyate yujyate | asya jIvasya | asya brahmaNa AbhAsatAm.h | evetyavigAnenAlaM vispaShyam.h | etaduktaM bhavati | na chetanatvAdyanumAnena jIvasya brahmAbhedasAdhanaM yuktam.h | jIvo brahmAbhinno na bhavati tadAbhAsatvAdyo yadAbhAso nAsau tadabhinno yathAsUryakAdiH sUyarAdinetyanumAnavirodhAt.h | na chAsiddho heturvispaShyashrutisiddhatvAditi |

ChAyeva ChAyA | visheShakau garuDasheShau | tasya dhAtushChAye tayoH garuDasheShayoH | punastayorindrakAmayoH | harerbrahmA | abhAsa iti sarvatra sambandhaH | AbhAsatvavyAkhyAnaM tadadhInata iti | sarva ityanena sarveShAM parameshvarAbhAsatvamupapAdayati | chashabdo haristviti tushabdAtharH | AbhAsAtve kimityata uktam.h- chetanatve.apIti || atrApi tadaMsha(tvasyopa)tvopalakShaNam.h | tasmAt.h

idAnIM "ata eva chopamA' iti sUtrAvayavaM vyAkhyAtuM tannivartanIyAmAshaN^kAmAha- AbhAsatvaM hIti ||
yajjIvasya paramAtmana AbhAsatvaM shrutibalena nirNItaM tadyuktiviruddham.h | nahi niravakAshayuktiviruddho.arthaH shrutyApi pratipAdayituM shakyate | tathA satyabhimAnyadhikaraNAnArambhaprasaN^gAt.h | ataH sA kathaJNchidyojanIyeti | 
kathaM na yuktamityata Aha- yaditi ||
yasmAdAbhAsaH sUryakAdirjalAdyupAdhyAyatto j~nAyate | AbhAsatvasyopAdhyAyattatvaM vyApakatvena sarvatra nishchitamityarthaH | tathA.api kuto na yuktamityata Aha- upAdhIti || 
jIvAnAmiti sheShaH | vyApakasyopAdhyAyattatvasya jIveShvabhAvAdvayApyamapyAbhAsatvaM na yuktam.h | tato hetorasiddherduShyamanumAnam.h | itashcha duShyamityAha- AbhAsatveti ||
AbhAsatvasya bhinnatvena virodhatashchAnumAnaM duShyam.h | tathAhi | darpaNAdinA sannikR^iShyAH pratihatAH parAvR^ittA nAyanarashmayo mukhena sannikR^iShyAstadeva viShayIkurvanti | natu tato.anya AbhAso nAmAsti | tatra vyavachChedaH parAktvaM savyetaravyatyAsashchetyAdikaM bhrAntyaiva pratIyate | sopAdhikashchAyaM bhrama iti yAvadupAdhibhAvaM na nivartate | evaJNchAbhAsatvasyAbhedena vyAptatvAdbhedasAdhane viruddhatvamiti | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | tattvamasyAdishrutiviruddhatvena kAlAtItatvamapi draShyavyam.h | 
evamAbhAsatvAnumAne duShye kim.h iti chennirAbAdhena prAguktAnumAnadvayenaikyaM siddhamityAha- chetanatveneti ||
aMshatvAchchetyanvayaH | aikyaM cha sAdhyamAnaM na mAyAvAdinAmivetyuktam.h- samudAyeti ||

samudAyaikyAN^gIkArato yachChatyAdyuktaM pR^ithaktvaM tatsamudAyasya tadaMshasya cha jIvasya bhavet.h | samudAyasya yAvaMshau jIveshvarau tayorbhavediti vA | etaduktaM bhavati | yadi jIvasya brahmaNA.atyantAbhedaH sA(dhyeta)dhyate tadA bhedashrutaya uparudhyeran.h | mAyika(bheda)paratvAbhidhAne chApramANamApadyeran.h | | nachAyamasmAkamasti doShaH | jIvabrahmaNorjIveshvarayoshcha bhedasadbhAvena tadviShayatvopapatteriti | etena chetanatvAdyanumAnasyAbhAsoddhAraH kR^ito bhavati |
samudAyaikyamityuktam.h | tatkiJNchitprapaJNchayati- IshAkhyeti ||
Ishashabdo brahmaparaH | samudAye chetanAnAm.h | etaduktaM bhavati | brahmaikyameva svabhAvasiddhaM tattvaM tatparamArthabhUtaM mAyAsambandhAdIshvaratAmApadyate | sa cha sarvaj~naH sarveshvaro jagajjananAdikartA | jIvAstu brahmaNoM.ashAshchitsvabhAvA vahneriva viShphuliN^gA ata eva brahmaNo bhinnAbhinnAH | parasparamIshvarAchcha bhinnA eva | brahma tu sakalachetanasamudAyAtmakamatiriktaM cheti | atra dR^iShyAntamAha- Isheti ||
yathA bhagavadrUpANAM matsyAdInAM samudAye bhagavatsaMj~nA na sthAnato.apItyAdau siddhAntinoditA tathA | etenAtyantAbhedaM parityajya bhedAbhedAN^gIkAre shrutidvayamivAMshatvAnumAnaM choktaM bhavati | yadi matsyAdayaH parameshvarasyeva jIvA brahmaNoM.ashAH syustadA matsyAdInAmaishvaryAdivajjIvAnAM nirduHkhatvAdikaM syAt.h | aMsheShvaMshisAdharmyasyAvyabhichArAt.h |

ityapi vachanaM suduShkaraM syAt.h | pramANAbhAvena sandigdhatvAditi bhAvaH | kiJNcha muktAvanusandhAnaM bhaviShyatIti vadatA vaktavyamidAnIM kuto.anusandhAnaM nAstIti | atha brUyAdavidyAkAmakarmAdi(nimitta)pratibandhakasadbhAvAditi | tatra vaktavyam.h | pratibandhakasadbhAvanibandhana evedAnImanusandhAnAbhAvo na punaraikyAbhAvanibandhana iti kutaste nishchaya iti | vayaM tu vadAmaH | aikyAbhAvanibandhana evAyamidAnImanusandhAnAbhAvo nAj~nAnAdinimitta iti | kuto.ayaM nishchaya iti tatrAha- sarvaj~na iti ||

Ishvara evAsAviti chet.h | kastato.anyaH paramAtmA pramANAbhAvAt.h | kiJNcheshvaro.api sarvaj~na eveti kimaneneti | api chaikye pramANasiddhe.anusandhAnAbhAvaH pratibandhakanibandhana iti kalpanopapadyate | nacha tadastItyuktam.h | nanu cha duHkhAdikaM jIvasya na chaitanyasvarUpAnubandhi | kinnAma vishiShyAkAragatameva | tatkathamIshvaro.anusandhIteti duHkhAdyananusandhAne.apyaikyaM tAvadanusandadhyAdevetyuktam.h- ekatAmiti || ata eva "vibhedajanake.aj~nAne nAshamAtyantikaM gate | Atmano brahmaNA bhedamasantaM kaH kariShyati' ityAdivAkyAnyathA yojyAni | vibhedashabdo hi virodhavAchI | mitrabheda iti yathA | tathAcha jIvasya paramAtmanA viparItamatitvamaj~nAnanibandhanam.h | tadapAye na bhavatItyarthaH |

nanvavidyamAnaM vidyamAnatayA.anusandadhAno mithyAj~nAnI bhavati | na chaikyamavidyamAnam.h | tatkathaM paramAtmano mithyAj~nAnitvamityaviditAbhisandherAshaN^kAmabhisandhimuddhATayanpariharati- vidyamAneti ||
yadyaikyaM vidyamAnaM tarhi tadidAnImananusandadhadasarvaj~naH syAt.h | nacha tadyuktam.h | ato nAstyeva taditi vAchyam.h | tathAcha tadanusandhAsyAnkathaM mithyAj~nAnI na bhavet.h | eteneshvarasyedAnIM sharIrasadbhAvAdananusandhAnamityapi nirastam.h | sArvaj~nahAniprasaN^gAnistArAt.h | Ishvarasya sAkAratAyA nityatvena na bhAvinyapyanusandhAne pratyAshA | 
yadai(dyai)kyamavidyamAnameva yadi vA vidyamAnameva tadoktadoShadvayaM syAt.h | nachaivam.h | kintvidAnImasadeva pashchAjj~nAnottarakAle bhavet.h | tatredAnImasattvAnna paramAtmanastadananusandhAne sAvarj~nahAniH | pashchAdbhAvAchcha na tadanusandhAne mithyAj~nAnitvamiti parishiShyaM pakShaM kasyachinmataM vA shaN^kate- asaditi ||
pariharati- syAditi || tarhIti sheShaH | na hyanAdau saMsAre yasya yena naikyaM tattenaikIbhUtamupalabdham.h | nacha tathA bhaviShyatItyatra pramANamasti | "pare.avyaye sarva ekIbhavanti' "yAvanmokShaM tu bhedaH syAjjIvasya paramasya cha | tataH paraM na bhedo.asti bhedahetorabhAvataH' ityAdishrutismR^itInAM sthAnaikyAdiviShayatvena sAvakAshatvAt.h | ataH saptamo raso bhaviShyatItivadiyaM pratyAshA.atyantAsambhAvitaviShayeti bhAvaH |

tAratamyAbhAvasya na sthAnato.apItyuktatvAt.h | anyathA.a.akasmikatvaprasaN^gAditi | yadvA na brahmA(dyA)dInAmAnando bhagavadAnandapratibimbaH | parasparaM vibhinna(chitra)tvAt.h | bimbAbhimate cha vaichityAbhAvAditi | ato.atredaM vishadayati- pratibimbavaditi ||
yadyepyeShAM brahmAdInAmAnandaH pratibimbavat.h | prasiddhapratibimbaistulyaM vartate | bhagavadAnandapratibimbo bhavatIti yAvat.h | tathA.api parasparaM vichitro bhavatIti sheShaH | katham.h | anyeShAM sAdhanabhUtAnAmupAdhiguNAnAM bhaktyAdInAM vaichityAnatikrameNa | tatra dR^iShyAntaH pratibimbavaditi | yathA sUryAdipratibimbAnAM sUryakAntajalAdigatAyAM sUryAdibimbavaichityAbhAve.api sUryakAntAdisthAnaguNavaichityAdvaichityaM tathetyarthaH | 
vaichitye hetvantaramAha- nArAyaNeti ||
bimbashaktyA cha vichitra ityarthaH | sthAnaguNasya bimbasAmarthyasya cha prayojakatvaM nyAyavivaraNe vyutpAditam.h anenopapatteshcheti sUtraM vyAkhyAtaM bhavati | bimbapratibimbayoraikyaM kechidichChanti | ataH pratibimbatvaM vyAkhyA(taM)ti nArAyaNeti | guNa AnandaH | chashabdena tatsadR^ishashcheti grAhyam.h | bimbAbhinna eva kinna bhavatItyata Aha- atyalpa iti ||
cho hetau | yasmAttadapekShayA.atyalpastasmAtsatataM bhinna iti | tadapekShayA.atyalpatvaM kuta ityAkAN^kShAM pariharannatra shrutimAha- anyaditi ||
anya AnandaH parasya jIvAnAM cheti sambandhaH | evamIshatetyapi yojyam.h | mukhyeshatetyupalakShaNayA hetumAha | iti shruteriti pUrveNa sambandhaH | 
|| iti sthAnavisheShAdhikaraNam.h || JOSHI-19 
| atha shrImannyAsudhAyAM pAlakatvAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM prakR^itaitAvattvaM hi pratiShedhati tato bravIti cha bhUyaH OM || atra pUvarpakShapradarshanaparaM bhAShyaM "sR^iShyisaMhArakartR^itvamevAsya na pAlakatvam.h | svataH siddheriti | tadayuktam.h | sR^iShyisaMhArakartR^itvAbhyupagamasya vyarthatvAt.h | svataH siddherityatrAsyetyapratIteshcha | sthiterityadhyAhAre.api svabhAvavAdAshrayaNasya sR^iShyisaMhArayorapi sAmyena tatkartR^itvAbhyupagamAnupapatterityataH pUrvapakShaM vishadayati- sR^iShyIti ||
iti Irite siddhAntinA.abhyupagate sati | tatashchAyamarthaH | Ishvarasya pAlakatvaM nopapadyate sthitestatprayojanatvAt.h | tasyAshcha svabhAvasiddhatveneshvarAnapekShatvAt.h | Ishvara eva hi vishvasya sR^iShyisaMhArayoH kartA nAnya ityabhyupagatam.h | tathAcha sR^iShTvA yAvanna saMharettAvatsthitiH svabhAvasiddhaiva na paravyApAramapekShate | yadi khalu sR^iShyisaMhArayoH katarA.anyaH syAttadodAsInasya tasya sR^iShyau preraNAdyarthaM saMhAre pravR^ittasya nivAraNArthaM cha sthitAvIshvarApekShA sambhavet.h | nacha tadasti | ataH saMhArodAsInatvAtiriktaM pAlakatvaM nopapadyata ityevamatra pUrvapakSha iti |
evaM tarhi siddhAnto na yuktaH | svabhAvattvayukteraparihR^itatvAdityataH sUtrAbhiprAyamAha- iti neti ||
parAnapekShatayA pratIyamAnaM svarUpaM dharmo vA svabhAva ityuchyate | sa sarveShAM padArthAnAm.h | (sa) sarvo.apIshAyatta eva | anyathA teShAM svAtantyaprasaN^genAsyeshatvAnupapatteH | sarvaM khalvityAdishrutivirodhApatteshcha | annadAnAdau vyApArashcha sphuTa eveti | 
|| iti pAlakatvAdhikaraNam.h |
|| atha avyaktAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM tadavyaktamAha hi OM || atra paramAtmano.avyaktatvamAdau vistareNa samarthitam.h | tatastarhi bhaktyAdisAdhanavaiyarthyamityAshaN^kaya "prakAshashcha karmaNyabhAsAt.h' iti dR^ishyatvaM choktam.h | tadetadubhayaM viruddhamityAshaN^kaya ato.anantena tathA hi liN^gamiti sUtritam.h | atra virodhashAntirna sphuTA pratIyata ityatastasya tAtparyamAha- avyakto.apIti ||
|| iti avyaktAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| atha ubhayavyapadeshAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM ubhayavyapadeshAttvahikuNDalavat.h OM || yadIshvarasya guNakriyAdayo dhamarAstato bhinnAstadA samavAyasya nirAkR^itatvAttadvattvamanupapannam.h | yadi chAbhinnAstadA j~nAnAdimattvamAnandAdibhoktR^itvamityAdyayuktamityubhayathA tatra bhaktyanupapattiriti pUrvapakShaprAptAvidamArabhyate | tatra hetudR^iShyAntAveva sUchitau | natu pakShaparigraharUpA pratij~nA | adhyAhAro.api hetudR^iShyAntabalena bhedAbhedapakShaparigrahasyeti pratibhAti | ataH pratij~nAM darshayati- tadabhinnA iti ||
nityashabdo niyamArthaH | pArameshvarAH sarve guNA dharmA nityaM tadabhinnAstenAtyantAbhinnastathA.api visheShashaktyA guNaguNyAdibhAvena sthitAH | 
syAdetat.h | parimANAdInAM yAvaddravyabhAvinAM bhavatu nAma bhagavatA.atyantAbhedaH | kriyANAM (j~nAnAdi)guNAnAM chAsrAkShItsR^ijati srakShyati vyaj~nAsIjjAnAti j~nAsyatItyAdi shrautavyavahArairanityatayA.avagatAnAM tu na yujyata ityata Aha- visheShAtmatayeti ||
teShAM parameshvarasambandhinyAM kriyAdInAM dharmANAM nityashaktyAtmanA nityaM sthitestathA visheShAtmatayA vyaktirUpeNa vyavahAraviShayatopapatternAnityateti yojanA | prapaJNchastu prAgeva kR^itaH | nanu cha kriyAdInAM yA vyaktatA sA tAvadanityaiva | anyathoktavyavahArANAM nirAlambanatvApAtAt.h | tatastasyA bhagavaddharmabhUtAyA api nAtyantAbhedopapattirityata Aha- na visheSheti ||
iyaM vyavahArAlambanatvenoktA | kuta ityata Aha- shaktIti ||
yadyasmAtsA visheShatmatA shaktirUpataiva | shaktishcha nityetyuktaM tasmAdityarthaH | nanvevaM tarhi shaktirvyaktirita vyavahAravisheSho na syAt.h | uktavyavahArANAM nirAlambanatvaM cha na parihR^itaM syAdityata Aha- savisheSheti ||
neyaM vyaktiH shaktyA nirvisheShAbhinnA | yenoktadoShaH syAt.h | kintu savisheShAbhinnaiva | yadyayaM sarvanirvAhaheturvisheSho bhagavato bhinnastadA sarveShAM taddharmANAM tenAtyantAbheda iti pratij~nA bhajyeta | abhinnashchedvisheShatA tasya na syAt.h | svarupamAtraparyavasAnena so.api na syAdityata Aha- visheSha iti ||
cho.avadhAraNe | ayaM visheSho.api bhagavatA naiva bhinnastena na pratij~nAhAniH | tathA.api tasya visheShatA syAt.h | katham.h | na hyayamabhinno bhavannirvisheShaH | evaM tarhi visheShaparamparayA.anavasthA syAt.h | na syAt.h | kutaH visheShasya svanirvAhakatAhetoriti |
evaM pratij~nA darshitA | tatra bAdhakAni parihR^itAni | atra choktvA | syAdevam.h | yadyeteShvartheShu pramANaM syAt.h | nacha tatpashyAma ityataH sautramubhayavyapadeshAditi hetuM vyAchaShye- visheShatveneti ||
akhilaiH ubhayavidhaiH pramANaiH vedavAkyaij~narAnAdidharmANAM bhagavadvisheShatvenApishabdAttadabhinnatvena cha vij~nAtervij~nAnAdityarthaH | nanu vij~nAteriti katham.h | "Atashchopasarge' ityaN^aH ktinbAdhakatvAt.h | "ktinnAbAdibhyashcha' iti vachanAdbhaviShyati | etadeva vivR^iNoti- sasarjeti ||
"sa idaM sarvamasR^ijate' ityAdishrutiM sasarjetyanenopAdatte | tattadattumadhriyate' ityAdikAM saJNjahAretyanena, sa AnandAdiH saH paramAtmaivetyanena "Anando brahma' ityAdishrutim.h | 
tadayamarthaH | "sa idaM sarvamasR^ijata, ukShA sa dyAvApR^ithivI bibharti, tattadattumadhriyata, sa aikShata so.akAmayata, Anandam.h brahmaNo vidvAn.h' ityAdishrutyA sarjanAdikaM brahmaNo visheSho.atishayo na brahmamAtramityavagamyate | tanmAtratve kriyAkartR^ibhAvAderanupapatteH | "Anando brahmeti vyajAnAt.h | satyaM j~nAnamanantaM brahma ekadhaivAnudraShyavyam.h' ityAdishrutyaiva tasya tenAbhedashchAvagamyate | tadevamubhayavyapadeshAnyathA.anupapattyA sakalamidaM kalpyate | sarveShAM brahmadharmANAM brahmaNA savisheSho.atyantAbhedaH | kriyAdInAM nityatA shaktivyaktirUpatA vyaktirUpasyApi nityatA shaktirUpapAbhinnatA savisheShatA visheShasyApyabhedaH svanirvAhakatA cheti | na hyeteShvartheShvanyatamasyApyakalpanAyAmudAhR^itobhayavyapadeshavirodhashAntirbhavatIti | etadeva prapaJNchayituM "nidarshanamAtreNa' ityataH prAktano granthasandarbhaH | 
atha matam.h | bheda eva brahmadharmANAM brahmaNA.astu | samavAyena visheShaNavisheShyabhAvo bhaviShyati | samavAyadUShaNAni cha shrutivirodhenAbhAsatAM yAsyanti | samavAyAbhAve.api vA dharmadharmiNoreva sa ko.api mahimA kalpyate | nachAbhedashrutivirodhaH | anAgantakatvenopachAropapatteH | ataH kimabhedamAdAya visheShAdyaN^gIkAreNeti | apara Aha akhaNDameva brahma na tu tatra kashchidvisheShaH | na chAparashrutivirodhaH | kriyAdiviShayANAM saguNaviShayatvAt.h | tasya cha mAyAmayatvenAvichAritaramaNIyatvAt.h | AnandaM ityAdInAM cha rAhoH shira ityAdivadupacharitatvopapatteriti | anyastvAha bhedAbhedAbhyAmevobhayavyapadeshasAmaJNjasyopapatteH kimanayA savisheShAbhedakalpanayeti |
maivam.h | tribhirapyetairantato.abhinne visheShasyAN^gIkatarvyatvAt.h | tato varamAdita eva tadaN^gIkaraNamityAshayavAnbhedavAdinaM tAvadvisheShamaN^gIkArayitumAha- bheda iti ||
visheShasya j~nAnAderbrahmadharmasya, yadi brahmaNo bhedo.aN^gIkriyate tadA pR^ichChAmaH | sa bhedo, bhedinA brahmaNA j~nAnAdinA cha saha, kathaM kiM prakAraH, pratipattavyaH | kiM bhinnaH kiMvA.abhinna iti | Adye doShamAha- bhinnashchediti ||
yadi bhedo bhedibhyAM bhinnastadA so.api bhedastathetyanavasthA syAt.h | visheShaNavisheShyabhAvAdipratipattaye khalu dharmadharmiNorbhedo.abhyupagamyate | sa cha pratIyamAna eva taddhetuH | tatpratItishcha visheShaNAdibhAvenaivetyuttarottarabhedapratItiravashyamapekShitaiveti susthA.anavasthA | 
abhinnatve.api vaktavyaM savisheShAbhinna uta nirvisheShAbhinna iti |
prathame doShamAha- abhinnashchediti ||
purA na kimiti | dhamarANAM dharmiNA savisheShAbhedaH kinnAN^gIkriyate.aN^gIkArya evetyarthaH | bheda iva vinA.api bhedena visheSheNaivopapattAvapi vR^ithA paramparAkalpanAyAM gauravaM syAttato dharmANAmeva savisheShAbhedAN^gIkAraH shreyAniti bhAvaH | astvevamityata Aha- visheSha iti || visheSho dharmobhinna ityeva tAvat.h | tena bhedavAdinA nAbhyupagamyate | dUre savisheShatvamityato.apasiddhAntaH syAt.h | samIhitaM cha naH (na) siddhayedityAshayaH | 
dvitIyaM dUShayati- abhinna iti ||
bhedo yadi bhedibhyAmabhinno nirvisheShashcha syAttadA tasya tadbhedatA tayorayaM bheda ityevambhAvaH kuto na kuto.api | tadIyatAyA bhedena visheShaNa vA vinA.anupapatteH | tanmAtratve cha dharmadharmiNAveva sto na bheda iti syAt.h | tathA cha dharmadharmiNAvityapi na syAt.h | bheda evAsti na dharmadharmiNAviti vA bhavet.h | tatashcha bhedo.api na syAditi |
bhedasya bhedisvarUpatvamaN^gIkR^itya visheShamanaN^gIkuvarANaM prati dUShaNAntaramAha- aneneti ||
bhinno.ayaM ghaTa iti sa bheda eva visheShato visheShaNatvena dR^ishyate na tu ghaTaH, kintu visheShyatvena | tathA.anenAnena | vyatyayo bahulamiti paJNchamyarthe tR^itIyA | sahayoge vA | paTAdbhinnastambhAdbhinno ghaTa ityeSha bheda eva savisheShaH pratiyogivisheShasAhityena dR^ishyate | tathA.ayaM padArtho.anena vakratvenAnena koTaravattvena puruShAdbhinna iti sa eSha bheda eva visheShato vyAvartakadharmeNa dR^ishyate | padArthastvakShasannikarShamAtreNa | tathA.asmAtpaTAdasmAtstambhAdasmAtkuDyAdbhinno.ayaM ghaTa ityeSha bheda eva savisheShataH pratiyogivisheShasAhityena nimittena bahudhA dR^ishyate | ghaTastvekadhaiva | ato na bhedo ghaTasya svarUpamiti yatsvarUpabhedasya dUShaNaM parairuchyate | tattasya kimuttaraM tvayA.abhidhAsyate, yadi visheSho nAN^gIkriyate, ityarthaH | yadi visheSho nAN^gIkriyate tadA bhedo bhedinA.abhinna ityapi nAN^gIkartuM shakyate | bhedabhedinorbhedasAdhakAnAmanekeShAM bhAvAt.h | visheShaNaiva hi teShAmanyathAsiddhiM vyutpAdya pratItibalena bhedasya bhedinA.abhedo vaktavyo nAnyatheti bhAvaH | 
tadIyatvena visheShaNatvena sapratiyogitvena liN^gitvena bahutvena cha pratIyamAno.anyonyAbhAvAdirUpo bhedo na bhedisvarUpatayA.aN^gIkriyate | yastu svarUpatayA.aN^gIkriyate nAsau tadIyatvAdinA pratIyata iti tasyottaraM brUma iti chenna | asyaiva prasiddhatvAdanyasya tadabhAvAt.h | anyathA svarUpasyaiva bheda iti pAribhAShikaM nAmAntaramuktaM syAt.h | na chAdvaitavAdinaH svarUpaM nAN^gIkurvate | tatkimanena bhedena | tadidamuktaM sa eSha iti prasiddhidyotakAbhyAm.h | tadIyatvAdirupachAra iti chenna | pratIteH sphuTatvAt.h | bAdhakAbhAvenAbhrAntitvAchcha | tadidamapyuktaM dR^ishyata iti |
dUShaNAntaramAha- abhedeti || 
na kevalaM bhedasya | kintvabhedasya cha bhedinaH svarUpatvameveti yojanA | yo bhedasya bhedinA ghaTenAbhedamaN^gIkaroti | tena tasyAbhedasyApi ghaTasvarUpatvamevAN^gIkaraNIyam.h | bhedasamAnanyAyatvAditi hishabdArthaH | tataH kimityata Aha- tayorapIti ||
abhedo.aN^gIkArya iti sheShaH | astvekena ghaTenAtyantAbhinnayorabhedabhedayorabhedastato.api kimityata Aha- avisheShatva iti ||
abhedabhedayoratyantAbhede visheShe chAsatyabhedAbhedashabdayoH paryAyatvaM syAt.h | ekAtharvAchitvAdghaTakalashashabdAditi hishabdArthaH | astvityata Aha- abhedeti || 
ko vadet.h na ko.api | pratyutAparyAyAvityeva vadati sarva ityaprAmANikaM pramANaviruddhaM chaitaditi |
etaduktaM bhavati | bhedo bhedinA.abhinnastannyAyena so.abhedo.api tatastAvanyonyamapyabhinnAviti tAvattvam.h | tathAcha bhedAbhedashabdayoH paryAyatvaprAptau visheShabalenaiva hi tatpariharaNIyam.h | tasya chAnaN^gIkAre duShpariharaM tadApadyeteti |
nanu bhedabhedishabdayorapi paryAyatvamApAdayitumuchitam.h | satyam.h | shiShyairUhyatAmiti noktam.h | 
shaN^kate- bheda iti ||
yadyapi bhedAbhedayoH bhedinA ghaTena sahAbhedastathA.api tayoranyonyaM bhedo.astIti na tachChabdayoH paryAyatvaM prasajyate | tatkiM visheShaNeti | pariharati- visheShiteti ||
evamaN^gIkurvANenApyabhinne vastuni visheShitA.aN^gIkaraNIyaivetyarthaH | tatkathamityata Aha- avisheSha iti ||
visheShAbhAve bhedo bhedinA eko.abhinnastathA.abhidA bhedinA ghaTenAbhinnA, punastayorbhedAbhedayoH parasparaM kathamupapannaM bhavet.h | kuto na bhavet.h | bhedAbhedayorbhedimAtratvataH | anyathA ghaTasyApi svato bhedaH syAt.h | ghaTenAbhinnayorbhedAbhedayoH parasparaM bheda(kArya)nirvAhArthaM ghaTena savisheSha evAbhedo.aN^gIkArya iti bhAvaH | 
shaN^kate- bhedinashcheti ||
chashabdAvanyonyasamuchchayArthau | evashabdau parasparaM savisheShAbhedavyAvR^ittyarthau | gamyate.abhyupagamyate | bhedasya bhedinashcha ghaTasyAbhedo visheShashcha mayA.abhyupagamyate | tathA.abhedasyAbhedinashcha tasya savisheSho.abhedo.abhyupagamyate | tathAcha bhedAbhedayorghaTatanmAtratvAbhAvena parasparaM bhedopapatterna shabdayoH paryAyatvam.h | tatashcha bhedAbhedayoH parasparamabhedo visheShashchAN^gIkAyar ityasaditi bhAvaH | 
evamapi dharmadharmiNorbhedamabhyupagachChatA.antato.abhinne vastuni visheSho.aN^gIrktavya ityabhimataM yadyapi siddhameva, tathA.apyuktaM tattvaM na parityAjyamityAshayavAnpariharati- kimiti ||
evaJNchedabhedabhedayorbhedaH kasmAtkalpyate | tayorapi savisheShAbheda evAN^gIkartavyaH | tatropapattimAha- visheShaNaiveti ||
sarvatra bhedabhedinorabhedAbhedinoshchAbhede.api visheSheNaiva tanmAtratAbhAvanibandhanA vyAvahR^itirbhavedityaN^gIkR^itaM chedbhedAbhedayostarhi bhedaH kiM kalpanAgauravAyaiva kalpyata iti solluNThavachanam.h | bhedAbhedayorghaTeneva parasparamapi savisheShatvenaiva sarvasyopapattau bhedakalpane kalpanAgauravaM syAt.h | anekapadArthakalpanAt.h dvidhA kalpanAchcheti bhAvaH | 
astvevaM tataH kimAyAtaM prakR^ita ityata Aha- visheSheNaiveti || bhedasya bhedinA.abhede.api tadIyatvAdivyavahR^itirbhedAbhedayo(shcha)rghaTenAbhede.apyaparyAyashabdavyavahR^itiryadi visheSheNaiva bhavet.h tadA dharmadhamirNorapi bhedaH kiM kalpanAgauravAyaiva kalpyate | dharmadhamirNorbhedamaN^gIkR^ityApyantato visheSho.aN^gIkAryaH tato varamAdita eva tadaN^gIkaraNam.h | anyathA kalpanAgauravaprasaN^gAditi | etena purA na kimitivivR^itaM bhavati | 
yadi kalpanAgauravabhayAddharmadharmiNorabhedamaN^gIkR^itya vyavahAravisheShArthaM visheSho.aN^gIkriyate | tarhi gavAshvayorapi tathA kalpyatAm.h | avisheShAt.h | tathAcha bheda eva jagati na syAdityata Aha- aikyeti |
bheda eva svIkriyate na visheShaH | gavashvayoriti pramAdapAThaH | mUlakosheShvadarshanAt.h | aikyapratItyabhAve.api kuto visheSho nAN^gIkriyata ityata Aha- sa eveti ||
dharmadharmipratibandyA hi gavAshvayovirsheShaH pareNApAdanIyaH | nacha tatrAvisheShaH | abhedapratItyA tatra tadaN^gIkArAt.h | iha cha tadabhAvAt.h | bhedasya pratItisiddhatvena kalpanA(gauravAbhAvAchcheti)bhAvAditi |
adhunA.abhedavAdinA.api visheShamaN^gIkArayati- sachchidAderiti ||
mAyinApIti | kriyAdiviShayANAM vAkyAnAM mAyikaviShayatAmaN^gIkurvatA.apIti yAvat.h | tatra hetuH sachchidAdeH padasamUhasya aparyAyatvasiddhayarthamiti | ayamiti aparyAyashabdapravR^ittihetuH | visheShasya tathAbhAvaH pramita iti hishabdaH | etaduktaM bhavati | santu tAvatkriyAdiviShayANi vAkyAnyasatyaviShayANi | tathA.api "satyaM j~nAnamanantaM brahma' ityAdIni tAvatsatyaviShayANi pareNAN^gIkR^itAnyeva | teShAM chAkhaNDArthaniShThatve satyaj~nAnAdipadAnAmekArthatvena paryAyatvaM syAt.h | nacha tadyuktaM sahaprayogadarshanAt.h | nacha bhedo.aN^gIkartuM shakyaH | ekamevAdvitIyamityAdishrutivirodhAt.h | ataH satye.api visheSho.aN^gIkAryaH | tasyAparyAyashabdapravR^ittihetutA chAnayaivArthApattyA siddhA | tathAtvenaiva tatkalpanAditi |
apohavAdAshrayeNa shaN^kate- yadIti ||
satyAdipadAnAM vidhivAchitve vidhIyamAnAnAM satyatvAdivisheShaNAnAM brahmaNyabhAvAt.h svarUpamAtrasya chaikatvAtparyAyatvaM syAt.h | na chaivam.h asatyatvAdyapohavAchitvAt.h | nachaivaM sati vaiyarthyam.h | brahmaNyasatyatvAdInAM visheShaNAnAM bhrAntikalpitatvena tannivAraNArthatvAt.h | santi hi nAsti brahma, sadapi na j~nAnaM parichChinnaM (che)vetyAdipratItayaH prANinAm.h | nacha satyapadamaj~nAnasyApyapohaM vakti yenaikenaivAlamiti syAt.h | tasmAnna paryAyatvaM vaiyarthyaM cheti | yadvA satyAdipadAni satyatvAdipR^ithagarthavAchInyeveti na paryAyatAmApadyante | brahmaNi tu lakShaNayA pravartanta iti na tatra visheShaNAni samarpayanti | nahi gaN^gApadaM tIre gaN^gAtvamarpayati | nachaivamekenaiva lakShitatvAditareShAM vaiyarthyamiti vAchyam.h | AropitAnAmasatyatvAdivisheShaNAnAM pratyektaM nivAraNena sArthakyAt.h | nacha saN^gatigrahaNaviShayAbhAvAllakShaNAnupapattiH | shabale gR^ihItasaN^gatikAnAM

shaN^kate- sA cheti ||

vAkyArthasyeti sheShaH | evaM tarhi na ko.api vAkyArtho vyavasthitaH syAt.h | satyatvAdivisheShavattayA.asatyatvAdivyAvR^ittimattayA chApratipAditatvAt.h | nahi saMsargabhedau vihAya vAkyAtharo.asti | brahmaiva vAkyArtha iti chenna | tasya svaprakAshatvAt.h | vyAvR^itteshchAsatyatvAditi |
yadvA pratItA sA cha svAbhAvavyAvartakatvenaiva vyavatiShThate na brahmaviShayatvena | yenAkhaNDatA vyAhanyata iti shaN^kArthaH | evamapi tadabhAvavyAvR^ittirUpavisheShaNavishiShyatAyA aparihArAdakhaNDatvahAnireva | sA.api tathA chet.h anavasthitiH brahmaj~nAnasyAvyavasthaiveti parihArAtharH | na kevalaM brahmaNo nirvisheShatve padAnAM paunaruktyAdi(kaM) kinnAmaikasyApi padasya tatra pravR^ittirna bhavedityAha- yadIti ||
guNakarmAdinimittamanAlambya kasyApi shabdasya pravR^ittyabhAvAditi bhAvaH | shaN^kate- lakShyate cheteneti ||
syAdayaM doSho yadi brahma shabdAbhidheyaM syAt.h | nachaivam.h | kintu tena shabdena lakShyata eva | nahi lakShaNA guNakriyAdyapekShA | tathAtve khalvabhidhaiva syAditi | pariharati- lakShyamiti ||
evamaN^gIkAre.api brahmaNo lakShyamiti visheShitA syAt.h | lakShyatvaM tAvadaparihAyarmityarthaH | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | mukhyArthayogAdinA.api visheShitA syAdeva | nanu lakShyatvamapi brahmaNo nAstyeva lakShyamityapi lakShaNayaivochyate nAbhidhAnavR^ittyeti chenna | atrApi vAkye pareNa lakShyapadasya prayogAllakShyatvavisheShaprApteH | tenApi lakShyameveti chettatrAha- punariti ||
