te mate iti sheShaH | tR^itIyArthe.avyayaM vA | yaduktaM mAyAvisheSharAhityavisheShaNavisheShitA satyasyApi bhavediti | tannAniShyam.h | abhAvarUpavisheShavattvasya mayA.aN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | "neha nAnA.asti' iti shrutiH "iha bhUtale ghaTo nAsti' itivadabhAvaM brahmaNyaN^gIkarotyeva | yachchoktaM na taduktirbhavettadeti | tadapyasat.h | bhAvanimittAbhAve.apyabhAvanimittena padapravR^ittyupapatteH | abhAvadharmavattvasya chAN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | etena lakShyamityetadapi nirastam.h | lakShyapadasyApyapohavAchitvopapatteriti bhAvaH | 
atra vaktavyaM paramasiddhAntamakhaNDatvaM parityajyAbhAvadharmavattvaM kasmAdaN^gIkaroShIti | atha brUyAt.h | satyaM j~nAnamanantaM vij~nAnamAnandamityAdipadAni tAvadbrahmaNi shrUyante | nacha teShAM vidhirUpo.arthaH svIkartuM shakyaH | neha nAnA.astItyAdishrutivirodhAt.h | abhAvadharmAN^gIkAre cha na virodha ityuktamiti | tatrAha- asArvaj~nAdIti ||
te aN^gIkAryamiti sheShaH | yathA hi satyaj~nAnAdipadAni brahmaNi shrUyante, evameSha sarvaj~naH, eSha sarveshvaraH, iti sArvaj~nAdipadAnyapi | tathAcha yathA tAnyanR^itatvAdyabhAvavAchInyevametAnyapi asarvaj~natvAdyabhAvavAchitayA (tvayA) aN^gIkartavyAnyeva | tatashcha satyaj~nAnAdivAkyaM tattvAvedakaM sArvaj~nAdivAkyaM mAyAshabalaparamiti vibhAgo na yukta iti bhAvaH | 
mA bhUdayaM vibhAgo.asArvaj~nAdyabhAvo.api brahmaNyaN^gIkriyata evetyata Aha- tadeti || 
brahmaNyasArvaj~nAdyabhAve.aN^gIkR^ite (sati) sAvarj~nAdibhAvadharmA durnivArA eva | kutaH | dvau naJNau prakR^itamarthaM sAtishayaM gamayata iti nyAyAdityarthaH | etachcha chaturthe spaShyayiShyate | 
asArvaj~nAdirAhityamapyevaM te bhaviShyatItyuktAnaN^gIkAre bAdhakamAha- yadIti ||

yasmAdevamakhaNDavAdibhyAM visheSho.aN^gIkAryastattasmAdeva hi khaNDAkhaDena khaNDAkhaNDavAdinA cha visheSho.aN^gIkArya eva | kuntAH pravishantItivadupalakShaNayA arshaAdibhyo.ajiti vA khaNDAkhaNDeneti sAdhu | tathAhi | dharmadharmiNorbhedAbhedAviti vadatA tau kiM tAbhyAmatyantaM bhinnAvaN^gIkriyete utAtyantAbhinnAvatha bhinnAbhinnau | nAdyaH | bhedAnavasthApatteH | bhedasya svarUpatve cha visheShAnaN^gIkAre tadIyatvAdyanupapatteH | bhedAbhedayoratyantabhinnayoH sambandhAbhAvena tadIyatvAnupapatteshcha | na dvitIyaH | tadIyatvAdyanupapatteshcha | bhedAbhedashabdayoH paryAyatvApatteshcha | na tR^itIyaH | anavasthApatteH | kvachidbhedAbhedayorabhede pUrvadoShAnuShaN^gAt.h | tasmAdbhedAbhedavAdinA.api kvachidvisheSho.aN^gIkArya iti |
tadevamubhayavyapadeshAnyathA.anupapattyA bhagavaddharmANAM savisheSho.atyantAbheda eveti siddham.h |

yata evamarthApattyA bhagavadguNAnAM bhagavatA savisheSho.atyantAbhedaH siddho.atra ityarthaH | atyabhinnatAM savisheShAm.h | niravakAshapramANAnusAreNa nidarshanatrayamapi savisheShAbhedopayuktatvena sUtrakArasyAbhimataM j~nAtavyamityAshayaH | tatrAhikuNDalaM yadyapi bhedAbhedavattathA.api mandAnAmabhede buddhimavatArayitumupAttam.h | yathA pR^ithivyAmoShadhayaH sambhavantIti yathA | prakAshashabdena cha bhAsvaraM rUpaM vivakShitam.h | tachcha yAvadravyabhAvitvAtsUryamaNDalenAtyantAbhinnameva | pUrvatvaM cha pUrvakAlasambandha iti sakalalokasiddhamiti | nanvekenaiva nidarshanenAlaM kiM trayeNetyata uktam.h- AdareNeti ||
evaM sAkShAdadhikaraNAtharM vyAkhyAyedAnImanuShaN^gasiddhamarthaM darshayati- tachcheti ||

yadAshabdo yadyarthaH | yadyapyasheShavisheShANAmityasheShavisheShAnvitasyetyarthaH | ekashabdo mukhyArthaH | padeShvekaM padaikamA(dye na)dyapadenetyarthaH | karmadhArayatve tu pUrvakAlaiketyekapadasya pUrvanipAtaH syAt.h | ApaM tathA.api | uttareNa padajAtenAnvayavisheShAvagatiH |
etaduktaM bhavati | satyaM j~nAnamanantaM brahma yaH sarvaj~naH sarvavidityAdibrahmapratipAdakavAkyagatAni sakalAnyapi padAnyanvitArthAbhidhAyIni | tatra brahmapadaM satyatvasarvaj~natvAdyasheShavisheShAnvitaM brahma pratipAdayati | nachaivaM satyAdipadAnAM vaiyarthyam.h | yataH sAmAnyata evAnvitAbhidhAne shaktiH padAnAM nAnvayavisheShAbhidhAne | ato brahmapadena sAmAnyataH samastayogyadharmAnvite brahmaNi pratIte satyatvenAnvitaM j~nAnatvenAnvitamiti visheShAnvayapratipattyarthAni satyAdipadAnIti |
nanvabhihitAnvayAdivAdAnAmanupapannatvamanvitAbhidhAnasyopapannatvaM cha prathamasUtre sUtrakAreNoktameva | tatkimatrAdhikaraNasiddhAntatayA tadvarNanena | uchyate | ataHshabdena hyanvayabodhe.astyupAya ityetAvanmAtraM pratIyate | na punaH padAnyeva na padAbhihitArthAdInIti visheShaH | tatra vyAkhyAtAraM prati kuto.ayaM sUtrakR^ito.abhiprAya iti bhavatyeva parichodanA | tatsamAdhAnAya chAdhikaraNasiddhAntavarNanamupapannameva | yadyapyupapannaH sUtrakArAbhiprAya iti shakyate vaktum.h | tathA.apyadhikaraNasiddhAntavarNanamiSheNa tatra saMkShepato vyutpAditopapattInAM prapaJNchAya prayatno.ayamityadoShaH |
taditi parAmR^iShyaM hetuM darshayati- yata iti ||
vastunA brahmaNA | chashabdAdvisheShashcha | ato nAbhihitAnvayAdivAdAH kinnAmoktavidhAnvitAbhidhAnamiti sheShaH | tathAhi | satyatvAdidharmANAM tAvadbrahmaNA.atyantAbhedaH samarthitaH | tato brahmavAchakasya brahmapadasya satyatvAdivAchakatvamAvashyakameva | kintvabhede.anvaya eva nAsti kutastadabhidhAnaM visheShato.abhidhAnaprasaN^gashchetyavashiShyate | tatra savisheShatvAN^gIkAra eva samAdhiH | abhede.api visheShashaktyA.anvitatvasya visheShAnabhidAnasya chopapattiriti |
syAdetat.h | asminnanvitAbhidhAnavAde visheShAnvayapratipattirnirnibandhanaivApadyate | sakalapadAnAM sAmAnyato.anvitAbhidhAne sAmarthyAt.h | nachAdyaM padaM sAmAnyato.anvitAbhidhAyyuttaraM tu visheShata iti vAchyam.h | AdyatvAderavyavasthitatvAt.h | vedavAkye.api hi kvachidbrahmapadamAdyaM kvachiduttaramityata Aha- sAmAnyata iti ||

savisheShAbhedasamarthanenoktaprakAraM padAnAmanvitAbhidhAnaM siddhamityayuktam.h | atiprasaN^gAt.h | rUpasya hi ghaTenAbheda iti tvachA tasmingR^ihIte tadapi gR^ihyeta | athAvisheSheNa pratibaddhaM tadgrahaNamityuchyate | tarhyatrApi pratibandhaH syAt.h | visheShAbhidhAnaM pratibaddhameveti chet.h | sAmAnyAbhidhAnamapi kuto na pratibaddham.h | atha sambhAvanaivaiShokteti mataM tadA nAyamadhikaraNasiddhAntaH | ekasya siddhAvanuShaN^gI yo.arthaH siddhayati so.adhikaraNasiddhAnto na hi sambhAvanAsiddhirityata Aha- svArtha eveti || JOSHI-20
yasmAtkenachidanvita eva padAnAM svArtha iti, anena satyatvena j~nAnatvena vA.anvita iti, tadvisheShato dharmavisheSheNa anvayaH taduktyaiva satyAdipadoktyaiva j~nAyata ityanubha(vena)vasiddham.h | tasmAduktaM yuktamiti sheShaH | pratyekaM padAni sAmAnyato.anvitAbhidhAyIni, visheShato.anvitArthapratItistu parasparasannidhAnAhitashaktibhiH padairbhavatItyetadanubhavasiddhamityarthaH |

etadbrahmAdikamAdyaM padam.h | iha satyaj~nAnAdivAkye | anyAnyuttarA(Nyapi)Ni padA(ni)nyapi tathA yadyananvitA(nyeva)neva svArthAnvadeyustarhyanvayamanvayaj~nAnaM tu kaH kuryAt.h | AdyaM padamalabdhasahAyaM prathamaM sAmAnyato.anvitamabhidhatte | uttarANi tvAdita eva labdhasahAyAni visheShata evAnvitAbhidhAyIni | tadidaM vailakShaNyaM sUchayitumetadanyAnIti vibhAgena grahaNam.h | anyathA yadi vAkyasthAni samastAni padAni nAnvitAbhidhAyIni kintvananvitAneva svArthAnabhidadhatIti, tarhyanvayaj~nAnaM nirnibandhanamApadyetetyavakShyat.h |
etadeva prapaJNchayati- vyApAra iti ||
yadA yadyasyAnvayasya shabdArthatvaM padAbhidheyatvaM na syAttarhyanvayasya j~nAnaM kathaM na kathaJNchit.h | upAyAntarAbhAvAt.h | tathAhi anvayaj~nAnAtpUrvabhAvitvena vAdibhiraN^gIkR^itatvena vA prasaktAni tAvadetAni padAni vA vaktA vA padairabhihitAH padArthA vA vAkyaM vA vAkyAntyavarNo vA varNamAlA vA sphoTo vA shrotA veti | tatra tAvadanvitAbhidhAnAnaN^gIkAre padAnAmupAyatvaM nopapadyata ityetadvayApAro na hItyardhenAha |

ananvitArthasyaiveti sambandhaH | jAtAvekavachanam.h | tairvAkyasthaiH | yadi padAnyananvitAneva svArthAnpratipAdya nivartante | tataH padArthA evAkAN^kShAdimanto.anvayaM bodhayanti | tarhyananvita eva shabdArthaH syAt.h | anvayasya shAbdatvaM na syAditi yAvat.h | padArthAkhyaM pramANAntaraM chApa(dyeta)dyate | bhavedetat.h | yadi padArthAnAmevAnvayabodhakatvaM brUmaH | na chaivam.h | kinnAma padairabhihitAnAm.h | tatkathamanvayasyAshAbdatvamityata Aha- neti ||
sa padArthaiH pratipAdito.anvayasteShAM padAnAmartho na hItyarthaH | tathA sati pratyakShAvagatadhUmapratipAditasyAgneH pratyakShaprameyatvaM syAditi bhAvaH |
astu tarhi vAkyasyAnvayabodhakatvamiti pakSha ityata Aha- nirAkAN^kSheti ||
padAnAmanvitAbhidhAnasAmathyarmanaN^gIkurvatA vAkyasyAnvayabodhakatvamaN^gIkartumashakyam.h | yataH padAnyeva vAkyamiti budhairuchyate | padavyatiriktasya vAkyasyAbhAvAdityarthaH | kechitpadAtiriktameva vAkyaM pratipannAstadUvyudAsAya budhairityuktam.h | tachcha nirAkariShyate | gaurashvaH puruSho hastItyAdipadAnAM vAkyatvaM mA bhUditi nirAkAN^kShetyuktam.h | sannidhAnAbhAve nirAkAN^kShatvameva na nirvahatIti nirAkAN^kShatvenaiva sannidhAnasya labdhatvAnna pR^i(tatpR^i)thaguktam.h | agninA siJNchedityAdau yogyatAbhAve.apyanvayapratIteH prakR^itAnupayogAdyogyatA.api noktA | 
nanvevaM vadatA bhavataiva padavyatiriktaM vAkyamaN^gIkR^itam.h | yathA khalu tantUnAM vikriyAvisheShaH paTo na tantumAtram.h | tathA padAnAM yo nirAkAN^kShatAlakShaNo vikriyAvisheShaH sa shakyaM, padAtiriktamevetyata Aha- tattaditi ||
na tantUnAM paTa iva padAnAM nirAkAN^kShatA vikriyA | yena padAtiriktaM vAkyaM syAt.h | kinnAma shrotR^ipuruShadharma eva | jij~nAsA khalvAkAN^kShA | nirAkAN^kShatA cha nivR^ittajij~nAsatvam.h | sA cha nirAkAN^kShatA padaiH syAditi padAni nirAkAN^kShANItyuchyante | nirAkAN^kShatAkAritvaM cha na padAnAM vikriyAvisheShaH | jij~nAsitArthAbhidhAnamAtreNa taddhetutvAt.h | tasya cha svabhAvatvAt.h | tathAcha jij~nAsitArthAnabhidadhati jij~nAsAM nivartayanti padAni nirAkAN^kShANItyuktaM bhavati | 
jij~nAsitArthAbhidhAnenaiva shroturnirAkAN^kShatA syAdityetadupapAdayati- apUrteriti ||
Anayetyevokte gavAdipadaprayogAtpUrvaM, yA kimi(tyAdi)tijij~nAsA (vartate) sA tAvatAM jij~nAsitAnAmarthAnAM karmAdInAmApUrtergavAdipadairanabhidhAnAditi yAvat.h | etaduktaM bhavati | shAbdI jij~nAsA yAvatpadAni jij~nAsitA(na)rthAnnAbhidadhati tAvanna nivartate | nivartate cha padaisteShvabhihiteShvityato.anvayavyatirekAbhyAM vij~nAyate tattadarthAbhidhAnenaiva nirAkAN^kShatA syAditi | vAkyAntyavarNo varNamAleti pakShadvayamatimandamiti na dUShitam.h | tathAchoktaM purastAt.h | 
astu tarhi nirastavarNapadavibhAgaM sphoTAkhyaM vAkyamevAnvayasya pratipAdakam.h | padAni tu tadabhivyaJNjakatayopayujyanta iti pakSha ityata Aha- karmeti ||
atra karmAdigrahaNamupalakShaNam.h | jij~nAsitAnAM padArthAnAmityarthaH | anyonyasaMsR^iShyAnAmiti sheShaH | pUrtAvabhidhAne sati padairiti sheShaH | anvayo bhavetpratipAdanIya iti sheShaH | etaduktaM bhavati | sphoTamanvayasya pratipAdakaM vadatA tatsadbhAve pramANaM vAchyam.h | anvayapratItyanyathA.anupapattiriti chenna | padAnAmeva saMsR^iShyArthapratipAdakatvasambhavAt.h | nacha tadatirikto.anvayo nAmAsti pratipAdanIyo yadarthaM sphoTAnveShaNamiti |
evamanaN^gIkAre bAdhakamAha- apUrtiriti ||
anvayasyApUrtiranabhidhAnam.h | uktairiti padAnAM pramitatvamabhipraiti | nR^ishR^iN^geNa sphoTeneti tasyAprAmANikatvam.h | nR^ishR^iN^gatulyeneti pUryate.abhidhIyate.anvaya iti sheShaH | idamuktaM bhavati | padavAdinaH kalpanAlAghavaM pramitAnAM padAnAmanvitA(rthA)bhidhAnasya kalpanAt.h | sphoTavAdinastu gauravam.h | yato niShpramANakaH sphoTastasyAnvayapratipAdakatvaM cheti dvayaM kalpanIyamiti |
astu tarhi navInAbhihitAnvayapakShaH | yadi hi padAni padArthAnpratipAdyaiva nivartante padArthA evAnvayaM bodhayantIti mataM tadA syAdevoktadoShaH | nachaivam.h | kintu padAnyeva padArthapratipAdanAvAntaravyApArANyanvayaM bodhayantIti | maivam.h | tathA sati padAnAM viramyavyApAraprasaN^gAt.h | tataH ko doSha ityata Aha- vyApArashchediti ||
achetanAnAmapi padAnAM yadi punarvyApAro viramyavyApAro.aN^gIkriyate tadA pR^ichChAmo.anuktAnAmapi padAnAM padArthAdipratipAdane vyApAraH kuto na bhavatIti | 
uttaramAshaN^kate- ukta iti ||
bhAve ktapratyayaH | buddhisthatA buddhiviShayatA | padAni hi j~nAtakaraNAni na tu chakShurAdivatsattAmAtreNa | uktistu(shcha tajj~nA)j~nAnopAvaya ityato.anuktau j~nAtatvAbhAvAnna vyApAra ityAshayaH | iti yadIShyata iti sambandhaH | 
punaH siddhAntI pR^ichChati- buddhisthatvAyeti ||
padArthabodhanAdivyApArAya yatpadAnAM j~nAtatvamAvashyakam.h, tadarthaM tAni padAnyukteH prAgeva yatnaM kathaM na kuryuriti cha tvAM pR^ichChAmaH | uktiM vinA.api buddhiviShayatAyai kuto yatnaM na kuryuriti prashnArthaH | yadvA buddhiviShayatvAya yaduchchAraNaM tadarthaM tUShNIM sthitaM kuto na prerayantIti | uttaraM shaN^kate- puruSheti ||
syAdetadyadi padAni chetanAni syuH | nachaivam.h | ato vaktR^ipuruShAyattAnyeva | sa yadochchAraNena vyanakti tadA shrotR^ibuddhisthAni bhUtvA padArthapratipAdanAdivyApAravanti bhavanti | natu svayaM kimapi kurvantIti |
evaM tarhyanvayabodhanarUpo.api viramyavyApAro na teShAmupapadyata ityAha- pashchAchcheti || 
pashchAdanvayabodhane sA puruShAdhInatA | etaduktaM bhavati | chaitanye hi padAnAmanvayabodhanAya samabhivyAhR^itAnAmasmAkaM na padArthapratipAdanamAtreNa kR^itArthatA | ato.anvayo.apyasmAbhiH pratipAdanIya iti vimR^ishya viramyavyApAro yujyate | na chaivam.h | anyathokta evAtiprasaN^ga iti | shrotAnvayaj~nAne kAraNamiti tu syAt.h | kintu kartaiva | tasya kAraNaM tu vichAryate | ananvitAbhidhAyIni padAnyeva karaNIkR^itya shrotA tatsmAritAnAmarthAnAmanvayaj~nAnAya yatata iti chettatrAha- pumAneveti ||
anvayashabdena tajj~nAnamupalakShyate | pashchAt.h padaiH padArthasmaraNAnantaram.h | ananvitAbhidhAnAnAM sAhAyyeneti sheShaH | saH pumAneva | uktishabdastatkAryaj~nAnopalakShaNaH | anvayAnabhidhAyibhirapi padairyadyanvayaM pratipadyate, tadA gavAdipadairashvAdikamapi pratipadyetetyarthaH | 
shaN^kate- shabdeti ||
gavAdipadAnAmashvAdau shaktireva nAsti tatkathaM taistatpratipadyatAm.h | na (hi) chakShuShA shabdaM pratipAdyata iti chedityarthaH | tarhi samaM prakR^ite.apItyAha- anvaye kathamiti ||
anvaye shaktirahitaistaiH kathamanvayaj~nAnAya yatetetyarthaH | 
yadyananvitamityAdinoktamarthamupasaMharati- taditi ||
tat.h tasmAt.h | tasyaiva vivaraNaM kalpanetyAdi | kalpanAgauravaM prathamasUtreNa vyutpAditam.h | abhihitAnvaya ityuktasamastapakShopalakShaNam.h | kathamanubhUtivirodha ityata Aha- kartR^ishabde hIti |
katarR^igrahaNaM sambandhimAtropalakShaNam.h | visheShadharmamiti tajj~nAnam.h | devadatteneti kartR^ivAchini shabde prayukte shrotA kimiti pR^ichChatIti tAvadavivAdam.h | sa cha pachanAdidharmavisheShaj~nAnami(manvi)chChanneva pR^ichChati | visheShajij~nAsA cha dharmasAmAnyaj~nAnAdeva | nacha tadA tasya dharmasAmAnyaj~nAnopAyo.astyanyaH padAt.h | ataH padena dharmasAmAnyAnvitaM vastu pratipAditamiti j~nAyate | kimiti prashno visheShajij~nAsayetyetatkuta ityata Aha- guNeti ||
nirAkAN^kSho nivR^ittajij~nAsaH | tasmAdvisheShadharmamanvichChaktimityeva hi pR^ichChatIti sambandhaH | etaduktaM bhavati | kartrAdipadashravaNAnantarabhAvI kimityAdiprashno jij~nAsAmUlaH | prashnatvAtsaMmatavat.h | sA cha jij~nAsA dharmavisheShaviShayA | taduktyA nivartamAnatvA(tsamatmata)tsampratipannavat.h | visheShajij~nAsA cha dharmasAmAnyaj~nAnapUvirkA visheShajij~nAsAtvAtsaMmatavat.h | sAmAnyaj~nAnaM chedametatpadajanyaM tadanantarabhAvitvAtsaMmatavaditi | padena padArthamAtre.abhihite avinAbhAvabalena dharmasAmAnyaj~nAnamiti chenna | dR^iShyapadaparityAgenAdR^iShyAnumAnakalpanAnupapatteriti |
etena visheShAnvitAbhidhAnapakSho.api parAstaH | 
abhihitAnvayAdipakShANAM tyAjyatve prakR^ite kimAyAtamityata Aha- shabdA iti ||
sarve.api shabdAH sAmAnyenAnvita(sva)svArthavAchakA ityeSha eva pakShA grAhya ityarthaH | 
adhikaraNasya sAkShAtpratipAdyamartamupasaMharati- ata iti ||
anantaguNAtmakatve.api na tasyaikyaM vihanyate, nApyekenAbhinnAnAmanantatvaM guNatvaM chetyarthaH | tachchetyAnuShaN^gika(martha)mupasaMharati- eka eveti ||
tushabdena sakaladharmAnvita iti sUchayati | 
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM ubhayavyapadeshAdhikaNam.h ||
|| atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM parAnandA(paramatA)dhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM paramataH setUnmAnasambandhabhedavyapadeshebhyaH OM || parameshvarasyAnandAdayo guNAH kiM laukikAnandAdisalakShaNAH kiM vA tadvilakShaNAH | Adye na tatra bahumAnaH sambhavati | na dvitIyaH | prakArapramANAbhAvAt.h | vimatA laukikasalakShaNA AnandAdishabdavAchyatvAditi bAdhakasadbhAvAchcha | anyathA tatrAnandAdishabdapravR^ittirna syAt.h | vyutpattyabhAvAt.h | atIndriyatvena tatropadeshA(dyupAyAdya)bhAve sAdR^ishyAnumAnasyaivAnusaraNIyatvAt.h | tasya chAsiddhatvAt.h | tatashcha vedavedyatvaM na syAdityasya samAdhAnArthamidamArabhyate | tatrAshaN^kitasakaladoShaparihAro na sphuTaH pratIyata ityato vyAchaShye- te cheti ||
te guNA na kevalaM guNinA.abhinnAH kinnAmAkhilebhyo laukikAnandAdibhyo vilakShaNAshcha | kathaM vilakShaNA ityata Aha- sarva iti ||
Anando.api j~nAnAtmako j~nAnamapyAnandAtmakamityAdi | na hyevamantaHkaraNapariNAmabhedAH sukhAdayaH | sarvakartAro jagatsR^iShyayAdikartArashcha | evashabdenopachAraM vArayati | anyonyamabhede shabdAnAM payarAyatvamanekatvAbhAvashcha syAdityata Aha- tathA.apIti ||
parasparAbhede.api | tato noktadoSha iti (sheShaH) bhAvaH | anena vailakShaNyaprakAro darshitaH | pramANaM cha vakShyate | tathAchAdyaM sUtradvayaM vyAkhyAtaM bhavati |
bAdhakaparihArArthaM sUtram.h OM buddhayatharH pAdavat.h OM iti | tadvayAchaShye- vidvaditi ||
api cha tathA.api taistaiH shabdaishcha bhaNyante | kathaM vidvad.hvyutpa(ttitaH)ttyanvitA | vidvAMso hi sAkShAtkR^itabhagavadguNAH pUrvairvidvadbhirvyutpAdayituM shakyante | aviduShAM kathaM vyutpattiH | bhavitavyaM hi tayA | anyathA vidvattvasyaivAnupapatterityata Aha- yujyate cheti ||
vidvadupadeshato.aviduShAmapi vyutpattiryujyate | atIndriye kathamupadesha ityata Aha- anyeti ||

AnukUlyaM nirupAdhipriyatvamAnandasya | bodhAtmakatvaM j~nAnasyetyAdi | aparamalpatvAsthiratvAdi | AnukUlyAdeH pravR^ittinimittasya sattvAttadAshrayeNa vyutpatterapi sambhavAdAnandAdishabdapravR^ittyupapattAvanumAnamaprayojakamityuktaM bhavati | nanu vilakShaNeShvAnandAdiShu vilakShaNA eva shabdAH kuto na prayujyante | tathA sati tatra buddhipraveshAbhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | alpatvAdisAdR^ishyaM kuto netyata Aha- pUrNatvAdIti ||
(tAM) shrutiM paThati- pUrNa iti ||
pUrNaH pUrNaguNaH | sukhAduttamaH shobhanAnandatamaH | ekalaH ekAkI parAnapekShaH | suniShkalaH sarvathA vibhaktAMshavikalaH | harerguNAnparAnvilakShaNAnvaktIti |

|| atha phaladAnAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM phalamata upapatteH OM || atrAdau tAvatsvarganarakAdikaM phalaM prANinAmIshvarAdeva bhavatIti shrutyupapattibhyAmupapAditam.h | tadAkShepArthaM sUtraM "dharmaM jaiminirata eva' iti | tasyArthaH | IshvaraH phalakAraNaM cheddharmAdharmAvapekShate na vA | neti pakShe vaiShamyAdyApattirvedAprAmANyaprasaktishcha | Adye kimIshvareNa tadapekShaNIyenaiva karmaNA phalasiddheH | anyathA gauravApatteH | na chAchetanatvopapattivirodhaH | nahi rAjAdiriva karma phalaM dadAtIti brUmo yenAchetanatvaM bAdheta | kintu kAraNamAtram.h | nacha shrutivirodhaH | phalakAraNayordharmAdharmayorIshvarakAritatvena tatstutaye tasya phalakAraNatvopachArAditi |
samAdhAnArthaM sUtram.h | OM pUrvaM tu bAdarAyaNo hetuvyapadeshAt.h OM || tenedamuktam.h | apekShata eveshvaro dharmAdharmau | nacha tAvatA tayorevAstu phalahetuteti yuktam.h | dharmAderiveshvarasyApi phalahetutayA shrutisiddhatvena tyAgAyogAt.h | bAdhakAbhAvena shruterupacharitArthatAkalpanA.anupapatteH | gauravasyAprAmANikaviShayatvAt.h | parasya brahmaNaH karmaNashchobhayorhetutve

anAdikAlatvaM cha pravAhApekShayoktam.h kAMshchit.h bodhayati savyApArIkaroti svayameveti sambandhaH | lIlayA karaNIkaroti na tu tena vinA dAtuM na shaknotIti bhAvaH | 
yadetadatroktaM dharmAdharmadarshanaM tatpreraNaM tatphaladAnaM tadapreryatvAdikaM cheshvarasya | tadeva vichAryamANaM tasminmahAntaM bahumAnamutpAdayiShyati kimu samastapadArtha ityAshayavAnkamarNAM svarUpaM tAvatprapaJNchayati- karmANIti ||
tAnItyasheShajIvasthetyAdyuktavisheShaNAni | pR^ithagityekaikadharmAdharmAdhiShThA(tR^i)nabhUtAni muktavyAvR^ittaye.achetanasharIrANItyuktam.h | tata eva svakarmaphalabhAJNji cha | teShu karmAbhimAniShu | evaMvidhAnIti chetanatvAdyuktadharmavanti tAni teShvapi karmasu vartamAnAni | tataH kimityata Aha- itIshasyeti ||
evaMbhUtAnAM karmaNAM darshanAdimataH | uttamA pratibandhAdirahitatvAt.h | karmaNAmevaMvidhatvaM kuta ityata Aha- ekaiveti ||

anena samagramitihAsaM saMkShepeNa smArayanti | vyAdhatvAdiprAptyA chetanatvAdikaM gamyate | tathAshabdaH pramANasamuchchaye | anyAni brahmahatyAyAH | pR^ithak.h pR^ithaguditAni | evaM chetanatvAdinA | hIti (parama)sA(N^.hkhye)N^.hkhyaprasiddhiM darshayati | kathaM chetanatvAdinA pratItisteShAmityata uktam.h- saMsAreti ||

|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM tR^itIyAdhyAyasya dvitIyaH pAdaH ||
upAsanA.asminpAda uchyata iti bhAShyam.h | tatropAsanArthasyAsya pAdasya kA pUrveNottareNa vA saN^gatirityato.asya pAdasya saN^gatiM vadanprasaN^gAdetadadhyAyagatapAdachatuShyayasyApyAha- vairAgyata iti ||
mImAMsAsAdhyAdvairAgyAttpAgeva bhakterbhAvyatvAddArDhyamityuktam.h | yadAshabdo yasmAdityarthe | tayA.aparokShyaM bhavet.h | iti tasmAt.h | 
ayamarthaH | sAdhanavichAro.ayaM tAvadadhyAyaH | mokShasAdhanaM cha bhagavatprasAda eva | tatsAdhanAni cha viShayavairAgyaM bhagavadbhaktistadupAsanA tatsAkShAtkAra iti chatvAri | tAni cha na samakakShyANi | kintvAdau vairAgyaM sAdhyam.h | tena bhaktiH | na hi heye rAgavata upAdeye pramotpattirasti | dR^ishyate tAvaditi chet.h | nAsau dR^iDha(H) premA | ata evaM choktaM bhaktidArDhyamiti | tena vairAgyeNa bhaktidArDhyena chopAsA bhavet.h | na hyanyatra rAgavatastatra bhaktirahitasyAdaranairantaryAbhyAmanuchintanamupapa(tpa)dyate | upAsanayA chAtidIgharkAlamanuShThitayA prasanno bhagavAnAtmAnaM darshayati | yasmAdevaM vairAgyAdInAM kramastasmAttadviShayANAmeShAM pAdAnAmapyayaM kramo bhavediti | 
evametadadhyAyagatAnAM chaturNAmapi pAdAnAmAnantaryalakShaNAM saN^gatimabhidhAya tatprasaN^gAtprathamasUtramArabhyAtItAnAM sarveShAmapi sUtrANAM parasparaM saN^gatiM vivakShuH prathamasUtrArthaM tAvadanuvadati yuktita ityArabhya(vishiShya) AchAryasampadetyantena |

chaturthasya visheSho darshitaH | adhyAtmaviShayashrutivirodhaparihAraj~nAnasya charamatvopapAdanAya tasyetyuktam.h | AdhyAtmikA(hi)bhAvA mithyA samyagvA viditA bandhamokShayorantaraN^gatAmashnuvate | na tathA bAhyAH | prANatattvagAnityanena chaturthapAdagatAnAmeva mukhyaprANaviShayANAmadhikaraNAnAM prameyamadhyAtmetyanenaiva labdhametatkasmAtpunaruchyata ityato visheSheNaitadbhAvyaM tatprasAdAyattatvAjjij~nAsAyA ityAshayavatoktaM tatprasAdeti | anuraJNchitaH samIchInaH kR^ita iti yAvat.h | dehakartR^itvamityAdinA trivR^itkurvata ityadhikaraNasya sarvakartR^itvata iti sarvakartR^itvaM vij~nAya tatashcha bhagavadbhaktimAnbhUtvetyarthaH | atrApi punarvachanasya tAtparyaM pUrvavadavadheyam.h | atiduHkhasAdhanatvaM vij~nAya | tadanyatra bhagavato.anyatrAdhikaM vairAgyamutpAdyeti tR^itIyAdyasya | ajij~nAsUnAmapi kadAchitkvachidvairAgyaM jAyate.ato.adhikamityuktaM atIti cha | tadguNAdhikyeti dvitIyasya | tadvashatvAttadvashatvaM vij~nAya bhakteH prAk.h siddhatvAddArDhyamityuktam.h | na chaitatsarvamanupAsitagurorbhavatItyato vishiShyetyabhihitamiti |
kathamayamathashabdasyArtha iti chet.h | uchyate | yadyapyathashabdo.anekArthaH | tathA.apyarthAntarANAmatrAyogAdAnantaryArthaH parigR^ihyata ityavivAdam.h | AnantaryaM na yataH kutashrichadabhidhAtavyam.h | vaiyarthyAt.h | kintu yena vinA na brahmajij~nAsA bhavati yasmiMshcha sati bhavatyeva tadAnantaryam.h | tathAvidhaM cha vedArthaj~nAnAdIti |
kiJNcha jij~nAsA nAma vichArAparaparyAyaM mananam.h | nacha tachChravaNamantareNa sambhavatItyato yAvadarthajAtamatra shAstre vichAryaM tAvataH shravaNajanyaM j~nAnaM pUrvavR^ittam.h | sati cha tasmiJNjanmAntarAnuShThitasatkarmaNaH satkulaprasUtasya sAttvikaprakR^itervairAgyAdikamavashyaM bhavatyeva | yattu parairnityAnityavastuvivekaH shamadamAdisAdhanasampadihAmutraphalabhogavairAgyaM mumukShutA cheti sAdhanachatuShyayaM pUrvavR^ittamuktaM tadasmAdukta evAntarbhavatItyaviruddham.h | uttamabhaktAnAM mumukShutA nAstItyAchAryeNa na saN^kIrtitA |
etena jij~nAsAsAdhyasya vairAgyAdestatsAdhanatve.anyonyAshrayatvaM syAdityapi nirastam.h | sAttvikaprakR^iteH satsaN^gavashAdIShadvairAgyAdimataH shravaNena tadabhivR^iddhau kR^itamananAderbhUyastadabhivR^iddhiriti |
evaM prathamasUtrArthamabhidhAya tena dvitIyasUtra(sya)saN^gatimAha- kartavyeti ||
ukte sati kimiti kartavyA prayojanAbhAvAnna kartavyeti saMshayo bhavati | saMshayashabdenAtra viparyayo.abhidhIyate | mithyAj~nAnatvasAmyAt.h | saMshaye sati tatparihArAya janmAdyasya yata ityAheti sheShaH | yadvA kiM kartavyA na veti saMshaye prayojanAbhAvAnna kartavyeti pUrvapakShe cha satIti vyAkhyeyam.h | ityAheti vakShyamANenaiva(vA) sambandhaH |
prathamasUtre.ataH shabdena jij~nAsAyA mokShArthatvAtkathaM punarAshaN^ketyata Aha- ata iti ||
ataHshabdena jij~nAsAyA mokShArthatve udite.apyasya mokShArthatvasya visheShAnuktito hetoH punaH saMshaya iti pUrveNa sambandhaH | evaM tarhi janmAdisUtreNApi naiShA shaN^kA nivartate | tatrApi(hi) mokShaH samAsArthatayA vyAkhyAtavya eva | na tu visheSheNokta iti chenna | pramANavisheShAnuktita iti vyAkhyAnAt.h | etaduktaM bhavati | mokShaprayojanatvAdbrahmajij~nAsAkartavyetyataHshabdenodite.api punarAshaN^kA bhavatyeva | tatra pramANasyAnuktatvAditi |
evaJNched.h dvitIyasUtramapi kathametadAshaN^kAM nivartayet.h | na hyatrAyamarthaH pramANenopapAdita ityatastadvayAchaShye- sR^iShyIti ||
shrutatvato.asau mokShAdidAtA | yatashcha mokShAdidAtA.asAvato vo yuShmAkaM mumukShUNAM jij~nAsya evetyatamatharM janmAdisUtreNAhetyarthaH | ayamabhisandhiH | janmAdyasya yata iti sUtre shrutamiti vAkyasheShaH | tathAcha parameshvarasya mokShadAtR^itve shrutiH pramANamityuktaM bhavati | kiJNchAtra mokShadAtR^itvaM pradhAnam.h | sR^iShyayAdikartR^itvaM tu tatra hetutvenoktam.h | kevalavyatirekI chAyaM hetuH | tasya chAsiddhiparihArAya shrutatvamabhihitamiti | kR^ityAnAM kartari veti va iti ShaShThI | 
nanu mokShAdikartR^itvasyetyAdi katham.h | kartari cheti tR^ijantena ShaShThayAH samAsapratiShedhAt.h | tR^innayaM tachChIlAdau vihitaH | tena cha shritAdiShu gAmigamyAdInAmupasaN^khayAnamiti dvitIyAyAH samAsaH |
j~nAnaM rashmaya iva j~nAnarashmayaH | vyAptaj~nAnavadityarthaH | apAM taratamo nAma "kashchana munirvyApto babhUva' iti pravAdadarshanAchChiShyANAM sUtrakAre bhaktimAndyaM mA bhUdityato visheSheNopAdanam.h | 
jij~nAsAyA mokShasAdhanatve pramANAbhAvenAkShipte bhagavato mokShasAdhanatvasamarthanamasaN^gatamityata Aha- yenaiveti ||
bandhAnmokSho bandhamokSha | paJNchamIti yogavibhAgAtsamAsaH | ShaShThIsamAso vA | yena prasanneneti sheShaH | gato j~nAtaH | gatyarthAnAmavagatyarthatvAt.h | cho yasmAdityarthe | prasAdamAtrasya mokShasAdhanatvAbhAvAtsushabdaH | asyeshasya jij~nAsA.asya jIvasya muktidA | etaduktaM bhavati | jij~nAsA tAvanna sAkShAnmokShasAdhanatvenAsmAkamabhimatA | kintu (su)prasanno bhagavAneva | sa chotkR^iShyatayA j~nAtaH suprasanno bhavati | utkarShaj~nAnaM cha jij~nAsayetyevamparamparayA | tatra bhagavato mokShadAtR^itvaM tAvatpramANaiH 
samarthitam.h | prasanna eva dadAtItyutkarShaj~nAnAtprasIdatIti jij~nAsayotkR^iShyatayA j~nAyata iti cha lokata eva siddham.h | kiM tatra pramANopanyAsena | ato bhagavajjij~nAsAya mokShahetutvaM pramitamiti manyate sUtrakAra iti |
nanu sthAnAntare.asya sUtrasyAnyathAsaN^gatiruktA | satyam.h | satyAM tasyAmiyamaparA.atrokteti |
tR^itIyasUtranivartyAmAshaN^kAmabhidhAya tatparihAratvena tat.h paThati- mokShAdIti ||
pradhAnaM mokShadAtR^itvaM tatsAdhanaM sR^iShyayAdikatarR^itvaM cheshasyaiveti sambandhaH | kathamavagamyate | na kathaJNchit.h | anumAnaistattadAgamaishchAnyeShAM tathA.avagamAditi bhAvaH | iti chettatroktamiti sheShaH | kathamidaM sUtrametadAshaN^kAyA nivartakamityatastad.hvyAchaShye- shAstragamyo hIti || mokShagrahaNaM sR^iShyayAderapyupalakShaNam.h | yasmAnmokShAdidaH puruShaH shAstramAtrasya viShayo.ato vedAdikaM yaM tathAvidhaM pratipAdayati sa eva tathA pratipattavyo nAnumAdinA kalpanIya iti |
mokShAdidAtuH shAstraikasamadhigamyatvaM kutaH | parisheShAdityAshayavAnpratyakShagamyatvaM tAvad.hdUShayati- pratyakSheti ||
yadi mokShAdidAtA pratyakShaH syAditi yAvat.h | kathaJNchana tatsevAdinA | tadA savare.api yuktAH syurityarthaH | mokShadAtuH pratyakShatve kutaH sarvairmuktairbhAvyamityata Aha- yasmAditi |
yasmAtpuruShAddhetoH | amumukShutvAnna dhAvantItyAshaN^kAnivAraNAya mokShasvarUpaM vyAkhyAtaM duHkhahAniriti | na hi ko.api duHkhI duHkhaM na jihAsati iti sambhavati | pratyakShataH pratyakShagamyAt.h | rAjAdyamiti sambhAvanayoktam.h | dAridrayaduHkhaM jihAsavo vadAnyaM rAjAdyamiveti vA | anumAnagamyatvaM dUShayati- anumeti ||
yadi kashchinmokShadAtR^itvenAnumIyata ityarthaH | anumaiva puruShatvAdikA | anumAnaM sapratipakShatvAnna tatra bhavatItyarthaH | 
AgamAstvApteranishchayAdasamarthA evetyAshayavAnparisheShamupasaMharati- taditi || tattasmAnmokShadaH puruSho dhruvaM lokaM shAstragamya eva bhavediti yojanA | 
astvevaM tathA.api mokShadatvena shAstragamyatvamanyeShAM bhaviShyati | tathA pratibhAsAditi chaturthasUtrasya saN^gatiM sUchayaMstattviti padadvayaM vyAkhyAti- shAstreti ||
mokShadatvena shAstragamyashcha keshavAdanyo nAsti | kintu sa eva kuta ityataH sautraM hetuM vyAkhyAti- mokShado hIti ||
svatantra eva hi mokShadaH syAdityanvayaH | svAtanteNa samanvayashcha bhagavata eva nAnyeShAm.h | yasya cha pratIyate shrutyAdau sa eva bhagavAnviShNuriti bhAvaH | paratantro mokShadaH kinna syAditi chet.h | sa kiM svatantramanAshritya svayameva mokShaM dadyAduta svatantramanyamAshritya | Adye doShamAha- paratantra iti ||
paratantra eva | kevalaM parAnapekShayA | yadyasau svatantramanapekShyaiva svabhaktamokShAya shaktaH syAttarhi svAtmAnamapi mochayediti na saMsArI syAdityAshayaH | dvitIyaM dUShayati- anyeti || 
eSho.avAntareshvaro.anyasya svatantrasya viShNorAshrayeNa svabhaktAya mokShaM dadyAditi yadyuchyate tadA sa svatantrastena mumukShuNA.anusR^ito.asevito.anyasyAvAntareshvarasya mama bhaktAya mokShaM dehIti prArthanAvAkyamAtreNa mokShaM naiva dadyAdityapi sambhAvitameva | tathA loke darshanAditi hishabdaH | tataH kimityata Aha- ata iti ||
tadarthamapyavAntareshvarAnmokShaprAptyarthamapi sa svatantraH | tathAcha bhagavajjij~nAsAyA aparihAryatvAdvayarthAvAntareshvarasya mokShadatvakalpaneti bhAvaH | 
prakArAntareNa hetuM vyAchaShye- yameveti || Joshi-21
nena yamevaiSha vR^iNute tena labhya iti shrutimupAdatte | tameva cheti shrutyA | "tamevaM viditvA.api mR^ityumeti' iti shrutiranenopAttA | "nAnyaH panthA vidyate' iti vAkyasheSheNAdaro gamyate | mokShadatvena shAstrayonitvamasya viShNoreva | anena shrutInAM samyak.h sAdaramanvayaH samanvaya ityuktaM bhavati | nanvetayoH shrutyoreSha iti tamiti cha bhagavAnuchyata ityetatkutaH | prakaraNAdiparyAlochanayA tadavadhAraNam.h | tadidamuktaM vedavAdibhiriti ||
atra shrutyantaramAha- ya enamiti ||
"ya enaM viduramR^itAste bhavanti' iti cha shrutyeti pUrveNa sambandhaH | mImAMsArthamasyAH shruteH pR^ithaggrahaNam.h | atrainamityukto harirityetatkuta ityata Aha- ityukta iti ||
ya enaM viduriti shrutau mokShahetuj~nAnatvenoktastu "yamantaH samudre kavayo vayanti' iti samudraga uktaH | tachcha harerliN^gamityarthaH | pramANAntaramAha- tadeveti ||
ityukta iti vartate | "tadeva brahma paramaM kavInAmiti' shrutyA brahmatvenAvadhAritaH | etaduktaM bhavati | enamityukte brahmapadashravaNAttasya cha bhagavannAmatvAdbhagavAnevAyamiti j~nAyate | yadyapi brahmapadasyAnyatrApi vR^ittirasti tathApyamukhyaiva | nachaivamatra shakyate grahItum.h | tadevetyavadhAraNavirodhAt.h | idaM khalvasya mukhyato brahmatvamAchaShye | anyatra brahmashabdavR^ittimAtrasya prAmANikatvena niShedhAnupapatteriti | yuktyantaramAha- yata iti ||
"yataH prasUtA jagataH prasUtiH' iti shrutistato ya etamityuktAnmUlaprakR^iteH sR^iShyimAha | nacha mUlaprakR^iteH kAraNatvaM paramapuruShAdanyasya sambhavati | ato.apyayaM bhagavAniti | etena mokShAdikartR^itvasya shrutatvata ityuktamapi vivR^itaM veditavyam.h | 
dvitIyaM hetuvyAkhyAnamupasaMharati- tata iti ||
mukhyata iti mokShadatveneti yAvat.h | 
viShNorivAnyeShAmapi shAstrayonitvaM pratIyata iti yaduktaM tatparihArAthartvenApi sautraM hetuM vyAchaShye- shAstreti ||
anvaya upapattyAdiliN^gam.h |
yato vAcho nivartante ityAdishrutibhirbrahmaNo.avAchyatvamAshaN^kaya vAchyatvamIkShatyadhikaraNe sAdhyate | tadasaN^gatam.h | prAgvAchyatAyA anuktatvAt.h | shAstrayonitvasya lakShaNAdinA.api sambhavAdityato.adhikaraNaM saN^gamayituM saMshabdaM vyAkhyAti- samiti ||
paramamukhyArthatochyate | saN^koche(pramANA)kAraNAbhAvAt.h | tataH kimityata Aha- evamiti ||
evaM mokShAdidatvena nArAyaNaH shruteH paramamukhyArtha ityasyArthasya nirdhAraNAyeti sambandhaH | yasmAtsamityupasargeNa paramamukhyArthatochyate, evaM tasmAtsaN^gatisadbhAvAt.h nAshabdamiti jagAviti vA | 
atrAdhikaraNe gatisAmAnyAditi sUtram.h | tatprAgvAchyatAsamarthanaparaM na bhavatIti na vyAkhyAtam.h | tasyedAnIM saN^gatimAha- kathamiti ||
saMshabdo dvayartho mukhyavR^ittyeti sarvavedAnAmiti cha | tatra dvitIyArtho.atrAkShipyate | atra evaikAdhikaraNatvameShAM sUtrANAm.h | saMshabdArthAkShepasamAdhAnasyaikatvAt.h | upakramAdiliN^gairjagajjanmAdikAraNatvena parameshvare sarvavedAnAM samanvayo na j~nAtuM shakyaH | kutaH | nR^iNAM svalpAyuH praj~nAdimatAM svalpashAkhAvedi(ta)tvasyaiva sambhavena sarvavedaj~nAnAsambhavAt.h | vedAnAmapi svalpatve shakyata eva tatsamanvayo j~nAtumasmadAdibhirapItyata Aha- vedA iti ||
anantA vai vedA iti shrutimanenopAdatte | Adyo hishabdaH shrautavaishabdArthaH | dvitIyaH shruteH prasiddhatvaM dyotayati | apiH samuchchaye | na kevalaM puruShAH svalpavedavidaH | kintu vedA apyanantA iti | anantatA vedAnAmiti sheShaH | santu puruShAH svalpavido vedAshchAnantAstathA.api kathaM samanvayaj~nAnamashakyamityata Aha- ananteti ||
svalpashAkhAvidAmiti vartate | mahApralayavAridheruttAraNopameti gamakatvAtsamAsaH | devadattasya gurukulamiti yathA | yo yadvAkyaM svarUpato na jAnAti sa tatropakramAdyanusandhAya vAkyArthamavadhArayatItyasambhAvitametaditi bhAvaH | etaduktaM bhavati | vimatAH puruShA na sarvavedasamanvayaj~nAnArhAH sarvavedAj~natvAt.h | yo yadvAkyaM na jAnAti nAsau tatsamanvayamapi jAnAti | yathA sammataH | vimatA na sarvavedavedanArhA alpapraj~nAdimattvAt.h yo yadapekShayA.alpapraj~nAdimAnnAsau tadveti yathA sammataH | vedA vA naitatpuruShavedyAH | etatpraj~nAdyatikrAntatvAt.h | AkShepamupasaMharati- ityasmAditi ||
atra viShNau | tatashcha shAkhAntare pratipAdyAntarashaN^kayA noktArthAvadhAraNaM sambhavatIti bhAvaH | 
etatparihArArthatvena sUtramavatArayati- ityAshaN^keti ||
Aha gatisAmAnyAditi sUtramiti sheShaH | nanvasya sUtrasya ko.arthaH | sarvAbhiH shAkhAbhirutpAdyAyA brahmAvagaterekarUpatvAtsarvA api shAkhAH paramapuruShamekameva jagajjanmAdikAraNatvenAvagamayantIti na kvachida(pya)nyathApratipAdanaM shaN^kanIyamiti chet.h | nanvetadeva vedAnAmanantatvena j~nAtumashakyatvAdupakramAdibhistannirNayo dUre nirasta ityAkShiptam.h | punastadevochyata iti kimanena kR^itaM syAdityataH sUtrakR^ito.abhisandhimAha- ashakyeti ||
madanyairiti sheShaH | hishabdena paropanyastaM pramANamabhyupaiti | uttAraNaM pAragamanam.h | upakramAdibhirnirNayanamiti yAvat.h | udamudakamasyAstItyudI | bhUmavivakShAyAminiH | samudra ityarthaH | romakUpe layodI yasyAsau tathoktaH | pralayasamudrasamAno.api vedo madIyaj~nAne.antarbhavatIti bhAvaH | etadeva vivR^iNoti- yadyapIti ||
avyAkR^itAkAshe paramANuriva majj~nAne.antarbhavati | bhUtAkAshasya parimitatvAdavyAkR^itagrahaNam.h | vivaraNAbhAve pUrvashlokoktaM 
kiJNchid.hvyAhataM kiJNchichchAsaN^gataM pratIyeta | abhiprAyamupasaMharati- itIti ||
uktaprakAreNa nikhilyApi vedasya svenAJNjasA prameyatAM prakAshayansUchayangatisAmAnyamAha na tu nirabhisandhiryenoktadoShaH syAt.h | vishvapatiriti sarvavedavittve pramANam.h | nahi pAlanIyamavidvAnpAlako bhavati | vishvAntargatAshcha sarve vedA iti | etaduktaM bhavati sUtrakAreNa | sarvavedaj~nAnAsambhavena sarvavedasamanvayaj~nAnaM kiM mAnavAdInAmuchyate uta sUtrakarturmama | Adye.api kiM visheShato.atha sAmAnyato.api | Adyo.abhyupagamyata eva | dvitIye tu vakShyAmaH | na tR^itIyaH | mama sarvaj~natvenAsiddhayAdiprApteriti |
evaM chedyadi kashchidanyaH sUtrakAravadviShayAntare gatisAmAnyaM brUyAttadA punaranirNaya evetyata Aha- ko nAmeti ||
j~nAnena sUyar iva j~nAnasUryaH | yathA sUryaH svatejasA vishvasya prakAshakastathA.ayaM j~nAneneti | "vinA vAtam.h' ityAdiprayogadarshanAdvinAyoga iva R^ite.api dvitIyA bhavatyeva | idamuktaM bhavati | kiM sarvaj~no viparItaM gatisAmAnyaM brUyAt.h | utAparaH | nAdyaH | sarvaj~noktyorvirodhAyogAt.h | yoge vA dvayoH sArvaj~nAnupapatteH | dvitIye sampratipannasarvaj~nasUtrakAravachanavirodhAnmithyAdR^iShyirvApratArako vA.asau syAditi kathamanirNaya iti | 
astu bhagavataH sarvaj~natvena gatisAmAnyaj~nAnaM, parasya tu kathaM yadarthamidaM shAstramityataH sUtrasyArthAntaramAha- anyo.aShIti ||
alpamatirapyanyastasya prasAdataH shAkhAchatuShpaJNchagataM vasu jAnannanumitatvenAnantAgamasampado gatisAmAnyaM brUyAditi yojanA | yAsAM shAkhAnAmudAharaNena sUtrakR^itA parameshvarasamanvayo.abhihitastad.hdR^iShyAntIkR^itya shAkhAtvAdvipratipannashAkhAnAmapi tatparatvAnumAnasambhavAdanyeShAmapi gatisAmAnyaj~nAnaM yuktamiti bhAvaH | anena gatisAmAnyAnumAnAditi sUtraM vyAkhyAtamiti | nanu chatuShpaJNchashAkhAgatamiti vaktavyam.h | taddhitArthottarapadasamAhAre cheti saN^khayAyA upasarjanatvAt.h | kaDArAH karmadhAraya ityupasarjanasya paranipAto bhaviShyati | vargArthau vA chatuShpaJNchashabdau | prapaJNcho yadi vidyeteti yathA |
idamevAstu sUtravyAkhyAnaM shrotR^ipratyAyanAN^gatvAt.h | na pUrvam.h | shaN^kAnirAsAhetutvAt.h | na hi sUtrakAraH sarvaj~natvAt.h sarvavedagatagatisAmAnyaM vettItyetAvatA.anyeShAM shaN^kA nivartata ityata Aha- iti mukhyatayeti ||
iti pratijaj~na iti sambandhaH | mukhyatayetyanumAnAdinA vinA.asheShavedagatisAmAnyavit.h | devAnAmityuttamAdhikAriNAm.h | apiH padAthare | shaN^ketyarthaH | madhuno.api syAditi yathA | pUryate nivAryate | ye sUtrakArasya paramAptatvaM jAnantyuttamAdhikAristeShAM tadIyapratimAmAtreNa shaN^kA nivartata eveti tAnprati pUrvavyAkhyAnam.h | anyAnprati tu dvitIyam.h | tathA bhAShyoktaM gatisAmAnyashruteriti tR^itIyaM cheti bhAvaH | 
nanvanayA paJNchAdhikaraNyA vaktavyasyoktvatvAtkimadhyAyasheSheNetyataH prapaJNchyaprapaJNchanarUpAM saN^gatiM darshayannAha- ata iti ||
atItaprabandhenetyarthaH | pR^ithag.h vistareNAdhyAyasheSheNeti sheShaH | 
tatra prathamapAde anyatra prasiddhAnAM shabdAnAM samanvayo.abhidhIyate | dvitIye.anyatra prasiddhAnAM liN^gAtmakAnAm.h | tR^itIye tatrAnyatra prasiddhAnAmubhayarUpANAm.h | chaturthe.anyatraiva prasiddhAnAmityuktam.h | tametaM kramamupapAdayannAha- tatreti || 
tatra prathamAdhyAye, prathamapAde, shabdAnAM nAmAtmakAnAm.h, atra viShNau | mahAmalleshabhaN^gena tulyaM vartate iti tathA | yathA.anekeShu malleShu pratyarthitayA.avasthiteShvapi bhagavatA kR^iShNena pradhAnatvAchchANUrAdimallAnAmevAdau bhaN^go vihitastathetyarthaH | ubhayatra prasiddhAnAM hi shabdAnAM samanvaye.anyatraprasiddhinivAraNamAtre yatno vidheyaH | anyatra prasiddhAnAM tu bhagavati prasiddhirapyupapAdanIyeti | tataH eteShAM prAdhAnyam.h | liN^gAtmakashcha dharmavachanA vyavadhAnenAnyabuddhiM janayanti | nAmAtmakAstu sattvavachanAH sAkShAdeveti tatsamanvaye yatnagauravamastIti liN^gAtmakebhyo nAmAtmakAnAM prAdhAnyamiti | 
yadi prAdhAnyAdanyatra prasiddhAnAM nAmAtmakAnAM shabdAnAM samanvayaH prathamapAde vaktavyaH syAttadA chaturthaShAdoditasyAnyatraiva prasiddhAnAM shabdAnAM samanvayasyeto.api prAdhAnyAtprAthamyaM bhavet.h | anyatra prasiddheranyatraiva prasiddhirbalIyasItyata Aha- ita iti ||
turyapAdoditasya samanvayasyeto(.atya)pyabhyadhikatve.apyasAvatrAdhyAye prAthamyena naivodita iti sambandhaH | tattu samanvayAditi saN^kShepeNa tasyApyatroktatvAdaJNjasetyuktam.h | kuto nodita utsargasyApavAdavisheShasadbhAvAditi tushabdaH | tamevApavAdahetuM darshayati- mahAsamanvaya iti ||
tarhi na vaktavya eva niradhikArikatvAt.h | nahi gAyamAno badhireShu gAyatItyata uktaM brahmaiveti | naikAdhikArikaM shAstramityato.anya ityAdyuktam.h | sarvAdhikArisAdhAraNamarthamAdAvabhidhAyAsAdhAraNaM pashchAdvakShyAmItyAshayaH sUtrakArasya | tatra sAdhAraNe tvidaM tAratamyaM chintitamiti | durgamatvAchcheti hetvantaram.h | prathamaM buddhAvanArohAdityarthaH | etaduktaM bhavati | 
brahmAdInAmeva tatra yadyapi mukhyAdhikAritA | tathA.apyasmadAdInAmIShadadhikAro.astyeva | nacha mandAnAmasau samanvayaH prathamaM buddhimadhirohati | sAdhAraNasamanvayaj~nAnena vaidikavyutpattyanuraktA tu buddhiH krameNa tatrApyavataratIti | tataH kimityata Aha- ata iti ||
prAdhAnyAdatiprAdhAnyAnyasyopapAditatvAchchetyarthaH | tushabdo.avadhAraNe | tatrAnandamayAdhikaraNasyAdyatve hetuM sUchayannAha- tatreti ||
tatra samanvayaprapaJNchane | prathamamityanuvartate | savareShu hi shubheShu mUrdhAbhiShiktA Anandavij~nAnAdayaH | ato mAN^galikaM AchAryastachChabdasamanvayamAdAvAheti | antaradhikaraNasyAkAshAdhikaraNasya chAnandamayAdhikaraNasaN^gatatve samAne kutaH krama ityatastatra hetuM sUchayannantaradhikaraNatAtparyamAha- devateti ||
devatAH khalu jaDebhyo mukhyAH | atastadvAchinAmAkAshAdijaDavAchibhya utkarShaH | sarve shabdA addhA vachanavR^ittyaiva nopachAreNa | katham.h | shabdavR^ittyoryogarUDhyornimittAnAM bahulaprayogAdInAM harau vidyamAnatvAt.h |
tatkimanyatra shabdAnAM vR^ittireva nAsti | yena viShNumevetyavadhAryata ityata Aha- tatsaN^gAditi ||
upachAraprakArashcha prAgeva vivR^itaH | akShAdishabdavadubhayatra sAmyena pravR^ittiH kiM na syAdityata Aha- iheti || indrAdishabdA hi paramaishvaryAdiguNAnvadati | te cha bhagavata evAsAdhAraNA iti tameva paraM mukhyaM brUyuH | iha devatAntare | tathA neti sheShaH | yadvA iha deveShu tatsaN^gAditi pUrvatra sambandhaH | rUDhinimittAtishayasyApyetadupalakShaNam.h | uttarAdhikaraNeShvapyevaM kramanimittAdikaM svayamUhanIyamityAshayavAnAha- evamiti ||
viShNumeva paraM brUyuriti vartate | 
anyatra prasiddhAnAM nAmAtmakAnAM shabdAnAmanantatvAtkathaM pAdaparisamAptirityAshaN^kAM nirAkurvanprathamapAdArthamanUdya dvitIyapAdasya saN^gatimAha- ityanyatreti ||
samAnanyAyasaJNchAraviShayatvAditi bhAvaH | j~nAte prathamapAdena | shaN^kA jAyata iti sheShaH | kathaM(iti) | prAyeNa liN^gabalena hyeSha nAmAtmakashabdasamanvayo.abhihitaH | liN^gAnAM chAnyagatatvaM pratIyate | tatashcha viruddhatavAttaiH pratItaH samanvayaH samyaN^.h na syAdeva | nahi kR^itakatvena nityatvaj~nAnaM samyagutpadyate | itishabdaH shaN^kAsamAptau | tatparihArAyAnyatra prasiddhAnAmasheShaliN^gAnAm.h | Aha dvitIyapAde | 
nanvevaM tarhi yAni antastaddharmopadeshAdityAdau samudrAntasthatvAdIni liN^gAni sAdhanatvenoktAni teShAmiha vichAraH karaNIyaH | na chaivam.h | kintu yAnyuktAni na tAni vichAryante | yAni cha vichAryante na tAnyaktAni | uchyate | sarvashrutigatAH sarve.apyanyatra prasiddhAH nAmAtmakAH shabdA bhagavadviShayA eva tatra tatra shrutaiH sarvairliN^gairiti hi prathamapAdasyArthaH | tatra yAni liN^gAnyasandigdhAni tAni vihAyetarANi vichAryanta iti ko virodhaH | ata evAsheShata ityuktaM prAk.h | 
tR^itIyapadAsya prathamadvitIyAbhyAM saN^gatimAha- ubhayeti ||
bhagavattaditaraviShayatvam.h | ato.anyatra prasiddhAnAM bhagavatparatvasya samarthanam.h | liN^gAtmakAnAM cha shabdAnAm.h | 
nanvanyavAchitvanirAso.api tatraiva netara ityAdinA vihita eva | tatkathaM shaN^kodayaH | maivam.h | anyatra tAtparyAbhAvo hi netara ityAdinA darshitaH | shaktistUbhayatra syAdeva | tarhi ta eva punarvichAryAH | satmay.h | teShveva yatra yatra vichAyaprAptiste vichAryante | yadA yatrAnupapattyAdInAM saJNchAraH sugamastanvihAyAnyatrobhayagatatvaM shaN^ketaiveti yuktamuktam.h | tathA cha tattvityavadhAraNAnupapattiriti shaN^kAsheShaH | ityAshaN^kAnivR^ittyarthaM tR^itIyapAdamArabdhavAniti sheShaH | ityAheti vakShyamANena vA sambandhaH | kathamiyamAshaN^kA tR^itIye parihR^itetyatastAtparyamAha- ubhayatreti ||
harau taditaratra cha | pratItito na tu vastuto vartamAnAnAM saliN^gAnAM shabdAnAM nAmnAM liN^gAnAM cha harAveva visheShataH paramamukhyayA vR^ittyA tAtparyeNa cha samanvayaH | kuta ityata Aha- yaditi ||
yadyasmAdvartata iti sheShaH | etadapi kuta ityata Aha- yata iti ||
svatantratAstIti sheShaH | svAtantAbhAve.api kuto.anyatra shabdAnAM mukhyavR^ittyabhAva ityata Aha- asvatantreShviti ||
nanvanyeShAmasvatantratvAtteShu mukhyataH shabdapravR^ittihetorguNAderabhAvAnmukhyataH shabdA na vartanta iti chet.h | mA vartiShata | 
tathA.api visheShataH samanvayo harAvevetyetatkuta ityata Aha- ata iti || itarasya mukhyArthatvAbhAvAdityarthaH | bhAvyaM khalu shabdasya mukhyArthena | anyathA tadapekShasyAmukhyasyAnupapatteH | tathAcha dvayoH prasaktayorekasya mukhyArthatvAnupapattAvitarasya mukhyArthatvamAvashyakameva | 
yadadhInAsta ityAdinA yuktyantaramAha | 
te bhagavato.anye padArthA bhagavadapekShayA.atyalpenaiva shabdapravR^ittihetunA guNAdinA yasminbhagavatyAyattAH santaH shabdAthartvamupagatAH sa bhagavAnevesho niravadhikashabdapravR^ittinimittatvAt.h | svatantratvatashcha mukhyashabdArtha iti hi svIkartavyaH | itareShu shabdapravR^ittinimittAnyalpAnyeva tAnyapi bhagavadadhInAni | bhagavati tu niravadhikaparAdhInAni chetyetadasiddhamityata uktaM manIShibhiriti | shrutyAdiparichayavadbhiH | yo yadadhInaH shabdArthaH so.amukhya itarastu mukhya ityatra dR^iShyAntaH | ayo yathA.anyAdhInaM sad.h dAhakatvaM dAhakashabdArthatvamupagatam.h ata eva dahatIti shabdastasminnamukhyo.agnau tu mukhyastathetyarthaH | atretarasyAmukhyArthatvamanUdyata eveti na punaruktiH ka ityAha tR^itIyapAdeneti sheShaH | 
chaturthapAdasya saN^gatiM karoti- evaJNcheti ||
evaJNchetyasyaiva vivaraNamatItena pAdatrayeNa keShAJNchichChabdAnAM nArAyaNasamanvaye siddhe.apIti | asheShashabdAnAM nArAyaNe samanvayo na yujyate | yaH pratij~nAto duHkhibaddhAvarAdishabdAnAM karmAdiviShayANAM cha kathaJNchana yogena rUDhyA vA pravR^ittyanupapatteriti sheShaH | katham.h | yato.avarAdishabdavAchyatve bhagavato.avaratvAderdoShasya prAptirbhavet.h | tasyAshcha sarvapramANavirodhAt.h | karmakramAdivirodhAchcheti | iti chettatra prativihitaM sUtrakAreNeti sheShaH |
kathamityataH prathamAdhikaraNatAtparyamAha- avaratvAdIti ||
avarAdishabdApravR^ittinimittamupalabhyate pramANaiH | hishabdasteShAM prasiddhiM dyotayati | kathaM dvividhamityata Aha- parasyeti ||
svayaM para eva sanniti na pravR^ittinimittakathanaM kintu svasyAvaratvAbhAve.apIti pradasharnArtham.h | parasminnavaratvAdidharmaniyantR^itvamekaM nimittamityarthaH | tasya pramitatvadarshanaM yatheti | paragatasya jayasya rAjAdhInatvena yathA rAjA jayishabdavAchyo bhavettathetyarthaH | avaratvAnubhavI anvayo.avarashabdArthaH | avaratvAdimattvamaparaM nimittamiti yAvat.h | etachcha suprasiddhamiti na pramANamuktam.h | tataH kiM prakR^ita ityata Aha- tayoriti | 
tayoH pravR^ittihetvormadhye | tenAvarAdishabdavAchyatva cheti sheShaH | kutaH pUrva evAN^gIkriyate na dvitIya ityata Aha- dvitIya iti ||
jIva iti jaDasyApyupalakShaNam.h | tathAcha satIshvaratvahAniH syAdityarthaH | adhikaraNaphalamAha- svAtantAditi ||
paragatAvaratvAdau svAtantyasyaiva nimittatvAN^gIkArAddhareravaratvAdikaM dUShaNaM na prasajyata iti | evamuttarAdhikaraNatAtparyamapi vaktavyam.h | 
prathamAdhyAyArthAnuvAdena dvitIyAdhyAyasya saN^gatimAha- evamiti ||
sarvashabdArthavivaraNamasheSheNeti | ukte sati dvitIye.asheShavirodhAnAM nirAkR^itirIshena kR^iteti sambandhaH | virodhahInasyaiva samanvayasya | 
tR^itIyAdhyAyasya saN^gatimAha- samanvayeti ||
tadarthayoradhyAyayorupalakShaNametat.h | vastunirNaye brahmanirNaye | kiM mayA kAryamiti | 
ayamarthaH | yadyapi brahmavichAraH kartavya ityuktam.h | kR^itashchAsau | tathA.api sAdhanaphalavichArasahitasya brahmavichArasya kartavyatayoktatvAtkR^itabrahmavichArasyAdhikAriNo yanmayA kAryaM sAdhanaM tatkiM kathambhUtamiti | buddhiH syAditi | phalaviShaye kuta evaM buddhirna syAditi chetsyAdeva | kintu phalApekShayA sAdhanasya pUrvabhAvitvAttadviShayaivAdau syAt.h | tadidamuktamevashabdena | tadarthaM tR^itIyo.adhyAyaH pravR^itta iti sheShaH | 
etadgatAnAM trayANAM pAdAnAM prAguktAmeva saN^gatiM sphuTIkaroti- tatreti ||
tatra tR^itIye.adhyAye | bhaktividhAnArthaM bhaktyutpAdanArthaM vairAgyArthamiti yAvat.h | abhaktAnAM kAmyArthakarmiNAM pApinAM dveShiNAM cha | uktAyAM prathamapAdena | asheShaguNochyate parameshvarasya prokte dvitIyena | upAsanA.asminpAde vaktavyAvasaraprAptA | nanUpAsanAyAM ko bhakterupayogo yatastadAnantaryasyetyata Aha- nityamiti || yasmAdupAsanA nityamAdareNa kartavyA | AdaranairantaryAbhyAmeva saMskArAtishayasyotpAdAt.h | Adaranairantarye chopAsanAyAM nAbhaktasya bhavataH | iti tasmAdidAnImupAsanA vaktavyeti sambandhaH | 
evaM tarhyupAsanaiva vichAraNIyA | sarvashAstraparij~nAnaM prathamAdhikaraNe kasmAdvichAryata ityata Aha- seti ||
yA vaktavyatayA.avasaraprAptA sA chopAsanA dvividhaiva | na tvekarUpaiva | katham.h | ekA shAstrAbhyAsasvarUpiNI | parA cha dhyAnarUpA | ato yuktaH prathamAdhikaraNasyAtrAntarbhAvaH | tathA.apyayaM kramaH kutaH | dhyAnasya shAstrAbhyAsasAdhyatvAt.h | 
tadidamuktaM pareti | dhyAnasamAdhyoranatibhinnatvaddhayAnashabdena samAdhirapi gR^ihyate | dhAraNApratyAhAraprANAyAmA.a.asanayamaniyamAnAmapyupAsanAbhedAnAM sattvAtkathaM dvaividhyamityata Aha- tadaN^gamiti ||
tasya dhyAnasyAN^gameva natu svatantramupAsanam.h | yogashAstre chaitatspaShyamavagantavyam.h | shAstrAbhyAsasya dhyAnAN^gatve.api svatantropAsanatvaM chAsti | brahmasAkShAtkArahetutvAt.h | chittavR^ittinirodhA(katvA)chcha | "athavA satataM shAstravimarshena bhaviShyati' iti |
kimato yadyupAsanAvasaraprAptA dvividhA cheti | tatrAha- tatheti ||
tathA tasmAdavasaraprAptatvAt.h | asminneveti sambandhaH | upAsanameveti cha (vA) | tena pareShAmidAnIM tu prativedAntaM vij~nAnAni bhidyante na veti vichAryata iti pAdArthakathanaM nirAkaroti | tathAhi | kiM bhedAbhedau, virodhAvirodhau, uta vilakShaNatvAvilakShaNatve | nAdyaH | gatArthatvAt.h | dvitIye brahmaNo.akhaNDatvena prAptyabhAvaH | saguNabrahmaviShayA prANAdiviShayA cheyaM chinteti chenna | prakR^itaviShayaprayojanaviruddhatvenAkartavyatvAditi | addhA upayuktaprameyeNa saha | ata eva vistarAt.h | anena keShAJNchidadhikaraNAnAmanantarbhAvashaN^kA nirAkR^itA bhavati | shrutigrahaNamupalakShaNam.h | atra saN^gatikathanaprastAve.api keShAJNchitsUtrANAmarthavyAkhyAnaM saN^gatisamarthanArthameveti na doShaH | 
evaM saN^gatimabhidhAyaitatpAdAdhikaraNeShu pUrvapakShayuktIH siddhAntayuktIshcha saN^graheNAha- pR^ithagdR^iShyirityAdinA ||

|| OM sarvavedAntapratyayaM chodanAdyavisheShAt.h OM || atra dhyAnopAsanArthibhiH kiM svashAkhA evAdhyayanashravaNamananairj~nAtavyAH kiM vA sarve.api vedA iti saMshaye shAkhAbhedasya suprasiddhatvAdanyathA tadanupapatteH prathamapakSha eva jyAyAniti prApte siddhAntitam.h sarvavedAntapratyayamiti | tatra sarvashabdo.asaN^kuchitavR^ittiriti pratItinirAsAya vyAchaShye- yashashaktIti ||
vij~nAyAvasthitasyetyadhyAhArAtsamAnakartR^ikatAsiddhiH | upAsanaM kurvANo bhavediti vA | upAsanaM kurvIteti vA | bhavedityasyottaravAkye.anvayaH | atra yathAshaktyakhilAnvedAnvijAnIyAdityeva vaktavyam.h | tathApyatrochyamAnaM sarvaparij~nAnaM dhyAnopAsanAN^gamiti dasharyitumevamuktam.h | tatashcha paretyuktaM vivR^itaM bhavati |
yathAshruta evArtho.astu kiM visheSheNenetyata Aha- tatreti ||
tatropAsakeShu yasmAtsamyagakhilasya vedasya vij~naptirbrahmaNa eva yuktA bhavennAnyeShAM tasmAdanyeShAM yathAyogaM yathAshaktyevAkhilaj~naptireShyavyA | etaduktaM bhavati | sarvAdhikArisAdhAraNaM tAvadidaM sUtram.h | chodanAdyavisheShAdiyuktibhistadavagamAt.h | saMshayapUrvapakShAsaN^gatatvaprasaN^gAchcha | nacha sarveShAM sarvavedavij~nAnaM sambhavati | vedAnAmanantatvAt.h | alpapraj~nAdimattvAchchA puMsAm.h | tato yuktamuktamiti | yadvA prathamavAkya eva bhavedityanenaivaiSho.abhihitaH | yasmAdevamevopapannaM bhavediti | tataH kasya kIdR^ishI shaktiriti jij~nAsAyAmidaM vAkyam.h | hishabdaH prasiddhau | yogo yogyatA | j~naptirj~naptishaktiH | 
upAsanAyogyatAsamanvaye khalvatra sarvavij~nAnamuchyate | nachAlpavedaj~nasya sA bhavati | "sarvaishcha vedaiH paramo hi devo jij~nAsyo.asau nAlpavedaiH prasiddhayet.h' ityAdishruteH | ataH sarvashabdo mukhyArtha eva vyAkhyAtavyaH | ata eva yadyapyasmadAdInAmasmiJNjanmani sarvavedaj~nAnamasambhavi | tathA.api tAdR^ishaM janma kalpanIyaM yatredaM sambhavatItyata Aha- tAvateti ||
yathAshakti vij~nAnamAtreNa | ayamabhisandhiH | dhyAnopAsane vedaj~nAnasya kathamupayogaH | dhyeyAj~nAne dhyAnAyogAditi chet.h | tarhi sarveShAM sarvavedArthadhyAnAbhAvasya vakShyamANatvAnna sarvavedaj~nAnamupayuktam.h | satyam.h | tathA.apyadhigataikashAkhasya shAkhAntare.anyathoktishaN^kayA dhyAnAsambhavAtsarva(veda)parij~nAnamAvashyakamiti chenna | gatisAmAnyAnumAnenaiva shaN^kAnirAsasyoktatvAt.h | anyathA parasparavirodhena vedAprAmANyApatteH | tataH shrutiryathAshaktItyeva vyAkhyeyeti |
yathAshakti vedaj~nAnaM bhagavadupAsanopayuktaM na sarvavedaj~nAnAvashyambhAva ityatra purANavAkyamapi paThati- mahattvasyeti ||
mahattvasya paraM pAraM viditveti sarvavedaj~natvamuchyate | vedena vinA bhagavanmahattvasya j~nAtumAshakyatvAt.h | stoShyatAmiti dhyAnasyApyupalakShaNam.h | samAnanyAyatvAt.h | nAstyeveti niyamaniShedhaH  yathAyogyAkhilaj~natA dhyAnopayoginIti vij~nAyata iti 
sheShaH | yathAyogyeti katham.h | avyayIbhAvasya napuMsakatvena yathAyogyamiti bhAvyam.h | satyam.h | yathAyogyAkhilaj~nateti samAso.ayamityadoShaH | yadvA yathA yAdR^ishI yogyA tathaiveti bhinne evaite pade | 
nanvatrAtmaj~nAnamevopAsanopayogitvenochyate | natu yathAshaktij~nAnam.h | ato na prakR^itopayogIdaM vAkyamityata Aha- Atmeti ||
atropAsanasyAtmaj~nAnAnurUpatvaM nAma yathAshakti vedavichAraNAdbhAvitvameva | anyathA vAkyasyAsaN^gatatvaprasaN^gAditi bhAvaH | sarvaj~nAnaniyame nirAkR^ite kintvityAshaN^kAyAM yathAshaktij~nAnaM hi vaktavyam.h | na tvAtmaj~nAnam.h | nahi paraj~nAnaM prAN^.h nirAkR^itam.h | tasmAdAtmaj~nAnaM nAmAtmayogyaM j~nAnamityeva vyAkhyeyamiti |
kutaH savarvedaj~nAnamityatashchodanAdyavisheShAdityuktam.h | tatra shAkhAbhedasya suprasiddhatvAchchodanAdikamapi visheShaniShThaM vyAkhyAtamityato yuktyantaramAha sUtrakAraH OM svAdhyAyasya tathAtvena hi samAchAre.adhikArAchcheti OM || tatra hIyantaM vyAchaShye- veda iti ||
anena "vedaH kR^itsno.adhigantavyaH sarahasyo dvijanmanA' iti smR^itimupAdatte | svAdhyAyAdhyayanaM kartavyaM bhavedityanena "svAdhyAyo.adhyetavyaH' iti shrutim.h | anyathA svasvashAkhAmAtraj~nAnAN^gIkAre | 
etaduktaM bhavati | svAdhyAyasya svAdhyAyavidhestathAtvena sAmAnyataH sarvavedAdhyayanavidhAyakatvena hetunA sarvaj~nAnamaN^gIkaraNIyam.h | adhyayanasyArthaj~nAnaparyantanAsthiteH | svasvashAkhAmAtraj~nAnAN^gIkAre chAsya vidhervaiyarthyApatteH | nacha vAchyaM shAkhAbhedasya prasiddhayA svAdhyAyapadakR^itsnapadadarshanAt.h | shAkhAbhedasyAshaktinimittatvopapatteriti |
nanu shrutyantaraM hishabdena smR^itiH sUtrakR^itopAttA tatkathamatra viparyayaH | uchyate | AkAN^kShAkrameNa sUtram.h | vyAkhyAnaM tUpodghAtaprakriyayeti na virodhaH | shrutismR^itibalAdeva yathAshakti savarvij~nAnasyaiva nishshaN^katAhetutvaM kalpyate | bhUyodarshanaM chAnumAnAN^gamiti suprasiddham.h | 
Aha nAdhyayanavidhiprayuktamadhyayanam.h | kintvadhyApanavidhiprayuktameva | adhyayanavidherniyojyarahitatvAt.h | nahyatra svargakAmo yajetetivatkashchinniyojyaH shrUyate | nApi vishvajidAdAviva kalpayituM shakyate | adhyApanavidhinaivAdhyayanasiddhau kalpakAbhAvAt.h | nachAdhyApanavidhirapi niyojyarahita iti vAchyam.h | AchAryakaraNakAmasya tatra niyojyatvAt.h | naShyavarShaM brAhmaNamupanayItetyAtmanepadashravaNAt.h | "sammAnanotsaJNjanAchAryakaraNaj~nAnabhR^itivigaNanavyayeShu niyamaH' ityAchAyarkaraNe nayaterAtmanepadavidhAnAt.h | tamadhyApayItetyupanayanAdhyApanayorekakartR^ikatApratIteH | na hyadhyApanamadhyayanena vinA bhavatIti svasiddhaye parA(pekSha kShepa)lakShaNenopAdAnopAdAnenAdhyApanavidhirevAdhyApanavidhirevAdhyayanaM prayuN^.hkte | kiJNchAdhyayane sati vidhij~nAnaM tatashchAdhyayanamitItaretarAshrayatvaM syAt.h | ato naitadvAkyodAharaNamatra saN^gatamiti | 
uchyate | syAdevaM yadyadhyApanavidhiprayuktamadhyayanaM syAt.h | nachaivam.h | adhyApanasya jIvIkArthatvAt.h | trINi karmANi jIviketi vachanAt.h | adhyayanasya cha nityatvAt.h | "yo.anadhItya dvijo vedAn.h' ityakaraNe pratyavAyashravaNAt.h | nacha nityamanityena prayujyate | kiJNchaikasya mANavakasyAdhyApanena charitArthatve mANavakAntarasyAnadhyayanaprasaN^gaH | yo yenopanItaH sa tenAdhyApanIya iti chet.h | tarhyupanAyake parete.adhyayanAbhAvaH syAt.h | yatpunaritaretarAshrayatvamuktaM tat.h prAtaHsandhyAmupAsItetyAdAvapi samAnam.h | ayamapyAchAryasyaiva vidhiH | shauchAchArAMshcha shikShayedityAderiti chenna | AchArye parete tadabhAvApAtAt.h | ato.adhyayanAdividhiM vR^iddhAH kathaJNchinmANavakaM bodhayantItyaN^gIkAryamityalam.h | Joshi-22
mAchAredhikArAchcha ityetadvayAchaShye- adyApIti ||
yataH sarvavij~nAnamAvashyakam.h | tenaiva hi kAraNena devAdyA adyApi shravaNamanane kurvanti sadA dhyAyanti cha | anyathA mahAmatInAM teShAmekaikashAkhAshravaNAderalpIyasaiva kAlena kartuM shakyatvenAdyApi tatkaraNaM na syAditi | yathAyogaM yathAshaktIti pratyekaM visheShaNam.h | R^iNvanta ityAtmanepada uktam.h | samAchArachchetyevokte devAdInAM vedAdhikAritvAbhAvAtkathametadityato devatAdhikaraNanyAyaM mA vismArShIriti sUchayituM sUtrakR^itA samAchAre.adhikArAchchetyuktam.h |
yadi brahmasAkShAtkAravanto.api devAdyAH shravaNAdyanutiShThanti tarhi tasya niravadhikatvaM prasaktamityata Aha- tathA.apIti ||
yadyapi sUtrakAreNa devAdyAchAraH pramANIkR^itastathA.api, vastu parabrahmAdikam.h | nirNayo yathArthaH parokSho nishchayaH | prathamasyaivashabdasyAvastunirNayAdeveti sambandhaH | vastunirNayahetutvAchChravaNAderiti hishabdAtharH |
vastunirNayaparyantaM shravaNamanane kartavye ityasat.h | nirNIte.apyarthe punaH kAraNAntaropanipAtena saMshayAdyutpAdasya darshanena vastunirNayasyAvadhArayitumashakyatvAdityata Aha- matIti ||
matirmananaM shrutiH shravaNam.h | uttamaH shiShyayogyatAbhij~naH | kurvataH shravaNAdikam.h | darshanaM brahmasAkShAtkAH | etaduktaM bhavati | brahmadarshanArthaM hi shravaNAdikam.h | nacha tadyathAkathaJNchidanuShThitaM tatsAdhanam.h | kintu shiShyayogyatAbhij~nagurupradAnapUrvakameveti vakShyati | atastAdR^isho gurureva shravaNAdikAlavisheShamupadekShyati | yataH paraM kAraNashatopanipAte.api na saMshayAdyutpAdaH syAditi | 
devAdyAH shravaNAdikamadyApi kurvantIti na yuktam.h | syAddhi darshanamiti shravaNAdestattvadarshanasAdhanatvasyoktatvAt.h | devAdInAM cha tattvadarshanasyautpattikatvAt.h | yathoktam.h "naiva devapadaM prAptA brahmadarshanavarjitAH' ityAdi | nacha prAptasAdhyaH sAdhanamutiShThatItyata Aha- shravaNamiti ||
dR^iShyatattvasyApi puMsaH shravaNaM mananaM dhyAnaM cha visheShAnandasamprAptyai yujyata eveti yojanA | evaM tarhi shravaNAderdarshanasAdhanatvoktirvyAhanyata ityata Aha- anyasyeti ||
adR^iShyatattvasyaitAni shravaNAdIni dR^iShyaye bhavanti | yathA khalu samuchchayavAdinAM j~nAnAtpUrvANi karmANi j~nAnArthIni | tataH parANi tu mokShArthAni | yathA cha sakAmAni karmANi saMsArakAraNAni niShkAmAni tu j~nAnakAraNAni | tathA shravaNAdInyadR^iShyatattvasya j~nAnArthAnIti na taduktivyAghAtaH | dR^iShyatattvasya tu visheShAnandArthAnIti devAdInAM tadanuShThAnaM cha yuktam.h | samAchArakathanaM cha yathAshakti vedArthashravaNamananayoH kartavyatAmAtropodbalanAya kR^itamiti nAsaN^gatam.h | visheShAnandaM tu vakShyAmaH |
shiShyayogyatAbhij~nagurUpadeshAnusAreNa shravaNAdikaM kartavyamityayuktam.h | tAdR^ishasya gurordulabhatvena shravaNAdyabhAvApatteH | labhyamAno.apyasAvanuShThitashravaNAdinA AdhyAtmikashaktisampannenaiva shiShyeNa labhyate nAnyena | tathAchAnyonyAshraya ityata Aha- yadIti ||
dvividhaM shAstraM nirNItaM nirNetavyaM cha | tatrAdyaM brahmasUtrAdikaM, dvitIyaM vedAdikam.h | tatra nirNItasya shravaNAdikaM samAcharet.h | sarvaj~nAnAM siddhAntAnusAreNa yo nirNayaM jAnAti tasmAt.h | idamuktaM bhavati | mukhyasya guroH prathamamalAbhe.api na shravaNAdyabhAvApattiH | amukhyAdapi gurostadupapatteH | tatra mukhyavadamukhyasyAtigahanavedAdivyAkhyAnasAmarthyAbhAve.api nirNItavyAkhyAnamupapadyata eva | nacha nirNItashAstrasyApi vyAkhyAnavipratipattyA.abhiprAyo duradhigama iti vAchyam.h | sarvaj~napraNItopAyagranthAnusAreNAmukhyasyApi gurostadavagamasambhavAt.h | evaM chAmukhye shravaNAdAvanuShThite mukhyo.api gururlabhyata iti |
sarvaj~nasya guroH shravaNAdyaN^gatve tadabhAve shravaNAdyabhAva eva kuto nAN^gIkriyate kimanenAmukhyena shravaNAdinA | sarvaj~naguruprAptistu puNyopachayenApi bhaviShyatItyata Aha- shravaNAdIti ||
santi tAvatsarvadA shravaNAdikaM kartavyaM kShaNamapi na tyAjyamityevamarthAH shrutismR^itayaH svAdhyAyapravachane eveti nAko maudgalya ityAdyAH | tatra cha sarvaj~no gururaN^gam.h | tadalAbhe tu guNe tvanyAyyakalpanamiti nyAyena yAdR^ishatAdR^ishamapi shravaNAdikaM kAryamevetIti bhAvaH | 
nanvetAH shrutaya evAnupapannArthAH | aparihAryanidrAdyupadravaprAptau shravaNAdeH kartumashakyatvAt.h | na hyAkAsharomanthanaM shakyavidhAnamityata Aha- atIti ||
parihartumashakye nidrAdau prApte tu punareva tadapagamanAnantarameva shravaNAdikaM samAcharet.h | ayamabhiprAyaH | yathA sAyamprAtaragnihotraM juhotItyAdividhayaH sannipAtAdyupaplavasambhave.api nAnupapannastathA prakR^ite.apIti |
nirNayaj~nasya gurorabhAve kiM shravaNAdyabhAva eva, netyAha- abhAva iti ||
nirNayaj~nasya gurorabhAve.api yAdR^ishatAdR^ishAtsarvadA R^iNuyAt.h | manvIta cha | nahi guNAlAbhe mukhyaparityAgo yukta iti bhAvaH | vedAdishravaNe sarvaj~no gururapekShitaH | taditarashravaNe tu nirNayaj~naH sarvaj~nakalpaH | dvayorabhAve.api shravaNAdikaM chedanuShTheyaM tadA.asachChAstrANAmiti pratItiH syAt.h | ataH sachChAstrANyevetyuktam.h | yAdR^ishatAdR^ishAt.h R^iNuyAdityanenAtiprasaktau satyAmAha- yadIti ||
yadi tasminpuruShe svApekShayA samyagj~nAnAdiprAchuryamupalabhyate tarhi tataH R^iNuyAt.h | na tvadhamAt.h | vaiyarthyAt.h | na hyadR^iShyamAtrArthaM shravaNAdikamiti bhAvaH | 
svato.adhikasya puruShasya prabandhena vyAkhyAnAsAmbhave kiM shravaNAdyabhAva evetyAkAN^kShAyAmAha- mahadbhaya iti ||
svato mahadbhayo, mahattvaM cha na sajj~nAnamAtreNa kintu viShNubhaktyAdiguNaishchetyuktaM viShNubhaktebhya iti | tAdR^isha eva hyAdaramutpAdayanvyAkhyAti | sAdarameva cha shravaNAdikaM phalAyAlam.h | saMshayAn.h aj~nAnaviparyayAMshcheti shravaNAdiphalamuktam.h | 
ekasmAtprabandhena shravaNAdyasambhave.api bahubhyo mahadbhayo yathAshakti yathAsambhavamekaikadeshashravaNAdikamapi kuryAdeva | tenApi saMshayAdichChedasya shravaNAdiphalasya lAbhAditi bhAvaH |

apichAvitaretarayoge | shrutA.a.avR^ittipravachanAbhyAmabhinavotprekShodayAtte.api shravaNAdiphalaM prasuvAte | samyak.h shravaNAdirahito vyAchakShANaH skhalanena pratyaveyAt.h | tatkathamuchyate shiShyebhyo brUyAditi tatrAha- saditi ||
brUyAditi sambandhaH | prAmANikatayA.abhimAno.arthaH siddhAntaH | natu prAmANika eveti niyama; | tathAtve shabdanityatvaM keShAJNchitsiddhAntaH | keShAJNchittadanityatvamiti na syAt.h | dvayoH prAmANikatvAyogAt.h | ayaM tu na tathA | api tu prAmANika evetyataH sadityuktam.h | svArthiko Nich.h | ajahadityarthaH | yadvA shiShyairahApayan.h | satsiddhAntahAnireva mahataH pratyavAyasya heturiti vakShyAmaH | kShudrasskhalitaM tvalpIyasa eva | nacha tAvatA mahAprayojanavyAkhyAnatyAgaH | tathA sati mR^igabhayAdbIjAnAvApaprasaN^gAditi bhAvaH | 
ko.asau satsiddhAnto yo na hAtavyaH | dvividhaH satsiddhAntaH parAparabhedAt.h | pratyekaM dvividho vAchanika AnuShaN^gikashcha | tatra vAchanikaM paraM satsiddhAntaM tAvadAha- asheSheti ||
anyattattantramiti sakalajagajjanmAdikAraNatvamuchyate | nirNIyata iti nirNayaH | samyagvinirNayo vAchanikaH parasiddhAntaH | sAkShAdbrahmasvarUpAvadhAraNapare janmAdisUtre khalvabhihito.ayamarthaH | AnuShaN^gikaM parasiddhAntamAha- svatantratvamiti ||
svatantratvaM svAdhInasattvAdimattvam.h | tasya viShNoH | dvitIyastasyetishabda uttaratra sambaddhayate | sarvato bhedashcheti | prakR^itijIvajaDebhyo.atyantabhinnatvam.h | nanvetadapyasambhavastu sato nAtmA.ashruteH pR^ithagupadeshAdityAdinA.abhihitameva | tatkathamAnuShaN^kikaH siddhAntaH | satyam.h | tathA.api pradhAnaprameyopayogitayoktatvAdadoShaH | svagatabhedavarjitatvAderupalakShaNametat.h | iti samyak.h sthitiriti vakShyamANenAnvayaH | 
kathamasyAtharsyAnuShaN^gikatvamityata Aha- adoShatvasyeti ||
viShNoradoShatvasya siddhayarthamaN^gIkAryo.ayamartha iti sheShaH | upalakShaNametat.h | asheShaguNapUrNatvasya sakalajagajjanmAdikAraNatvasya chetyapi draShyavyam.h | anena kathaM tatsiddhirityata Aha- yadIti ||
yasmAjjagatA.abhede viShNordoShasambandhaH prasajyate tasmAditi pUvareNa sambandhaH | atrApyabheda ityasvAtantyasyApyupalakShaNam.h | tadanvaya iti cha guNapUrtyAdyabhAvasyApi | anyattattantramityanyashabdo.amuktaviShaya iti pratItiH syAttadarthamAha- tattantratvaM cheti ||
chashabdo vakShyamANena bhedena saha samuchchayArthaH | aN^gIkAyarmiti sheShaH | kimarthamidamaN^gIkAryaM janmAdisUtrasyAmuktaviShayatayA.apyupapatterityata Aha- taditi ||
nahi muktAnAM tattantratvena vinA tasya nirargalamaishvaryaM siddhayati | nacha tadantareNa guNapUrtirbhavatIti | syAdetat.h | yadi muktAH paramAtmano bhinnAH syuH | nacha tathA | tatkiM tattantratvenetyata Aha- muktAnAmapIti ||
paramAtmano.atyantabhedashchAN^gIkAryaH | anena "tasya bhedashcha sarvataH' ityetadapi vivR^itaM bhavati | kimarthamityataH prayojanaM vaktuM pIThamArachayati- nahIti ||

bhinnamabhinnatAM gachChatItyasyArthasyAbhAvo.anubhavasiddho.api | tataH saMsAre.apyabhinnAnAmeva muktAvabhedo vyajyata ityeva vaktavyam.h | tathaivAstvityata Aha- pUrveti ||

bhedena sahito.abhedo bhedAbhedaH | "vipratiShiddhaM chAnadhikaraNavAchI' iti dvandvaikavadbhAvo vA | atrApi pUrvanyAyena saMsAre.api bhedAbhedAvaN^gIkAryau | tatashchAbhedena doShANAmapi sambhavaH | bhedena tatparihAro bhaviShyatIti chettarhi kimajAgalastanAyitenAbhedeneti | idAnImaparaM siddhAntamAha- nirdoShatvamiti ||

etadvedAdikam.h | tataH paraM tadviruddhaM tadudAsInaM cha | R^igAdyA bhArataM chaivetyAdyAgamo.atra sphuTa eva | dushshAstraM nAbhyasediti vaktavye parityajediti vachanaM na kevalaM tatrodAsInatvaM kintu hetutayA j~nAnamapi bhAvyamiti j~nApayitum.h | atra chAsachChAstrAdhigamanamiti pAtakeShu parigaNanaM pramANam.h | sphuTAni chAchAryeNAnyatrAtrArthe vAkyAnyudAhR^itAni |

saMshayashabdena viparyayo.api lakShyate | nirNaye sati nididhyAsanena brahmadarshanaM bhavatIti yojyam.h | etaduktaM bhavati | satyaM nididhyAsanaM brahmadarshanasAdhanamiti | kintu tatsiddhaye shravaNamanane api kartavye | avitathaM brahmAnuchintanaM hi nididhyAsanam.h | vitathAnuchintanasya chaturthe nirAkariShyamANatvAt.h | nachAviditasyAnuchintanaM sambhavatIti | tadvedanAtharM shravaNamabhyarthanIyam.h | shrute chArthe liN^gAbhAsapratibhAsena saMshayaviparyayodayena vitathaM tadbhavatIti tad.hvyudAsaheturmananamapyeShyavyamiti |
anye punarmanyante | shravaNameva brahmAparokShaj~nAnasAdhanam.h | manananididhyAsane shravaNaM prati phalopakAryaN^gabhUte | asambhAvanAviparItabhAvanAkh.hyachittavikShepapratibaddhaM hi brahmAparokShaj~nAnaM nAvidyAnirmUlanasyeShyam.h | mananAdikaM cha pratibandhaM nivartayatIti | tadasat.h | shabdasya sAkShAtkArakAraNatAyAH kvApyadarshanAt.h | brahmaviShayashabdavaddharmAdiviShayasyApi tathAtvApatteshcha | nacha visheShaheturasti | yena brahmaviShayasyaiva tadbhAvo na dharmAdiviShayasyeti pratImaH | pratyakShalakShaNAkrAntatayA shabdasya tatrAntarbhAvashchApadyeta | atha matam.h | dR^ishyate tAvaddashamastvamasItyAdivAkyasya sAkShAtkArakaraNatvam.h | nacha tatrApIndriyameva karaNaM na shabda iti sAmpratam.h | shabdasyApyanvayavyatirekasiddhatvAt.h | astu tarhIndriyameva karaNaM shabdastu sahakArIti chenna | vaiparItyasyApi suvachatvAt.h | tathA.api kutA vinigamanamiti chet.h | kvachidbahalatame tamasi kvachichcha lochanavirahiNo.api vAkyAddashamo.asmItyaparokShapratItidarshanAditi vadAmaH | dharmAdiviShayasyApi 
shabdasyAparokShaj~nAnasAdhanatvApAdanaM chAsat.h | vaiShamyAt.h | prakR^ito hi shabdo.aparokShabrahmAtmaviShayaH | na tathA.anyaH | asti chAsyAparokShaj~nAnasAdhanatve pramANam.h | nAnyasya | tathAhi | vimataM sha(shA)bdaj~nAnamaparokSham.h, aparokShaviShayatvAt.h sukhAdij~nAnavat.h | aparokShatvaM vedAntavAkyajanyaj~nAnavR^itti, aparokShaj~nAnaniShThAtyantAbhAvApratiyogitvAt.h j~nAnatvavaditi | nacha vivAdAdhyAsitaH shabdo.aparokShaj~nAnajanako na bhavati, shabdatvAt.h, jyotiShyomAdivAkyavaditi yuktam.h | dashamastvamasItyAdau vyabhichArAt.h | shrUyate cha "taddhAsya vijij~nau tamasaH pAraM darshayati' ityupadeshamAtradevAparokShapramitijanma | ata eva brahmAtmaviShayavAkyAnyatvena pratyakShalakShaNaM visheShaNIyamiti |

kathametachChativirodha ityata Aha- ityAdIti ||
