vivikShurveshanasambhAvanAviShayaH | AshaN^kAyAmachetaneShUpasaN^khayAnamiti vachanAt.h | shvA mumUrShatIti yathA | atyAgAttamaH | mama pitA mahyaM mannimittaM tvamanindat.h | mayi madviShaye chAghavAnaparAdhavAn.h | tasmAdviShNuvaiShNavanindAparAdhajAdaghAnnityanirayAt.h | nindAdikaM cha dveShamUlamiti prasiddhameva | narahariM prati prahlAdasya vAkyamidam.h | tataH sthAnAt.h | nindAM R^iNvato yadA.adhaHpAtastadA nindakasya kimu | mAnuShIM manuShyasadR^ishIm.h | ye mAmavajAnanti te moghAshAdimanto bhavanti | teShAM sukhalesho.api na bhavati | AtmaparadeheShu prerakatvena sthitam.h | saMsarantyatreti saMsArA dehAH | tasya vivaraNamAsurIShvevetyAdi | loko janastasyAntashchaNDAlAdistatparyantasya | 
kathametatsmR^itivirodha ityata Aha- ityAdIti ||
j~nAyata iti sheShaH | tamo.api nirutthAnamiti tushabdaH | 
ato yamAdyaN^gamavashyAnuShTheyamiti siddham.h |
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM anubandhAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM vidyAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM vidyaiva tu nirdhAraNAt.h OM || yadyapIdamadhikaraNamanubandhAdibhya ityataH pUrvaM tathA.apyupAsanasvarUpAvagame satyeva tatsAtharkyasamarthanasyAvasaro nAnyatheti vyutkrameNa vyAkhyAtam.h | tathAhi | na bhagavadupAsanaM kartavyaM vaiyarthyAt.h | nacha sAkShAtkArArtham.h | tasyApi vyarthatvAt.h | nacha mokShaprayojano.asAviti vAchyam.h | chArvAkadishA mokShasyaivAbhAvAt.h | bhAve vA jainAdimatAnusAreNa sAdhanAntarasAdhyatvAditi prApte mokShasadbhAvaM tasyApi bhagavaddarshanasAdhyatvaM cha sAdhayitumidamArabhyate | yadyapi samayapAde chArvAkAdimatAni nirAkR^itAni | tathA.api mokShatatsAdhanaviyadUShaNavisheShavyutpAdanAtharo.ayaM prayatnaH | tatra chArvAkamataM tAvadanuvadati- naiveti ||
evashabdaH svarUpaniShedhadyotanArthaH | anyathA puruShavisheShAdisambandhena niShedho.api j~nAyeta | tasmAdupAsanaM vyarthamiti sheShaH | 
tarhi kaH puruShArtho.astItyata Aha- bhoga iti ||
srak.hchandanAdiviShayasukhAnubhavo bhogaH sa puruShArtho.astIti prAhuriti sambandhaH | bhogashchaihika eva na tu svargAdigata ityAha- sharIreti ||
sharIrapAtaparyantamityarthaH | kutaH svargApavargayorasattvamityata Aha- bhasmIbhAva iti ||
tataH pAtAnantaraM sharIrasya bhasmIbhAvo bhavet.h | idamuktaM bhavati | sharIrapAtottarakAlamAtmanaH svargApavargau vaktavyau | AtmA cha na sharIrAtirikto.asti | sharIraM cha pAtottarakAlaM nashyatyeva | tataH kasya tau syAtAmiti | iti prAhuriti sambandhaH | shaN^kAsamAptau vetishabdaH | 
tadetatpramANAbhAvena dUShayaMstAvatpR^ichChati- taditi ||
mokSho naivAstIti vAkyArthaM taditi parAmR^ishati | kena mAneneti | pratyakSheNa vA taditareNa vetyarthaH | dR^iShyamavagatam.h | dvitIyastAvachchArvAkeNa nAN^gIkartuM shakyata ityAshayavAnAha- pratyakSheti ||
pratyakShamekameva pramANaM nAnyadityabhyupagachChatA | pUrveNa sambandhaH | AdyaM nirAkaroti- nahIti ||
anumAnAdikaM tAvatparasya mAnaM na bhavati | yachcha mAnatvenAN^gIkR^itaM pratyakShaM teneti yAvat.h | mokSho hi nAma paramAnandAvAptivishiShyAtyantikI duHkhanivR^ittiH | tadabhAvashchaivamavagantavyaH | nAsti ko.api puruShaH paramAnandAnubhavI sarvo.api duHkhI cheti | nacha puruShAntaravartinI sukhaduHkhe tadabhAvau vA puruShAntarapratyakShaviShayAviti kathaM mokShAbhAvaH pratyakSheNAvasIyeteti hishabdArthaH |
mA bhUtpramANAbhAvena mokShAbhAvanishchayaH | tatsadbhAvanishchayo.atrapa durghaTa eva | pramANAbhAvAt.h | tAvattatra pratyakShaM pramANam.h | parapuruShavartinoH paramAnandaduHkhAbhAvayoH parapratyakShasya sAmarthyAbhAvAt.h | svaniShThastu tadabhAva eva pratyakSheNokShyate | nApi pratyakShAdanyat.h | tatprAmANyasiddheH | tatashcha sAdhakabAdhakapramANAbhAvAdapratipattirnityasaMshayo vA mokShe syAditi nopAsanAnuShThAnaM sambhavatIti | maivam.h | pratyakSheNa tAvanmokShanishchayopapatteH | 
nanUktamatra pratyakShasya tatra sAmarthyaM nAstIti tatrAha- ghaTata iti ||
yadyapi prAkR^itAnAM pratyakShaM na mokShaM gocharayituM kShamate | tathA.api mahattamapuruShapratyakSheNa mokShanishchayo yujyata eva | tadIyapratyakShAvagamashcha pareShAM tadvAkyena bhaviShyatIti bhAvaH | nanu kartR^ikarmaNoH kR^itItyatra ShaShThayA bhavitavyaM kathaM tR^itIyA | sheShavivakShAyAM ShaShThI vihitA | nachAtra sheShavivakSheti chenna | asminyoge sheShagrahaNasya nivR^ittatvAt.h | uchyate | hetAveShA tR^itIyA | na kartari karaNe vA | mahIyasA puruSheNa hetunA karaNena vA tadIyapratyakSheNeti yAvat.h | itareShAM muktidR^iShyirmuktisadbhAvanishchayo ghaTata iti | yadvA muktiviShayA pratyakShadR^iShyirghaTate | katham.h | yato mahIyasA puruSheNaShakShyate mokSha iti vadAma iti yojanA | athavA kriyamANeti padAdhyAhAre na doShaH |
evaM tarhi mayA.api vaktuM shakyata eva | yadyapi parapuruShavartI mokShAbhAvo.asmadAdInAM na pratyakShaH | tathA.api mahIyasaH puruShasya lokAyatAchAryasya pratyakSha eva | tadavagamashchAsmAkaM tadvAkyena bhaviShyatIti | tathAcha satpratipakShatayA punaranishchaya evetyata Aha- netIti ||
kasminnapi puruShe vartamAno.anAgato vA mokSho nAstyevetyahaM pratyakSheNekSha iti vaktustviti sambandhaH | mahattvameva na vidyate kuto mahIyastvamityevashabdArtho vA tushabdaH | mahattvamiha bahuprakAramapekShitam.h | itarapuruShApratyakShArthasAkShAtkAritvaM tadupayuktAsAdhAraNadharmavattvaM yathArthavAditvaM cheti | tatraikaprakAramapi na lokAyatAchAryasya vidyate | kutastena satpratipakShatAshaN^kA mokShavAdinAM mahApuruShANAm.h | 
kuta ityata Aha- sAdhayanniti ||
dharmAdyabhAvapratipAdanena sarveShAM puMsAM samAnatvaM sAdhayaMllokAyatAchAryaH kathamevetarebhyo.atishayavAnbhavati | na kathaJNchit.h | etaduktaM bhavati | puruShAntarApratyakShasya parapuruShagatasya mokShAbhAvasya sAkShAtkaraNe lokAyatAchAryasyetarebhyo visheSheNa bhAvyam.h | anyathetareShAmapi tatprasaN^gAt.h | na chAsAvasti | tapasA yogena vA janito dharmavisheShastathA | sa chetareShAmiva svAtmano.api nAstIti tenaiva sAdhitam.h | ataH kAraNAbhAvAditaravattasyApi parapuruShavartimokShAbhAvasAkShAtkaraNaM nAstyeveti nishchIyate | tata evAhaM mokShAbhAvaM sAkShAtkaromIti tadIyavachanamayathArthameva | bhUtapariNAmavisheSha evAtishayo.astviti chet.h | sa kiM pratyakSho.apratyakSho vA | nAdyaH | anupalambhAt.h | yAdR^ishatAdR^ishasya prakR^itaphalahetutve mAnAbhAvAt.h | anyathA.atiprasakteH | na dvitIyaH | atIndriyArthaM nirAkurvatA tenaivetaravadAtmanyapi tadabhAvasya sAdhitatvAditi |
yathA yuShmAbhirabhidhIyate nAstyeva mokShAbhAvasAkShAtkArI mahApuruSha iti tathA ahamapi vadAmi | nAstyevAsau mahIyAnpuruSho yaH pratyakSheNa mokShamIkSheta | pramANAbhAvAditi | tathAcha punaranishchaya evetyata Aha- dR^ishyanta iti || 
na kevalameka iti bhAvaH | loke.asminneva bhUmaNDale | te cha vasiShThAdayaH | teShAM mahIyastvamAha- j~nAnavij~nAnapAraj~nA iti || 
atra viShayibhyAM viShayAvupalakShyete | sAmAnyavisheShAkArapAraj~nAH | na kevalaM vartamAnAsheShavidaH kinnAma parAvaravido.api | tatkimanumAnAdinA netyAha- aparokShadR^ishashcheti || asmadAdibhyaH ko visheShasteShAmityata uktaM yoganiShThAshchAmalachakShuSha iti | yoganiShThAjanitavishiShyAdR^iShyena divyadR^iShyayaH | kintenaiva netyAha- pratyakShamiti || yogasAmarthyena paradevatAM sAkShAdupalabhya tanprasAdAsAditaprakAshAdyaishvaryavantaH | vasiShThAdayo yogardhisampannayA divyayA dR^iShyayA paramapuruShavartinaM mokShaM sAkShAtkuvarANAH pratyakSheNaiva dR^ishyante.ato na mokShAnishchaya iti | asmadAdibhiranupalabdhatvAtte na santItyata Aha- niShiddhayanta iti ||
nR^ibhirityanena mandabhAgyaiH parimitA viviktadeshaparichayavadbhiriti sUchayati | nahi te vaNigvIthyAM vartante | yena yuShmAbhirupalabhyeran.h | ato viprakarShAdanupalabhyamAnA na niSheddhuM shakyanta iti bhAvaH | 
nanu puruShasvarUpamAtre na vipratipattiH | teShAM mahIyastvaM tu kuta ityata Aha- dR^ishyate cheti ||
na kevalaM puruShAH kintu teShAmatimAhAtmyaM mahIyastvaM cha dR^ishyate | katham.h | atimahaujasAm.h | etaduktaM bhavati | dR^ishyante tAvadvindhyasthaganasamudrapAnAdIni teShAmatimahAntyojAMsi | tAni cha mahaishvaryakAyarANi | nacha kAryANi vinA kAraNairbhavitumarhanti | mahaishvayareShu cha sArvaj~nAparanAmakaM prAkAshyamiti teShAM mahIyastvasiddhiriti |
nanu tadIyaM mokShaviShayaM pratyakShaM pareShAM kutaH siddham.h | tadvAkyAditi chenna | teShAM vipralambhakatvopapatterityata Aha- yadIti ||
vipralambho hi prayojanamUlo bhavati | nacha teShAM prayojanAnusandhAnaM sambhavati | AptasamastaishvayartvAt.h | prayojanAntarasya chApramitatvAt.h | evaMbhUtA api te yogino yadi vipralambhakA iti niShiddhayante | tadIyaM vAkyaM vipralambhamUlatvena nirAkriyata iti yAvat.h | tadA te tvadabhyupagatA lokAyatAchAryoktiH kiM tathaiva na niShidhyate | sA.api vipralambhamUleti kalpayitvA.anAdaraNIyA syAt.h | avisheShAditi yAvat.h | 
etenaitadapi nirastam.h | viprakaSharvashAdasmAbhiranupalabhyamAnA api yoginastanmAhAtmyaM tadIyaM svapratyakShaviShayaM vAkyaM chAsmAbhiH kuto.avagantavyam.h | itihAsapurANebhya iti chenna | teShAmapramANatvAditi | doShadarshanena hi teShAmaprAmANyaM kalpyam.h | nacha tatra pramANamasti | vAkyatvenaiva prAmANyapratiShedhe lokAyatAchAryokterapi tatpratiShedhaprasaN^gAditi |
na lokAyatAchAryoktirvipralambhashaN^kayA nirAkriyate | pratyakShasaMvAdena prAmANyanishchayAditi chetsamaM prakR^ite.apItyAha- yadukteti || 
yairyogibhiruktAnAM vAkyAnAM prAmANyaM pratyakSheNa pratyakShasaMvAdenopalabhyante te.apIti pUrveNAnvayaH | kathamityata Aha- varAdayo.apIti ||
tairyogibhirdattA varAH shApAshcha sadA.avyabhichAreNa satyA bhavanti | hi yasmAttasmAditi pUrveNaiva sambandhaH | te prasannAH santastavedaM bhadraM bhaviShyatIti vA kupitAH santastavedamabhadraM bhaviShyatIti vA yadAhustattathaiva bhavatpratyakSheNopalabhyata iti |
syAdetat.h | pratyakShayogyArthe bhavatu tatsaMvAdena tadIyaM vAkyaM pramANam.h | atIndriye tu mokShAdau kathamiti | evaM tarhi lokAyatAchAryavachanamapi pratyakShayogyAthare tatsaMvAdena pramANamastu | atIndriye tu mokShAbhAvAdau kathamiti samAnam.h |
atha manyase pratyakShayogyArthe tAvattadIyaM vachanaM pratyakShasaMvAdyevopalabdham.h | tenAtIndriyArthaviShaye.api tatra vishvasimaH | loke tathopalambhAditi | tadidaM prakR^ite.api samAnam.h | tadidamuktamanuktasamuchchayArthenApipadena | 
evaM satpratipakShatAnirAsAya yoginAM mokShapratyakShavAdasya prAmANyam.h, aprAmANyaM cha lokAyatAchAryasya mokShAbhAvapratyakShokterupapAditam.h | hetvantareNApi tadaprAmANyamupapAdayati- aprAmANyamiti ||
hetusamuchchaye chashabdaH | vR^ithAvAcheti bhAvapradhAno nirdeshaH | vR^ithAtvAdityevokte tR^iNAdidarshane vyabhichAraH syAt.h | tadarthaM vAggrahaNam.h | kathaM lokAyatAchAryoktervR^ithAtvamityata Aha- na hIti ||
paralokasya mokShAdernivAraNAt.h nAstitvapratipAdanAllabhyaM kiJNchitprayojanaM nAstItyetatprasiddhameva | tathAhi | tadukteradR^iShyaM vA prayojanaM syAd.hdR^iShyaM vA | na tAvadadR^iShyam.h | paralokanivAraNAt.h | adR^iShyaM hi svargAdAvupabhogyaM vA syAddehAntareNehaiva vA | nAdyaH | svargAdeH paralokasya pareNa pratiShiddhatvAt.h | na dvitIyaH | dehAtmavAdinA.asyAtmanaH paralokasya dehAntarasya nivAraNAt.h | nApi dR^iShyam.h | pratipAdakapratipAdyayorarthakAmalAbhAnupalambhAditi | 
vaidikAnAM dharmAdharmavyavasthApakairvavachanairuparuddhakAmabhogAnAM prANinAM dharmAdyabhAvApratipAdanena kAmopabhogoparodhanivR^ittirUpaparopakArastAvadAchAryasya prANinAM dharmAdyabhAvapratipAdanena kAmopabhogoparodhanivR^ittirUpaparopakArastAvadAchAryasya prayojanamasti | yadyapyupakAro na svarUpeNa prayojanam.h | 
nApyadR^iShyahetutvena | tathA.apyupakartAraM pratyupakurvantyeva | vineyAnAM cha kAmopabhogoparodhanivR^ittirevAsti prayojanam.h | tatkathaM vR^ithAtvamityata Aha- vR^ithA vAchamiti ||
atra vR^ithAvAchamiti sAdhyanirdeshaH | evamapi vR^ithAvAktvaM na parihAryamiti | adR^iShyaprayojanarahitavAchamiti vA | yadi kashchittamAchAryaM vineyaM vA vR^ithaiva hanyAttadA taM prati tasya kimuttaram.h | na kiJNchit.h | 
etaduktaM bhavati | na sta eva dharmAdharmau, atastvayA niraN^kushena kAmopabhogaH karaNIya ityAchAryeNa bodhito.antevAsI tadIyakamanIyakAntAdyapahArArthaM taM hanyAdeva, tadA.asya kA pratikriyA | upakarturapakAro mahApratyavAyaheturiti ChAndasoktestenaiva tyAjitatvAt.h | upakartAraM pratyupakurvantItyetadapi dharmAdivAsanAyAM satyAmeva | sA tu tenaiva nishsheShitA | ato nAstyevAchAryasya prayojanam.h | pratyuta svajIvanahAnilakShaNo.anartha eva evaM vineyAnAmapyanyonyadhanavanitAdyapahArAyaparasparavadhAdAveva pravR^ittiH na tu kAmopabhogAvasaraH | mahatA.anarthenAkrAnto.alpIyAnkAmopabhogo.anartha eveti |
astvevaM lokAyatAchAryoktervR^ithAtvamanarthahetutvaM cha | tathA.apyaprAmANyaM kuta ityata Aha- sveti ||
svashabdaH pareShAmapyupalakShakaH | vyarthaM cheti sheShaH | vyarthAnarthahetuvAktvena lokAyatAchAryasyAprekShAvattvamanumIyate | tatastadvachanasyAprAmANyamiti sheShaH | uktashchAyamarthaH prayojanAdhikaraNe | 
uktamarthaM buddhayArohAya saN^kShipyAha- prAmANyaM iti ||
(atra) prAmANyashabdenAptatvamuchyate | kimityAkShepe | apishabdo garhAyAm.h | svetyupalakShaNam.h | dR^iShyasya darshanayogyasyApi bahorarthasya | chashabdo visheShaNasamuchchaye | devoktItyatIndriyAntarasyApyupalakShaNam.h | svoktaM sarvaM pratyakShasaMvAdena lokAnubhavaM lokAshvAsaM prApayan.h | 
yaH svajIvanaviruddhoktitvAdivisheShaNo lokAyatAchAryo yashchAtIndriyadevoktishrotR^itvAdivisheShaNo yogI tayorapi puruShayoH prAmANye saMshayaH syAtkiM, na syAdeva | kintvAdyasyAprAmANyameva dvitIyasya prAmANyameva nishchIyata iti yojanA | 
evaM nimittAbhAvenAsambhAvitAtIndriyaj~nAnasya kAmukatvAdinA sambhAvitavipralambhasya lokAyatAchAryasya yogardhisampadA sambhAvitasArvaj~nAvAptasamastaishvaryavattvAdinA.atyantAsambhAvitavaJNchakatvAtpratyakShasaMvAdivachaso yoginaH prati, pratipakShatvAsambhave (na) tadvachanAvagatena tatpratyakSheNa mokShaH siddhayatItyuktam.h | idAnIM vedenApi taM siShAdhayiShustatprAmANye vipratipannaM prati kiM saMvAdarahitatvAdvedasyAprAmANyamuchyate | uta vAkyatvAdunmattavAkyavat.h | athavonmattavAkyAdanishchitavisheShatvAdatha(vA) bAdhitatvaditi vikalpyAdye.api kiM sarvasya saMvAdo nAsti utaikadeshasyeti vikalpyAdyaM nirAchaShye- ata iti ||
vaidikAnuShThAnavatAM tatphalasiddherdR^iShyatvAdityarthaH | pratyakShagamyatvAt.h pratyakShasaMvAdena siddhatvAt.h | pramANasamuchchaye chashabdaH | vedena cha mokShasiddhiriti | anena sarvasyApi vedasya pramANAntarasaMvAdo nAstItyetadasiddham.h | aishvaryAdisAdhanatayA yogAdikamupadishato vedabhAgasya saMvAdadarshanAdityuktaM bhavati | mokShapratipAdakAni cha vedavAkyAni tatra tatrodAhR^itAnyeva draShyavyAni | phalavisaMvAdo.api vedasya dR^ishyata iti chenna | tasya kartR^ikarmAdivaiguNyahetutAyAH prAguktatvAt.h | tadidamuktaM sphuTamiti | Adye dvitIyaM dUShayati- yadIti ||
yadi bhAgavisheShasya saMvAdAbhAvena kR^itsnasyApi Agamasya no mAnatvam.h apramANatvamityuchyate tarhi akShajasya pratyakShamAtrasya tathA apramANatvaM bhavet.h | asthAtsukhAdiviShayasya pratyakShasya saMvAdAbhAvAt.h | yadi cha saMvAdarahitasyaiva vedabhAgasya no mAnatvamityuchyate tadA.asmatsukhAdiviShayasya pratyakShasyAprAmANyaM bhavedeveti | yadyapi yogipratyakShasaMvA(do.asti tathA)daH prAguktastathA.api taditarapramANApekShayedamuditaM veditavyam.h | syAdetat.h | pratyakShaM svata eva pramANaM tatra kiM saMvAdenetyata Aha- yadyakShajasyeti ||
yadi saMvAdena vinA.akShajasya svata eva pramANatvaM syAttarhi Agamasya tat.h svata eva prAmANyaM kathaM na bhavet.h- avisheShAdbhavedeva | 
dvitIyaM nirAkaroti- yadyAgamasyeti | yadi vAkyatvamAtreNonmattavAkyavadAgamasya na mAnatvamityuchyate | tarhyakShajatvena shuktirajatAdiviShayAkShajavatstatstambhAdyakShajasyApyaprAmANyaM syAdavisheShAt.h | nirdoShatvAtstambhAdiviShayamakShajaM pramANamityata Aha- yadyakShajasyeti || yadi nirdoShatvAtstambhAdiviShayasyAkShajasya pramANatvaM syAttarhyAgamasyApi tata eva kathaM na bhavet.h | na hyapauruSheyasya sadoShatA sambhavati | veda ityupakramAttathaiva vaktavye yadAgamasyeti vadati tadanenaiva nyAyena pauruSheyAgamasyApi 
prAmANyaM sAdhanIyamiti sUchayitum.h | 
tR^itIyaM nirAkaroti- loketi ||
unmattAdivAkyAt.h | visheSho vedasya | avyabhichAreNa bAdharAhityena | nahi vaidiko.arthaH pratyakShasiddho yena tattatra bAdhakatayA.avakAshaM labheta | 
etena chaturtho.api nirastaH |
tadevaM pratyakShAgamAbhyAM mokShaM sAdhayatehAmutra phalabhogavairAgyavatAM yoginAM pravR^ittiH saphalA prekShAvatpravR^ittitvAtsammatavadityanumAnamapi sUchitam.h | anumAnaprAmANyaM cha prAgeva samarthitam.h | 
apare purananumimate | duHkhasantatiratyantamuchChidyate santatitvAddIpajvAlAsantativaditi | tadasat.h | sakalajIvagataduHkhasantatipakShIkAreM.ashe bAdhitatvAt.h | nityasaMsAriNAM keShAJNchitsattvasya tairapyaN^gIkR^itatvAtsamarthayiShyamANatvAchcha | tadvayatiriktajIvagataduHkhasantatipakShIkAre tu tatraiva vyabhichArAt.h | pArthivaparamANurUpAdisantAne vyabhichArAchcha | sarvamuktipakShe phalamUlayorabhAvena so.apyatyantamuchChidyata eveti chenna | sarvamuktipakShasyaiva nirAkariShyamANatvAt.h | kAlakShaNasantAne vyabhichArAchcha |

kR^itavyAkhyAnametat.h |

syAdetat.h | nAtmaj~nAnaM devadatto gAmiva mokShaM dadAti | kintu prakAsho.andhakAramiva virodhAd.h duHkhaM nivartayati | tatra kimachaitanyaM kariShyati | svAtmaj~nAnameva cha svaduHkhavirodhi nAtmaj~nAnamAtramiti dvitIyaheturapyaprayojaka ityAshaN^kayAha- yadIti ||
kathaJNchana duHkhAtmaj~nAnayovirruddhatvena | tarhi j~nAnAduttarakAlaM dehavAnapi sadA nirantaramaduHkhI kinna syAt.h, syAdeva | etaduktaM bhavati | prakAshaH khalvandhakAravirodhitvAttannivartayan.h utpattyanantarameva nivartayati na tu vilambena | vilambe 
virodhasyaivAnirvAhAt.h | tathA.atmatattvaj~nAnaM yadi duHkhAdyanarthavirodhitvAttannivartyAtmAnaM muktaM kuryAt.h | tarhi jinAdayastattvaj~nAnasampannA j~nAnotpattyanantarameva muktAH syuH | na chaivam.h | dehAdimattvenopalambhAt.h | tathAvidhAnAM cha duHkhAderavarjanAditi | iShyApattinirAsAya sadetyAdyuktam.h | ayamatra prayogaH | duHkhAdikamAtmatattvaj~nAnavirodhi na bhavati bahulaM kAlaM tena saha sthitatvAtsammatavaditi | kiJNchAtmatattvaj~nAnaM na tAvadAmokShAdekam.h | j~nAnAnAM kShaNikatvadarshanAt.h | tathAcha yadanantaraM mokSho.abhilaShyate tajjinasya charamaj~nAnaM na mokShasAdhanamAtmaj~nAnatvAtprathamAdij~nAnavat.h | anyathA prathamameva mokShaM sAdhayedavisheShAditi |
nanu bhavadbhirIshvaraj~nAnaM mokShasAdhanamabhyupeyate | tatrApi samAnamidaM dUShaNamityata Aha- Isheti ||
IshavAdino mama mate tadichChAvisheShAnusAreNa kAlAtkaJNchana kAlamativAhya muktiH syAt.h | ayamabhisandhiH | na vayamIshvaraj~nAnaM mokShasAdhanamAchakShmahe | kinnAma prasannaH parameshvara eva | j~nAnaM tu prasAdasAdhanatvAnmokShasAdhanamiti gIyate | sa cha chetanaH kAmapi kAlakalpanAM karoti | asminsamaye.amuM muktaM kariShyAmIti | tatkalpanAnusAreNa bhavatyevAsau mukta iti na kashchiddoShaH | yathA brAhmaNasya vidyAcharaNAdinA prasanno.api prabhushchetasA kalpayati | AgAmini sUryoparAge.asmai gAM dAsyAmIti | sa brAhmaNasya vidyAcharaNAdinA prasanno.api prabhushchetasA kalpayati | AgAmini sUryoparAge.asmai gAM dAsyAmIti | sa tadanusAreNa tasmAdgAM labhate tathaiveti |
evamAtmaj~nAnasya mokShasAdhanatvaM nirAkR^itya dharmasyApi taM nirAchaShye- karmeti ||
karmaNA hetutvaM karmahetutvaM mokShaM prati | yadvA karmahetutvamiti bahuvrIhiH | mokShasyeti sheShaH | tushabdo.avadhAraNe | naiveti sambandhaH | nishchaitanyAtkarmaNaH | vimataM karma na mokShasAdhanaM bhavati achetanatvAtpaTavadityarthaH | vyAptimupapAdayati- nahIti || netyubhayatra sambaddhayate | nahi kvachidachetane mokShasAdhanatvamAvayoH sammatam.h | yenAtra vyAptirna syAdityarthaH | 
nanvachetanatve.api vishiShyaM karmedaM mokShasAdhanaM kinna syAditi chet.h | kimAmokShaprApteH kriyamANamekameva karmotAnekAni | nAdyaH | kriyANAmanekatvadarshanAt.h | pratikriyaM karmotpatteH | ekatve cha jAtasyaiva janma vA kriyANAM vaiyarthyaM vA viramyavyApAro vA.a.apadyeta | abhyupagamyaikatvaM bAdhakamAha- asheSheti ||
yathedAnIM prathamakriyottarakAlaM jAtaM karmAsheShaduHkhavilaye mokShasya kAraNaM na bhavati | tathottarakAlaM vivakShitakAle.api mokShakAraNaM na syAt.h | karmatvAditi sheShaH | ekasyApi karmaNaH kAlabhedena bhedAtpakShasapakShatvaM yujyate | vipakShe tUtpattyanantarameva mokShaM sAdhayedavisheShAditi | 
dvitIye.api bAdhakaM pramANamAha- asheSheti || atredAnImitIdAnIntanI karmavyaktiruchyate | uttaramityantimA | anyatsamAnam.h | nachAntimakarmavyatiriktAnAM karmaNAM mokShasAdhanatvamasti | tathA sati tadanantarameva mokShaprasaN^gAt.h | nacha pUrvasahakR^isyAntimasya karmaNo mokShasAdhanatvaM vAchyam.h | iyattAbhAvenAniyatakAraNakatvApatteH | nahi j~nAnodayAnantaramiyataiva kAleneyantyeva karmANi kR^itvA.apavrajyata iti niyamaH pramANavAn.h | nacha jainairiShyate | jinAnAM viShamakAlatvAbhyupagamAt.h | 
AbhAsoddhAraM karoti- dR^iShyIti ||
yasmAdiyaM dR^iShyipUrvA pramANagR^ihItavyAptyAdimatI | tato.anumA na tvAbhAsa ityarthaH | 
yaduktamIshaklR^iptyanusAreNeti tadasat.h | j~nAnAdIshvaraprasAdastato muktirityatra pramANAbhAvAditi chenna | shruteH sadbhAvAt.h | tatprAmANyasya sAdhitatvAt.h |
AbhAsAdanuddharanneva(vA) chAnumAnamapyAha- dR^iShyIti ||
shaktasyAnyasya vij~nAnaM vishiShyaj~nAnaM guNotkarShAdij~nAnamiti yAvat.h | tatprItijanakamiti yadyanumIyate | yadi cha tayA tatprItyaiva bandhahAniH syAdityanumIyate | tadA kinnAma dUShaNam.h | na kimapi | kutaH | yato dR^iShyipUrvA pramANagR^ihItavyAptyAdimatIyamanumetyarthaH | arthamAtramidamuktam.h |
eShA tu prayogaprakriyA | saMsArabandhahAniH samarthapuruShAntaraprItinibandhanA bandhahAnitvAt.h rAjaprasAdAdhInabhR^ityanigaDabandhahAnivat.h | yashchAsau puruShaH sa eveshvaraH | vipratipannA prItirguNotkarShAdij~nAnajA anijaprItitvAdrAjaprItivat.h | karmAdinA bhavannIshvaraprasAdo.api guNotkarShAdij~nAne satyeveti na doShaH | yadveshvaraviShayaM guNotkarShAdij~nAnatvAtsaMmatavat.h | nacheshvarasiddhayA doShaH | prathamAnumAnena tasya siddhatvAt.h | tadidamuktaM shaktasyAnyasyeti |
nanvetadviparItamapi mayA.anumIyate | tataH satpratipakShateti chet.h | kiM vimatA bandhahAniH svaj~nAnanibandhanetyanumIyate uta 
paraprasAdanibandhanA na bhavatIti | Adye doShamAha- svaj~nAnAditi ||
dR^ishyata ityetatkAkvA na dR^ishyata iti vyAkhyeyam.h | tathAcha vyAptyabhAva iti bhAvaH | dvitIye tu bandhahAnitvAde rAjaprasAdAdhInanigaDabandhahAnyAdau vyabhichAraH | paraprasAdanirapekShaiva kAchidbandhahAnirdR^ishyate | tatra bhavatAmapi vyabhichAra iti chenna | pakShatulyatvAt.h | sarvA.apyaniShyanivR^ittirIshvaraprasAdAdhIneti hi tattvavidAM panthAH |
yaduktaM dharmaj~nAnayormokShasAdhanatve tadaiva mokShaH syAditi tadasat.h | karmaNaH pratibandhakasya sadbhAvAt.h | nahi pratibandhakavashAtkAryamakuvarANo heturaheturbhavati | atiprasaN^gAt.h | anekavidhaM khalu kamar | tatra yadyapi j~nAnAvaraNA(NIyA)dikaM j~nAnAdeva nivR^ittam.h | tathA.apyAyurAdikAraNamastyeveti chet.h | syAdidaM pratibandhakasadbhAvakalpanaM yadi "ahiMsAdirUpo dharmaH, sharIraparimANatvAdinA.a.atmaj~nAnaM cha tattvaj~nAnam.h, ete cha dharmaj~nAne mokShasAdhane' ityeSho.arthaH pramito bhavet.h | nachaivam.h | evameva kalyane.atiprasaN^ga ityAshayavAndharmAdisvarUpe tAvatpramANaM nAstItyAha- ahiMsAyAshcheti ||
chashabdo j~nAnasaN^grahArthaH | yadvA saptaghaTikAbhojanAdisamuchchayArthaH | j~nAnavisheShasya chopalakShaNam.h | jinavAkyenAvagamyata iti chenna | tatprAmANyasAdhakAbhAvasyoktatvAt.h |
satpratipakShaM cha jinavAkyamityAha- hiMsAyA eveti ||
atrApi pUrvavadupalakShaNaM j~nAtavyam.h | jinavAkyAdahiMsAyA dharmatvaM pratipannasya bhinnakAchAryeNa hiMsAyA eva dharmatvamityakte kimuttaraM syAnna kimapi | tathAcha na dharmanishchayaH syAt.h | bhinnakAchAryo nApta iti chet.h | jino.api kathamAptaH | (sArvaj~nagu)sarvaguNopetatvAditi chet.h | bhinnakAchArye.api tulyametat.h | aprAmANikAstatra te guNA iti chet.h | jine.api kiM pramANasiddhAH | jinadarshinAM vachanena teShAM tatra siddhiriti chenna | samAnamanyatrApi | bhinnakAchAryadarshino bhrAntAH pratArakA veti chet.h | jinadarshino.api kuto na tatheti |
idAnIM dharmAdermokShasAdhanatvamapyaprAmANikamityAha- dharmasyeti ||
sukhaM mokShaH | jinavAkyenAvasIyata iti vadataH pUrvavatsatpratipakShatetyAha- hatyAyA iti ||
mokShahetutvaM kenachidAchAryeNoktamiti sheShaH | hanasta chetyatra supIti nAnuvartate | brahmahatyAdayastu ShaShThIsamAsAH | ato hatyeti sAdhuH | "santi khalvakShayaM ha vai chAturmAsyayAjinaH sukR^itaM bhavati' ityAdishrutimanusR^itya hiMsAtmakasya yAgasya mokShahetutvaM vadanta ityayuktameva jainAnAM mokShasAdhanamiti |
adhunA bauddhAbhimataM mokShasAdhanaM nirAkurvANaH shUnyavAdyuktaM tAvadapAkaroti- nacheti ||
shUnyameva tattvaM samastaM tatrAdhyastamiti parij~nAnam.h | tathaiva shUnyabhAvanayA shUnyadhyAnena | apichAvanyonyasamuchchaye | mokSho na bhavediti sambandhaH | kathaM cha netyanenedamAchaShye | shUnyaparij~nAnAdikaM mokShasAdhanamityatra pramANAbhAvAttatraiva bandhahAniH syAdityuktapramANavirodhAchcheti | yadvA shUnyaparij~nAnAdikaM kiM svayameva mokShaM sAdhayati kiMvA shUnyaprasAdajananena | nAdyaH | achetanatvAtpaTavat.h | na dvitIyaH | shUnyasya prasAdaguNAnaN^gIkArAt.h | anyathA shUnyatvavyAghAtAditi |
syAdetat.h | bandhastAvatsaMvR^ivinAmakAj~nAnanimitto.adhyAsaH | saMvR^itishcha virodhinA shUnyaj~nAnena nivartyate | tatastanmUlo bandhAdhyAso.apIti kimachetanatvAdikaM kariShyati | nacha evambhAvanAvaiyarthyam.h | asambhAvanAviparItabhAvanAnivR^ittyarthatvAditi | maivam.h | bandhasyAdhyastatAyA nirastatvAt.h | aN^gIkR^itya doShamAha- yadIti ||
shUnyaparij~nAnAdityAdikaM sarvamanuvartate | shUnyaj~nAnena kathaJNchaneti shaN^kitarItyA mokSho bhavediti yadyuchyate tarhi sa mokShaH kathamidAnIM j~nAnodayAnantarakShaNe na bhavet.h | tadaiva bhavitavyamityAshayaH | nahi pradIpasya virodhyandhakAranivartane vilambo.asti | aN^gIkriyante cha shUnyaj~nAnasamanantaramapi saMsarantaH puruShAH pareNa | asambhAvanAviparItabhAvanAsadbhAvAdvilamba iti chet.h | te kiM saMvR^itikArye na vA | dvitIye shUnyavadanivR^ittireva | Adye saMvR^itau nivR^ittAyAM kathaM tadanivR^ittiH | anyathA saMvR^ityanivR^ittirvA tadakAryatvametayorvA syAt.h | saMvR^iteranivR^ittau cha kathaM j~nAnavirodhitvam.h | pashchAdapi kathaM nivR^ittiH | 
nanu yathA bhavanmate j~nAnodayAnantaramapi saMsArAvasthAnaM tathA.asmanmate.api kiM na syAdityato vaiShamyamAha- pareti ||
anuShThitasvakR^ityasyApi tena paraprasAdanechChostu phalAvAptau vilambo nAma yujyate | loke tathA darshanAt.h | mokShasya puruShAntaraprasAdAdhInatA no chedAsthIyate kevalaM shUnyaj~nAnaM bandhavirodhitvAdbandhaM nivartayatItyaN^gIkriyate tadA j~nAnodayAnantaraM mokShasya vilambaH kiM nibandhano bhavet.h | pratibandhakatvena kalpyamAnasya saMvR^itikAyartvena j~nAnavirodhitvAt.h | nahi prabodhAnantaraM svApnabandhanivR^ittervilambo.asti |
paraprasAdAnapekSheShvapi kAryeShu vilambo.asti | trivR^inmUlAbhyavaharaNAdau kR^ite.api virechanAdevirlambadarshanAt.h | tatkathamuchyate pumichChAdhInatAbhAve vilambo na bhavediti | tatrAha- anyatrApIti ||
mokShAdanyatra | etAvatA kAlenedaM bhavatvitIshechChaiva nimittaM tataH | kuto.atreshvarechChAnimittaM kalpyata ityata Aha- anyatheti ||
IshvarechChAyA akalpane kAraNaM syAchchettrivR^inmUlAdanAdimAtraM virekAdeH kAraNaM yadi bhavettadA tasya sadbhAvAtkAryaM virekAdikaM kasmAnnopajAyate | upajAyetaiva | kAryAnudayenaiva sAmagrIvaikalyaM kalpyate | na(chAdR^iShyavai)cha dR^iShyasya vaikalyamatrAstIti parameshvarechChaiva kalpyA | nacha dharmavaikalyaM kalpayituM yuktam.h | uttarakAlamapi kAryAnudayaprasaN^gAt.h | nahi tanmadhye kashchiddharmo.anuShThIyate | vidyamAna eva prAgalabdhavR^ittirdharma iti chet.h | keyaM vR^ittirnAma | kiM kAryakAraNamuta sahakArisAhityam.h | nAdyaH | karaNameva kuto nAstIti vichAryamANatvAt.h | dvitIye tadeva sahakArIshvarechChaivochyate | auShadhasya sharIrAshayavyAptyabhAvAtkAryAnudaya iti chenna | tasyApIshvarechChAmantareNAnupapatteriti |
kiJNcha prAptasAdhanAbhimatAnAmapi mokShavilambe sAmagrIvaikalyaM vA pratibandhakasadbhAvo vA.anyairvAdibhiH kathaJNchichChakyate vaktum.h | natu bauddhenetyAshayavAnAha- kAraNe satIti ||
asya bauddhasya mate kAraNe sati kAryasyotpAdaH suniyato na tvanyeShAmivApratibaddhakAraNasAmagyrAM satyAm.h | samarthasya kShepAyogAditi tadvachanAditi hishabdArthaH | ataH shUnyavij~nAnAdikaM na mokShasAdhanamiti siddham.h |
vij~nAnavAdyuktaM mokShasAdhanaM dUShayati- vij~nAneti ||
dvitaiva dvaitam.h | svArthiko.aN.h | na dvaitamadvaitam.h | vij~nAnasyAdvaitaM vij~nAnAdvaitam.h | vij~nAnamekameva tattvaM na tato.anyadastIti vedanAt.h | vij~nAnabhAvanAt.h vij~nAnAdvaitadhyAnAt.h | Adyashchashabdo vAdisamuchchaye | dvitIyaH sAdhanasamuchchaye | evashabdo naiva ghaTata ityAdyaH sambaddhayate | dvitIyastu sAdhananiyamArthaH | vij~nAnavAdina iti tenai(tAbhyAM)va tAbhyAM sAdhanAbhyAM bhavatIti pratipAditaH | sAmarthyAdvij~nAnAdvaitavedanAdikaM vij~nAnavAdinoktaM mokShasAdhanaM naivopapadyata ityarthaH | yadvA vij~nAnavAdina iti tena pratipAditAdvij~nAnAdvaitavedanAdikAnmokSho naiva ghaTate naiva sampadyata iti yojanA | kuta ityataH pUrvoktaM savarM smArayituM kvachitkAle hyasau, natu j~nAnodayottarakAla eva bhavatItyuktam.h |
vaibhAShikasautrAntikAbhimataM mokShasAdhanaM parAchaShye- antariti ||
sharIrAntaHsthitasya j~nAnasya | upalakShaNametat.h | vij~nAnavedanAsaMj~nAsaMskArANAM bAhye sthitasya rUpasya cha yatkShaNikatvaM tasya vedanAt.h | uktamArgeNa kShaNikatvena | na muchyate puruShaH | kuto.atrArthe mAnAbhAvAt.h | akR^itAbhyAgamakR^itavipraNAshAdayo doShAH sphuTA eveti noktaH |
evaM vedabAhyamatAni nirAkR^itya vaidikAni nirAkurvANaH sAN^khayokteH mokShasAdhanaM tAvadanuvadati- prakR^iteriti ||
prakR^iterantaHkaraNAdirUpAyAH puruShasya svAtmanaH vivekaH svarUpato dharmatashcha bhedadarshanaM sAN^khayAH prAhuH | dUShayati- na cheti ||
etasmiMshchArthe mAnaM nAsti | kathaM nAsti | "ya enaM vetti puruShaM prakR^itiM cha guNaiH saha | sarvathA vartamAno.api na sa bhUyo.abhijAyate | kShetrakShetraj~nAyorevamantaraM j~nAnachakShuShA | bhUtaprakR^itimokShaM cha ye viduryAnti te param.h' ityAdyAgamAnAM sattvAdityata uktam.h- IshAprasAdata iti || 
IshaprasAdena vinA kevalaM prakR^itipuruShaviveko mokShasAdhanamityasminnathare mAnaM nAstItyarthaH | ayamabhisandhiH | bhavatyeva prakR^itipuruShaviveko mokShasAdhanam.h | kintu bhagavatprasAdasAdhanatvena | prakR^itipuruShaviveke hi puruShasya vairAgyaM sampadyate | viraktasya bhaktyAdidvArA bhagavatprasAda iti | tadarthAni chaitAni vAkyAni | nirIshvareNa tu sAN^khayena sAkShAnmokShasAdhanatvaM prakR^itipuruShavivekasyochyate | nacha tasminvisheShe pramANamastIti |
nanvetAni vAkyAni prakR^itipuruShavivekasya mokShasAdhanatvaM tAvatpratipAdayanti | nacha pAramparyakalpane kAraNamasti | ata eteShAmeva sAkShAtsAdhanatve prAmANyamityata Aha- shrutaya iti ||
yasya prasAdAdityAdyAH shrutayaH | aj~nAnAM j~nAnado viShNurityAdyAshcha smR^itayaH | evashabdasya na prAkR^itapuruShavAkyAnItyarthaH | yadA yasmAt.h | niyamAtmasAdhashrAntaravyavachChedena | nApareNa | sa evaika iti vachanAt.h | taM prasAdam.h | bhavenmuktiH | balavadbAdhakasadbhAvAt.h lAN^galena vayaM jIvAma itivat.h pAramparatvameva teShAM vAkyAnAM yuktamiti bhAvaH | 
vaisheShikAdyuktaM mokShasAdhanaM nirAkaroti- kaNAdeti ||
yogashabdena yogAnushAsanasya praNetA pataJNjalirupalakShyate | anupapannabhAShiNa iti sheShaH | na kevalaM sAN^khayAdyA ityaperarthaH | 
nanvete trayo.apIshvaraprasAdasAdhyAM muktiM bruvate | tathA hi vaisheShikeNa yadyapi dravyAdipadArthAnAM sAdharmyavaidhamyartattvaj~nAnaM niHshreyasaheturityuktam.h | tathA.api na sAkShAt.h | kintu dharmadvAraiva | anyathA yato.abhyudayaniHshreyasasiddhiH sa dharma iti sUtravirodhAt.h | nacha dharmo.api sAkShAnmokShahetuH | api tvIshvaraprasAdasahakR^ita eva | yathoktam.h | tachcheshvarachodanAbhivyaktAddharmAdeveti | spaShyaM cha "tuShyermochayato baddhAnatuShyerbadhnataH punaH | kArAgAramidaM vishvaM yasya vande tamIshvaram.h' iti |
akShapAdo yadyapi pramANAdiShoDashapadArthatattvaj~nAnAnniHshreyasAdhigama ityAha- tathA.api pramANAdipaJNchadashapadArthatattvaj~nAnasyAtmAdidvAdashavidhaprameyatattvaj~nAnahetutvameva | AtmasharIrendriyAtharbuddhimanaHpravR^ittidoShapretyabhAvaphaladukhApavargAstu prameyamiti tushabdakaraNAt.h | AtmAdij~nAnamapi na sAkShAnmokShasAdhanam.h | kinnAma parameshvaraprasAdopetameva | "svargApavargayormArgamAmananti manIShiNaH | yadupAstibhasAvatra paramAtmA nirUpyate' iti sampradAyavidvachanAt.h | 
atha kathamanupapannabhAShiNa ityata Aha- Ishasyeti ||
Isha(sya)prasAdato muktiM bruvANA apyete kiJNchidayuktamAhuryato.anupapannabhAShiNaityarthaH | 
tathAhi | yadyapi vaisheShikairIshvaraprasAdo.aN^gIkR^itastathA.api dharmasahakAritvenaiva | IshvarachodanAbhivyaktAditi vachanAt.h | evaM pataJNjalirapi tapaHsvAdhyAyAdisamAnakakShyatAmeveshvarapraNidhAnasyAha | naiyyAyikA apyAtmatattvaj~nAnameva mokShasAdhanamIshvaraprasAdastu sahakArimAtramityAsthitAH | dvitIyasUtre tathaiva vyutpAditatvAt.h | shrutismR^itayastu dharmAdikaM samastaM sAkShAtparamparayA vA bhagavatprasAdasAdhanam.h | bhagavatprasAdastvananyApekShaH sAkShAdeva mokShasAdhanamityAchakShate | "sarvaM tadantarAdhAya muktaye sAdhanaM bhavet.h | na kiJNchidantarAdhAya vimokShAyAparokShadR^ik.h' ityAdyAH | ataH kathaM nAnupapannavAdina iti | 
itashchAnupapannabhAShiNa ityAha- bhogAdeva cheti || Joshi-25
aisheShikAdayastattvavida iva j~nAnAtpUrveShAM karmaNAM j~nAnAdeva vinAshaM na manyante | kintu samAdhimahimnA.aparimitadehavyUhanirmANenAnantAnyapi viShamavipAkasamayAnyapi karmANi piNDIkR^itya tatphalasukhaduHkhabhogenaiva j~nAnino vinAshayantIti prAhurato.apyanupapannabhAShiNa ityarthaH |
nanvetadasaN^gatam.h | mokShasAdhanavichArasya prastutatvAditi | maivam.h | avidyAkAmakarmAdilakShaNo hi bandhaH | atastannivR^ittirmokSha iti kathaM kamarkShayo na mokShaH | vakShyati cha | karmakShayastathotkrAntirityAdi | ato mokShasAdhanaviShayaiveyaM chinteti |
tathAbruvANA api kathamanupapannabhAShiNa ityato.asyArthasyAprAmANikatvAdityAha- kutashcheti ||
j~nAnino.api karmaNAM phalabhogenaiva kShaya ityetatkuta eva pramANAtpratipattavyam.h | na kutashchit.h | akShINakarmaNAM mokShAnupapattestatkShayahetoshchAnyasyAbhAvAdatyantasukhaduHkhasaMj~nAnameva tatkShayakAraNamiti kalpyata ityata Aha- prasanna iti || kuta etaditi vartate | j~nAnena prasanno bhagavAnevAbhuktaphalAnyeva karmANi vinAshayatItyanyathaivopapatteH kuta etatkalpyata ityAshayaH | bhagavAnapi kathamadattaphalakarmakShayasyeShya iti na shaN^kanIyam.h | tadaishvaryasya kvApyapratihatatvAditi bhAvenoktaM jagadIshvara iti |
sambhAvitamevaitanna tu pramitam.h | tatkathamanyathaivopapattirityata Aha- bhidyata iti ||
hR^idayagranthiravidyA | parA apyavarA yasmAtsa parAvaraH | AtmanyAtataguNe jagadIshvare | AdyaM kaThashrutivachanam.h | dvitIyaM bhAgavatavachanam.h | Adipadena vakShyamANAnItihAsavachanAni gR^ihyante | anyathA phalabhogena vineshvaraprasAdenaiva karmaNAM gaterapagatervinAshanishchayAdanyathaivopapattiriti |
nanvatra parameshvare dR^iShye karmANi kShIyanta ityuchyate natu darshaneneti | to bhogeneti vyAkhyAne.api na virodha iti chenna | tathA sati hR^idayagranthibhedanasaMshayachChedanayorapyanyasAdhyatAsvIkArApAtAt.h | dR^iShya evetyevashabdavirodhAchcha | bhogena kShayasya sarvasAdhAraNyAddarshanavisheShaNasya vaiyarthyAchcha |
aj~no na sarvANi karmANi bhogena kSheptuM kShamate | bahutaratvAdviShamavipAkasamayatvAchcha | j~nAnI tu samAdhisAmarthyAtkAyavyUhaM nirmAya sarvANi samAhR^itya phalabhogena vinAshayatItyato visheShaNopapattiriti chetkuta eShA kalpanA | uktArthApattyaiveti chenna | asmadudAhR^itavachanAnAmanyathAvyAkhyAnasthitAvarthApattisthitiH | tatsthitau cha vachanAnAmanyathAvyAkhyAnasthitiriti 
parasparAshrayApatteH | vachanAnAmanyathAvyAkhyAnanirAse satyarthApattinirAsastannirAse (satyanya)nAnyathAvyAkhyAnanirAsa iti bhavatAmapi parasparAshrayApattiriti chenna | avadhAraNAdinA niravakAshasyoktatvAt.h | "bhinatti karmasaN^ghAtaM prasanno bhagavAnhariH' ityAdInAmatyantAnavakAshAnAmanyatrodAhR^itatvAchcha | ata eva "nAbhuktaM kShIyate karma kalpakoTishatairapi' ityAdisAmAnyavachanamaj~nAniviShayam.h | j~nAninAmapi prArabdhakarmaviShayam.h | "Atmano vai sharIrANi bahUni manujAdhipa | prApya yogabalaM kuryAttaishcha sarvAM mahIM charet.h | bhuJNjIta viShayankaishchitkaishchidugraM tapashcharet.h | saMharechcha punastAni sUryastejogaNAniva' ityAdikaM j~nAninAM prArabdhakarmaviShayam.h | visheShavachanabalena prArabdhakarmavinAshasya vakShyamANatvAt.h | 
ata eva "j~nAnAdevAsheShakamarkShaye tadaiva muktiH syAt.h | nachaivam.h | jIvanmuktAnAmupAlabdheH' ityanavakAshaM chodyam.h |
vimataM karma phalabhogavinAshyaM karmatvAtsampratipannakarmavadityanumAnaM tu kR^itaprAyashchittakarmaNyanaikAntikam.h | prAyashchittaM na karmakShayaheturityetaduttaratra nirAkariShyAmaH | akR^itaprAyashchittakarmatvaM heturiti chetkimidaM prAyashchittaM nAma | pApanivR^ittyarthatvena vihito vratavisheSha iti chet.h | tarhi mahAnubhAvAnAmanugrahAdinA vinaShye karmaNi vyabhichAraH | pApanivR^ittihetumAtraM prAyashchittaM vivakShitamiti chenna | tathA.api mahadavaj~nAdinA vinaShye puNye vyabhichAraH | kShayahetvantararahitakarmatvaM heturiti chet.h | tatkiM vidhireva hetutvaM gamayati | tathA sati samAdherapi kAyavyUhanirmANAdau hetutvaM na syAt.h | ArthavAdikaM phalamaviruddhaM svIkriyata iti chet.h | samaM prakR^ite.api | na hyatra kashchidvirodho.astItyuktam.h | alaukikatvaM tUbhayatrApi samAnam.h |
kiJNchAsminmate na kadA.api karmakShayaH | bhogakAle.api punaH karaNAt.h | na karotIti chAsambhAvitam.h | "nahi kashchitkShaNamapi' ityuktatvAt.h | kriyamANApi pravR^ittirnAdR^iShyajananIti chenna | shrutismR^itivirodhAt.h | j~nAninAM j~nAnasAmarthyAttathetyanyaviShayaM shrutyAdikam.h | "tadyathA puShkarapalAshe',"brahmANyAdhAya karmANi' ityAdishrutismR^itibalAditthaM kalpyata iti chet.h | prAktanakarmasvapyayaM prakAraH kuto nAbhyupagamyate | rAgadveShayorabhAvAnna pravR^ittiradR^iShyakAraNam.h | yathoktam.h | "na pravR^ittiH pratibandhAya hInakleshasya' iti | maivam.h | prAmAdikabrahmahananAdInAmadharmahetutvAbhAvaprasaN^ga ityalam.h |
pAshupatAdyuktaM mokShasAdhanaM nirAkaroti- nacheti ||
pAshupatashabdena chaturvidhA api gR^ihyante | Adipadena skAndasaurAdayaH | dvitIyenAdipadena skAndAdayaH | anugrahAnmokSho bhavatIti sheShaH | 
nanu cha pAshupatAdyukteti tAvannAnugrahasya visheShaNam.h | asAmarthyena samAsAnupapatteH | tathA sati pAshupatAdyuktAditi syAt.h | ata eva na mokShasya visheShaNam.h | tathA sati pAshupatAdyukta iti bhavet.h | shivAdivisheShaNatve tu vaiyarthyamiti |
uchyate | astu tAvadanugrahavisheShaNam.h | tatra shivAdInAmanugraha iti samAsa eva | ShaShThayA Akrosha iti ShaShThayA aluk.h | "j~nAtvA shivaM shAntimatyantameti' ityAdishrutivirodhaparihArashcha tatprayojanam.h | yaH saMsAradharmairIShadapyaspR^iShyaH paramashivastatprasAdAnmuktiriShyata eva | yastvaj~nAnAdyupetastathA pramitastadanugrahAnmokSho netyuchyata iti | "mokSho j~nAnaM cha kramasho muktigo bheda eva cha | uttareShAM prasAdena nIchAnAM nAnyathA bhavet.h' ityAdivAkyavirodhaparihArAya pAshupatAdyuktetyanugraho visheShitaH | aN^gIkriyata eva shivAdyanugraho bhagavatprasAdasAdhanabhUto mokShahetuH | natu pAshupatAdyuktaH svatantrasAdhanabhUta iti | yadvA pAshupatAdyuktetyapi bhinnaM padam.h | supAM sulugiti paJNchamyA luk.h | yadvA prathamAyA luk.h | mokShasya chedaM visheShaNam.h | tatra vAdinirdeshaprayojanaM vaktameva | yadvA.astu yathAshrutaM shivAdInAmeva | ye shivAdayaH pAshupatAdibhiH svAtanteNopAsyA uktAsteShAM (ya)tathopAsitAnAmanugraha eva nAsti pratyuta koSha eva | ato.anugrahAnmokSho dUranirasta iti bhAvaH | 
kutaH shivAdInAmanugrahAnmokSho netyata Aha- nAnya iti || 
tamevamiti shrutau sahasrashISharA puruSha iti prakatapuruShaj~nAnato.anyaniShedhenAmR^itatvamuktaM hi yasmAttasmAtpuruShottamAnugraha eva j~nAnenerito mokShaheturna shivAdyanugraha iti |

tataH kimityata Aha- sameti ||
samAdhikasyeti dvandvaikyavadbhAvaH | asau nArAyaNAnuvAkoktaH | upa samIpe chAro yasyAsau pradhAnasyopasarjanabhUta upachArapumAn.h pashupuruSho netyarthaH | nArAyaNanAmAdinA harirevAyamiti shiShyaireva j~nAtuM shakyata iti noktam.h |
adhipatirAhityasarvAdhikatvayostato.avagatasya samAdhikarAhityasya cha pashAvanupapatterna tadviShayo.ayaM puruShashabdaH | kintu nArAyaNAdinAmnA.abdhishayatvAdiliN^gena cha viShNuviShaya evetyastu | na tAvatA puruShashabdasya viShNau vAchakatvashaktiH siddhayati | prayogasyAmukhyayA vR^ittyA.apyupapatterityata Aha- sameti || asau viShNurupachAreNa puruShashabdaviShayo na bhavati kintu mukhyavR^ittyaiva | kutaH | mukhyAsambhave hyupachAraH kalpyate | puruShashabdasya mukhyArthaH pUrNatvam.h | tachcha viShNoreva samAdhikarAhityAdyujyata iti |
astvevaM puruShashabdasya viShNau vAchakatvashaktistathA.api puruShasUkte j~nApakAbhAvAttatparatvaM nAstIti dvitIyaM nirAkaroti- puruSha eveti ||
yadbhUtaM yachcha bhavyaM yachcha bhavadamuktaM vishvamidaM sarvaM puruSha eva | puruShAdhInameva | yata evamannenAnnamadanIyamamuktavargamatirohati atikrAmati | amuktAdhipatirita yAvat.h | tasmAdamR^itatvasyota bhAvabhavitrorabhedAnmuktavargasyApIshAnaH | saMsAre svAdhInaM jagadyadi muktau svAdhInatvaM jagadyadi muktau svAdhInatvaM jahyAttadA prekShAvAnna mochayet.h | ato muktAvapi tadadhInameveti sA shrutiH puruShasUktamantrastasya muktAmuktapareshatvamAha | tachcha muktAnAM paramA gatirityAdinA viShNorevAvagataM pashostvasambhAvitamevetyataH puruShasUktaM viShNuparameveti j~nAyate |

puruSha evedaM sarvamiti puruSheNaivedaM sarvaM vyAptamAtR^iNAdAkarIShAtsarvaM bhagavAniti mithyAdR^iShyireveti shAkhAntarabrAhmaNaM cha taM mantraM prati pravR^ittaM tasya mantrasya vyAkhyAnarUpamevAha atashcha na sarvatvamarthaH | vyAptaM vashIkR^itam.h |

dharmAnavaiShNavAnkAmyArthAMshcha | sharaNaprAptishcha "sarvottamatvavij~nAnapUrvam.h' ityAdinA.anyatra bhagavatpAdaireva vyAkhyAtA | tataH prasanno.aham.h | mA shuchaH | na shochiShyasi mukto bhaviShyasi | Adipadena "gatasaN^gasya muktasya' ityAdeH saN^grahaH  bhagavadvAkyaishcheti sambandhaH | tadyatheti shruteruktArthaH bhagavadvAkyairavasIyata iti vA |
bhATTAnAM mokShasAdhanamanuvadati- nityeti ||
nityaM nAma yadakaraNe pratyavAyo, brAhmaNyAdikameva cha nimittamupAdAya vihitaM taduchyate | yathA sandhyAvandanAdi | naimittikaM nAma yadakaraNe pratyavAyaH pitR^imaraNAdyAgantukaM cha nimittamupAdAya vihitaM taduchyate | yathA pitR^ishrAddhAdi | anyatkAmyaM niShiddhaM cha | tatra yatkAraNe phalamakaraNe na pratyavAyaH | kAmAnanimittaM tatkAmyAt.h | yathA jyotiShyomAdi | pratiShiddhaM niShiddham.h | yathA brahmahatyAdi | upAttaM cha karma bhogena kShapayanniti chashabdArthaH | 
ayamAshayaH | sukhaduHkhatatkAraNarUpo hi saMsAraH | sa cha karmanimitta eva | nityanaimittikayorakaraNe tvadharmapravachayena duHkhatatsAdhanAvAptirasya bhavati | niShiddhakaraNe.api tathA | kAmyakaraNe tu dharmotpAdanena sukhatatsAdhanAvAptirjAyate | mumukShustu nityaM naimittikaM cha nityameva karoti | parityajati cha niShiddhamiti na duritopachaya; | kAmyamapi parityajatIti na dharmopachayaH | evamanAgatayordharmAdharmayoranutpAde prAgupAttau cha bhogena kShapayannirbIjAyAH saMsR^itermuchyata iti | yathoktam.h | "mokShArthI na pravarteta tatra kAmyaniShiddhayoH | nityanaimittike kuryAtpratyavAya javAMsayA' iti | nacha paJNchamI karmavidhA.asti | yatkaraNe.akaraNe vA dharmAdharmodayaH syAditi |
nirAkaroti- etadapIti ||
etena nAnyaH panthA iti shrautena bhagavajj~nAnavyatiriktamokShasAdhananiShedhena | api cha nityanaimittikakarmaNAM niyamena samyaganuShThAnaM tAvadashakyameva | "charanti devA vihitaM samastamardhameva munayo dashAMshato manuShyAH' ityAdishruteH | nApi niShiddhAkaraNaM sambhAvitam.h | prAmAdikAnAM mAnasavAchikakAyikAnAmaparihAryatvAt.h | prAyashchittAttatkShaya iti chenna | prAyashchittasyApi samyaganuShThAtumashakyatvAt.h | pUrvopArjitakarmaNAM bhogena kShayastvatyantAsambhAvita eva | anantatvAdityalam.h |

vidyaiva tu nirdhAraNAditi sUtreNa | svayameva na tvarthataH | "vAjasaneyino.adhIyate | ShaT.htriMshatsahasrANyapashyadAtmano.agnInarkAnmanomayAnmanashchitaH' ityAdi | tatra saMshayaH | kimete.agnayaH 
kriyAnupraveshinastachCheShabhUtA uta svatantrAH kevalavidyAtmakA iti | kriyAmayasyAgneH prakaraNAttadviShaya evAyamupadesha iti prApte.abhidhIyate | vidyAtmakA evaite.agnayo na kriyAsheShabhUtAH | te haite vidyAchita eveti nirdhAraNAt.h | iti pareShAM vyAkhyAnamasadeveti bhAvenoktamimamevArthamiti | viphalatvAdasyAshchintAyAH | pakShadvaye.apyabhyudaya eva hyasya prayojanam.h | yastu nityAnityavastuvivekavAJNChamadamAdisampannaH sarvabhogavairAgyopeto mumukShurathashabdenottaramImAMsAyAmadhikArI sUchitaH sa kathametAsu phalguchintAsu pravartata iti |
evaM sUtrakR^itA pUrvapakShitAni matAni nirAkR^ityedAnIM ye sUtrANAM vR^ittikArA anyathA bhAShante teShAM matAni nirAkurvANaH samuchchayaniyamavAdinAM mataM tAvadapAkaroti- vineti ||
saMsAranivR^ittimAtraM kevalena j~nAnena bhavati | AnandavR^iddhistu kamarsApekSheNaiva j~nAneneti bhagavataH panthAH | yadvakShyati sahakAritvena cheti | ato j~nAnakarmabhyAM mokSha ityanuktvA karma vinA kevalaj~nAnena na mokShaH kintu karmasahitenetyuktam.h | ityetadapi mataM saiva sUtragR^ihItaiva nAnyaH panthA iti shrutiH spaShyaM nivArayati | tamevaM viditveti j~nAnamAtrasya mokShasAdhanatvamuktvA punarnAnyaH panthA itrata vachanAdAdaro.avagamyate | nacha samuchchayaniyame kimapi pramANamasti | andhantamaH pravishantItyAdInAmanyArthatvAt.h | "yathA.annaM madhusaMyuktaM madhu chAnnena saMyutam.h | evaM tapashcha vidyA cha saMyukte bheShajaM mahad.h' ityAdInAM parokShaj~nAnaviShayatvAt.h | aparokShaj~nAnaviShayatve.apyAnandavR^iddhayarthatvAt.h | 
mAyAvAdino vadanti | dvividho mokShaH parAparabhedAt.h | tatrAparo vaikuNThasatyalokAdiprAptilakShaNaH | parastvavidyA.astamaye satyadvaitabrahmAvasthAnarUpaH | pratIkAdiviShayamanyathopAsanamaparasya sAdhanam.h | parasya tvekatvaj~nAnamiti | tatrAnyathopAsanasya vaikuNThAdiprAptisAdhanatvaM tAvadapAkaroti- anyatheti ||
evaM yathAsthitenaiva prakAreNa na tvanyatheti vadantI shrutiranyathopAsanamapi puruShArthasAdhanaM nivArayati | na kevalaM paramapuruShaj~nAnavyatiriktapakShAn.h | tamityanena yathArthaj~nAnaM labdhameva | saprakArasya prakR^itasya parAmarshopapattAvekadeshaviShayatvakalpanAnupapatteH | tathA.api yadevamiti vadati tadA.a.adarasUchanArthamiti | paramamokShaviShayeyaM shrutirastu | aparastu puruShArtho.anyathopAsanena bhaviShyatItyata Aha- neti ||
"na pratIke na hi saH' iti sUtrakAro.anyathopAsanasya sarvathA.apyakartavyatvaM vakShyati | ato na tatpuruShArthaleshahetuH | 
sUtrasyArthAntaraM vakShyAmIti vadantaM prati shrutivirodhamAha- andhamiti || puruShAtharsAdhanamiti sheShaH | shrutistvanyatra smR^itisammatipradarshanena vyAkhyAtA | 
idAnImekatvaj~nAnasya paramokShasAdhanatvaM nirAkaroti- nacheti ||
cho.avadhAraNe | ekatvavij~nAnAdapi puruShaH saMsArAnna muchyate | kutaH | uktanyAyena "tamevaM vidvAn.h' itrata sahasrashirastvAdimahAmahimopetasya bhagavato j~nAnamamR^itatvasAdhanamabhidhAya "nAnyaH panthAH' iti sAdhanAntarAbhAvasyoktatvAt.h | "puruSha evedaM sarvam.h' ityuktamekatvamevaMshabdena parAmR^ishyata iti chenna | uktanyAyena tasya vAkyasyaikatvaviShayatAyA abhAvAt.h | "tadyo yo devAnAM pratyabuddhayate' ityAdishrutayastu tadguNasAratvAdityuktanyAyena naikyaj~nAnasya mokShasAdhanatAM vadanti | 
kiJNchaikyaj~nAnamanyathAj~nAnamiti pR^ithagupadeshAdityuktanyAyena siddham.h | mithyAj~nAnaM chAnarthasAdhanamityuktam.h | 
api chAdvaitaj~nAnasya na tAvadyAgAdivadrAjasevAdivadvA mokShasAdhanatvam.h | kintu avidyAvirodhitvena | virodhinA.advaitasAkShAtkAreNAvidyAyAM nivR^ittAyAM tadupAdAnako bandhaH svayameva nivartata iti | tathAcha sAkShAtkR^itAdvaitAnAmuttarakShaNa eva dehAdidvaitadarshanAbhAvaH prApnoti | aN^gIkriyate cha jIvanmuktiH | j~nAnenAvidyAyAM nivR^ittAyAmapi tatsaMskAreNa dvaitadarshanAnuvR^ittirbhavatIti chenna | saMskArasyAvidyAkAryatve.avasthAnAnupapatteH | na hyupAdAne nivR^itte kAryamavasthitaM dR^iShyam.h | anyathA satyatvaprasaN^gaH | j~nAnodaye.apyanivR^ittasya tasya nivartakAntarAbhAvAtsarvadA(.anivR^i)nuvR^ittau na kadA.api dvaitadasharnanivR^ittiH syAt.h | asaN^gasyAtmano vinaivAvidyAsambandhena saMskArAshrayatvaM chAyuktameva | etena prArabdhakarmavashAd.h dvaitadarshanA(.anivR^i)nuvR^ittirityapi nirastam.h | j~nAnena nivR^ittA.apyavidyA dagdhapaTanyAyena kiJNchitkAlamavatiShThate | tena dvaitadarshanAnuvR^ittirghaTata iti chenna | AtyantikanivR^ittau kAraNAbhAvena dvaitadarshanAnuparamaprasaN^gAt.h | etena avidyAleshAvasthAnapakSho.api pratikShiptaH | leshashcha paTasya tanturivAvayavo vA syAtpradesho vA dharmo vA | nAdyaH | akAryatvAdavidyAyAH | na dvitIyaH | pradeshAnaN^gIkArAt.h | pradeshino nivR^ittau pradeshAvasthAnAsambhavAchcha | na tR^itIyaH | dhamiNo.apagame dharmAnapagamAnupapatteH | 
atha matam.h | saMsAramUlakAraNabhUtA.avidyA yadyapyekaiva | tathA.api tasyAH santyeva bahava AkArAH | tatraiko bandhasya paramArthasatyatvavibhramahetuH | dvitIyo.arthakriyAsamarthavastukalpakaH | tR^itIyastvaparokShyapratibhAsaviShayAkArakalpakaH | tatrAdvaitasya satyatvAdhyavasAyena samastadvaitasatyatvakalpaka AkAro nivartate | arthakriyAsamarthaprapaJNchopAdAnaM mAyAkArastattvasAkShAtkAreNa vilIyate | aparokShapratibhAsayogyArthAsajanakastu mAyAlesho jIvanmuktasya nivR^ittaH samAdhyavasthAyAM tirohito.anyadA dehAbhAsajanakAbhAsahetutayA.anuvartate | prArabdhakarmaphalopabhogAvasAne tu nivartata iti | tadayuktam.h | asyAH kalpanAyAH niShpramANakatvAt.h | indro mAyAbhiH pururUpa Iyata iti shrutiratra pramANamiti chenna | atra pArameshvarashaktipratipAdanAt.h | j~nAnabAdhyAnirvAchyamAyAkArapratipAdanApratibhAsanAt.h | "tasyAbhidhyAnAdyojanAttattvabhAvAd.h bhUyashchAnte vishvamAyAnivR^ittiriti shvetAshvataramantre.api bhUyobhUyastasminmanaso yojanAdyo jAyate tattvabhAvastattvaj~nAnaM tasmAduditAttasya parameshvarasyAbhidhyAnAdanugrahAtkarmakShayAnte vishvabandhakamAyAnivR^ittirbhavatItyuchyate na tvanirvAchyavidyAkArANAM krameNa nivR^ittirbAdhalakShaNA | kiJNcha yo.api mAyAkAro.anuvartata ityuchyate tattvaj~nAnaM tasya virodhi na vA | Adye kathaM na nivartate | dvitIye j~nAnena na nivarteta | tathAcha satyaH syAt.h | karmakShaye sati nivartata iti vadatA karmaNAM tatkAraNatvamuktaM syAt.h | anyathA tannivR^ittau nivR^itteranupapatteH |
atha manyase | j~nAnamevAvidyaleshasya nivartakam.h | kintu prabalena prArabdhakarmaNA pratibaddhaM na nivartayati | phalabhogena tu pratibandhake kShINe nivartayatIti | tadapyayuktam.h | nirupAdAnakarmAvasthAnAnupapatteH | sa evAvidyAleshaH karmopAdAnamiti chenna | karmAvasthAne.avidyAleshAvasthAnaM tadavasthAne cha karmAvasthAnamiti parasparAshrayatvApatteH | utpattyAdAvivAvasthAne.api tasya doShatvAt.h | 
kiJNchAsyArthasya na kiJNchitsphuTaM j~nApakAntaramasti | tato mA nAma bhUdavasthitAvitaretarAshrayatvam.h | j~naptau tu bhavatyeva | jIvanmuktyanyathA.anupapattyaivaiSho.arthaH kalpyata iti chenna | paramapuruShAnugraheNaiva mokSha ityasya sakalashrutItihAsapurANAdisiddhasyArthasyAN^gIkAreNaiva sarvasyopapattAvasyAH kalpanAyA anavakAshAditi |
adhikaraNArthamupasaMharati- iti sarvamiti ||

svayogyata ityuktam.h | tAmeva yogyatAM vivR^iNoti- brahmeti || 
brahmaiveti sambandhaH | sarvairvedoditaiH | chashabdaH kriyAdravyasamuchchayAtharH | harimupAsIteti vartate | vedoktasamastaguNakriyopetatayA.anantarUpaM harimupAsituM brahmaiva yogya ityarthaH | chastvarthaH | sarasvatI tu kriyAsAmAnyataH kriyAsaN^kochenopAste | sakalavedoktaguNopetatayA.anantarUpaM harimupAste | trivikramatvAdikriyAstu nityavikrAntyAdiShvantarbhAvayatItyarthaH | guNasAmAnyataH samastarUpANyupAste | guNAnkriyAMshcha saN^kochayatItyarthaH | pare shakrAdayaH | dravyANi rUpANi guNakriyAsaN^kochastu siddha eva |

kiM sarveShAM j~nAninAM prArabdhakarmaphalopamarda ekavidha evota nAnAvidha ityapekShAyAmAha- devAdInAmiti ||
yeShAmadhikaM j~nAnaM teShAmadhika ityAdi | etena "nAvisheShAt.h' iti madhye paThitasya sUtrasya pUrvatrottaratra chopayoga ityuktaM bhavati | 
prArabdhakarmaNAM bhogena vinA na kShayaH | kintu brahmaj~nAnena phalahrAso bhavatItyuktam.h | tatraike manyante | achintyo hi brahmaj~nAnasya mahimA | atastatsAmarthyAdaprArabdhAnIva prArabdhAnyapi karmANyabhuktaphalAni kShIyante | nAbhuktaM kShIyate kamaretyAdivAkyAni tvaj~nAniviShayANi | tatashcha j~nAnAgniH sarvakamarANIti sarvashabdo.ayapIDitaH syAditi | anye tu parameshvarechChopodbalitAni prArabdhAni bhojayantyeva sarvaM svaphalam.h | na kashchidapi phalahrAso.astIti | 
tatrAdyaM mataM tAvadapAkaroti- sarvAtmaneti ||
brahmadarshino.api prArabdhasya karmaNaH sarvAtmanA tvabhogo na syAdeva | vinA bhogena brahmaj~nAnAdeva prArabdhAnyapi karmANi kShIyanta iti matamanupapannamityarthaH | tathA sati brahmavidAM saMsArAvasthAnaM na syAt.h | nirbIjatvAt.h | lokAnugrahArthameva vigrahAMste bibhratIti chenna | shApAdinimittAnAmApAdAmapItihAsapurANeShu bahulamupalambhAt.h | tasya tAvadeva chiramityAdishrutyA chAvagamyate karmAvasthAnamiti hishabdArthaH | dvitIyaM matamapAkartumAha- phaleti ||
prArabdhasya kamarNa iti vartate | OMmityachchAryAntarimamAtmAnamabhipashyopamR^idya puNyaM cha pApaM cha kAmamAcharanto brahmAnuvrajanti' ityAgamAditi bhAvaH | yastvAgamaprArabdhaviShayaM vyAkhyAya prArabdhakarmaphalasyeShadapi hrAso nAstIti brUyAntaM pratyAha- sarvAtmaneti ||
IShadapItyarthaH | brahmahatyAdikarmavipAkakShayarogAdinivR^ittyarthAH prAyashchittavidhayo.atra kAmyavidhayo vivakShitAH | 
ayamatrottarakramaH | "brahmahA kShayarogI syAt.h' iti smaraNAtkShayAdikaM tAvadbrahmahatyAdeH phalam.h | tata utpAditakShayAdikaM brahmahatyAdiprArabdhameva | tasya cha prArabdhakarmaphalasya kShayAdeH prAyashchittakaraNe nivR^ittirdR^ishyate | tatkathaM prArabdhakarmakaphalasya sarvathA.apyanupamardaH | 
atha manyeta | prAyashchittaM na kShayanivR^ittihetuH kintu bhoganimittakarmakShaya eveti | tadA prAyashchittaviShayo vyarthAH syuH | gR^ihadAheShyayAdivatprAyashchittAnAM naimittikatvaM bhaviShyatIti chenna | kShayAdisaMyogena vidhIyamAnAnAmeShAM tadvighAtaphalasambhave phalAntarakalpanAnupapatteH | kiJNchAtra niyatapashchAdbhAvitvamasamAhitameva | tadidamuktaM kAmyeti | tathA.api brahmaj~nAnaM na tadarthaM vihitamiti chenna | phalashrayaNenaiva vidhikalpanAt.h |
anenaiva nyAyena prAyashchittAnAM kamarkShayahetutvAbhAvo.api nirastaH | tathA sati prAyashchittavidhInAM vaiyarthyApatteH | naimittikatvapakShasya cha dR^iShyAdR^iShyahAnopAdAnaprasaN^gena nirastatvAt.h | 
atha karmaNo dvayI shaktiH | ekA tAvatphalajananI aparA tvasaMvyavahAryatvahetuH | prAyashchittairdvitIyA.apAkriyata iti chet.h | evaM tarhi karmavipAkaprAyashchittAnAmapIyameva gatiriti kathaM nopamardaH | kiJNcha na sarvo rogaH sarvaM cha duritamasaMvyavahAryatAheturiti tatra prAyashchittavaiyarthyameva syAt.h | api cha kShayakuShThAdyupahato.api na prAyashchittAcharaNamAtreNa saMvyavahAryaH | kintu kShayAdyapagama eveti tatkAraNatvameva prAyashchittAnAmaN^gIkAryam.h | maraNAntikaprAyashchittAnAmAnarthakyaM cha syAt.h | shrAddhAdivyavahArasiddhayarthaM taditi chenna | parivrAjakAnAM tadabhAvApAtAdityalam.h | 
upasaMharati- ityukteti ||
itishabdastasmAdityarthe | prArabdhakarmaNAM bhogAdeva kShayastathA.api phalahrAso.api vidyata ityuktaniyamo bhavedupapanna iti sheShaH | Joshi-27
